RABB
Now. here is something VERY cool I want to draw your attention to. When this person was reflection on Allah and his creations. and reached various conclusions. WHAT word did he use to call upon his creator?. How did he address his creator the very first time? .  Let's look at the ayats again. He begins the process of his reflection.
إِنَّ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَٱخْتِلَفِ ٱلَّيْلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ
‏ٱلَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ ٱللَّهَ قِيَمًۭا وَقُعُودًۭا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِهِمْ وَيَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ
At this point he reaches the conclusion and finds purpose. and now he's about to communiate with his creator. Now look what he says.
رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا
The word he used. is Rabb. He did not say. اِلٰہُنا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا. Oh Ilah! you did not create this in vain. He did not say. خالقُنا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا.  Oh Creator! You did not create this in vain. NO!. He says. رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا. Oh my Rabb. you did not create this in vain. Why did he use the word Rabb?.  Of ALL the attributes he saw reflecting in the creation. he could have used ANY attribute. right?. جلیل. جمیل . کبیر . عظیم. علو.  Why did he choose Rabb?.

.
So now let's look at the meaning of the word Rabb. so we can REALLY appreciate his thought process.  Actually I wanna show you something from the jamaal of Quran. this symmetrical beauty of Quran. I was debating if I should share this or not because of time constraints. but I can't resist. I find this simply too amazing. I want to show you this symmetry between the words Allah and Rabb.

When we look at the very first Surah of the Quran. which is the fateha. we see that Allah is mentioned twice.  and then Rabb is mentioned once after that. We have بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم. Allah is mentioned here. and then after that we have.الحمد للہ. Allah is mentioned again. and THEN we find.  رب العلمین. So Allah is mentioned twice before the word Rabb is mentioned once. correct?. And after that. in the remaining ayaats. neither Allah nor Rabb is mentioned again. right?. So this is the begining of Quran.
Now if we go to the END of the Quran. to surah AlNaas. and if we work our way backwards what do we see?.  What's mentioned in Naas?. Allah or Rabb?. Rabb is mentioned. قل اعوذ برب الناس. You go to the surah before that. what is mentioned?. Allah or Rabb? .  قل اعوذ برب الفلق. Rabb is mentioned again. But now if you go the the surah before that. Surah Ikhlaas. what is mentioned? Allah or Rabb?.  قل ھو اللہ احد. Allah is mentioned.
From the beginning. Allah is mentioned twice. Rabb is mentioned once. .  From the end. Rabb is mentioned twice. Allah is mentioned once.  SubhanAllah!. And also in the last two surahs. you see the word Rabb used. but you see no mention of the name Allah!. And in Surah Ikhalas. You see only the name Allah mentioned. and you don't see the word Rabb mentioned at all. SubhanAllah!. Not bad for spoken text huh?

OK. Now let's understand this word Rabb. The word Rabb is commonly translated as LORD. I don't know what that word means. I don't know of any lord. except lord of the rings. Lord is not a good translation of the word Rabb to the arabi linguists. So let's first understand the meaning of the word Rabb in classical Arabic.  before we try to find a one word equivalent for it in English.

Rabb is an extremely powerful word that is used in numerous contexts. And just like other words we've studied. its a composite word. and it has several linguistic implications. If you remember when we studied Surah Naas. I told you that even though this word is used for Allah. it is not reserved for him. It can also be used for human beings. It can be used for parents. teachers. guaridans. remember?. So the first thing to know is that it is a wordthat is used in Classical Arabic for Allah.  as well as human beings. OK!.

Linguists define Rabb as.

الرَبُّ ھُوَ المَالِکُ وَ السَّیِّد وَ المُرَبِّی وَ المُرْشَدُ وَ المُنعِمُ وَ القَیِّمُ
Allah as Rabb is 6 things. Malik. Sayyed. Murabbee. Murshad. Munim. and Qayyim. 6 things. And he ALL these things. ALL at the same time. OK?. Now let's look at each of these meanings individually.



The first meaning is Al-Malik. which means. owner. OK?. Someone who has ownership is called Rabb. And the thing that he owns is called. Milk. Not the english milk that cows produce. In Arabic Milk means PROPERTY. OK?. That's why propery is called مِلکِیَّۃ. And the owner of that property is called. Maalik.
Now do we own things?. Do we own a phone? an iPad? a computer?. Yes. So that makes us Rabb too. Do teachers have some ownership over their students. Sure!. Do your parents have ownership over their children. Sure!. Despite the way you guys sometimes feel. It's MY life mom. It's MY LIFE dad. You can't tell me what to do. You don't own me!. Despite these beautiful sentiments that we sometimes have. whether we like it or not. whether we agree with it or not. our parents have ownership over us. YOUR parents have ownership over you. They DO actually own your life. Why?. Because this MY life that you talk about. You wouldn't have it. had THEY chosen to NOT have you. And regardless of how you feel. you OWE them a TON of gratitude for allowing you to have an existence. So in that sense. parents are also Rabb. because they have ownership.
But do parents have ULTIMATE and ABSOLUTE ownership?. NO. Because even though they gave birth to you. they did not CREATE you. Allah CREATED YOU. Allah created you and your parents. So ULTIMATE. and ABSOLUTE ownership belongs. ONLY to Allah. You understand?. So Allah as Rabb. is the absolute owner of his creation. He is Maalik. And if he is Maalik. what does that make us?. That makes us his property. It makes us his مِلکِیَّۃ.




The second meaning is the word Sayyed. and this goes along with the previous meaning of Maalik. Maalik means owner. Sayyed means someone who has authority. Sayed is the one who is incharge. You understand the difference?. Malik is someone who has ownership. Sayyed is the one who has authority.
Is it possible to own something. but then not have complete authority over it?. Sure. it's possible.  For example. I own a car. but do I still HAVE to get it registered.  Do I still HAVE to get it inspected every year.  Do I HAVE to drive within the speed limits. Do I HAVE to drive it on the road. Can I just drive it on the side walk if I want. NO. unless I'm in Pakistan. So even though I own my car. I do not have COMPLETE authority of it. You understand?
And this applies the other way too. I may have complete authority over something. I may be able to do whatever I want with it. but I may not have complete ownership of it. Like for example. the computer in my office. I can do whatever I want with the software that is installed. I can install new stuff. I can uninstall stuff. I can change existing stuff as I want. Nobody is going to stop me. But do I own THAT Computer?. NO? My company does. .  So I can own things but not have complete authority. I can have complete authority but not necessarily have ownership. understand?.
But Allah as Rabb. he has ABSOLUTE ownership. AND He has ABSOLUTE authority. Both at the same time. He he can do WHATever he wants. WHENever he wants with his property. If he wants to burn it he can burn it. If he wants to tear it apart.  he can tear it apart. If he wants to drown it. toss it. discard it. He can do so at his will. YOU and I don't get to question him about it. why?. Because HE has complete ownership. HE has complete authority. And even if we do complain. guess what?. He does not care. Makes not difference to him. If your parents are grounding you. they're taking your phone away. your xbox away. you can cry and complain as much as you want. you ain't gettin it back. Because they are maalik. you are milkiyyah. And if our crying and grumbling doesn't get us anyway with our parents. who are limited Rabb. It sure as hell won't work with the one who is the ABSOLUTE Rabb. We are creation. He is our creator. He is not the one on trial. We are.  The fact that he lets us understand the wisdom of his design. through the Quran. is HIS favor on us. He is NOT obligated to do ANYTHING for us. But he DOES it anyway. Because that is what the Rabb does.




The third meaning of the word is Murabbee. Now THIS is a VERY powerful word. Murabbee means someone who ensures growth. Someone who takes care of something. who nurtures something . so that it can grow.  A Murabbee is someone who is responsible for the growth and development of the one placed under his care. Now is it possible for me to own something. have authority over it. but not take good care of it?  . Sure! I'll send you a picture of my backyard! .  I could own a car.  but its possible that I never get it serviced. right?. We own our bodies. and we have authority over it. but we don't necessarily take good care of it. right?
So we can have ownership. we can also have authority over it.  but that does not necessarily mean that we also take good care of it. A Rabb is someone who not only owns. who not only has authority.  he also takes complete care of it. He ensures its proper growth. He nurtures it.  And this process of his taking care of it is called. Tarbiyyah. A poet says.



The depth of the ocean. nurtures the white clear pearl. So even the ocean is called Rabb. because it helps develops the pearl within its shell. So there are all these different kinds of tarbiyah. Tarbiyyah is all about setting limits. setting boundaries. That's what Tarbiyyah is.

Tarbiyah of a plant would be you taking care of it.  watering it at the right time.  making sure it gets enough sunlight. not too much sunlight. protecting it from insects and bugs. So a bunch of dos and don'ts. until it matures into a tree and starts bearing fruit. You understand?. You just leave the plant to grow by itself. that's not tarbiyyah. because you aren't setting boundaries.

Tarbiyah of a child is taking care of their physical needs. their diets. their clothing. their mental needs. educating them. protecting them. Basically. monitoring their progress. from birth. until they mature into a healthy sound, decent human being. From a physical point of view. from a psychological point of view. and from a social point of veiw. This is.  تربیۃ الاولاد .
Now. Is tarbiyyah an easy process.  or is it a VERY long. VERY time consuming process?. It's VERY hard work!. In fact it is THE MOST DIFFICULT process there is. It's a FULL TIME job.  And that's why it's appreciation. and the gratitude for it. has been placed by Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) in  التحیات . that we recited in EVERY SINGLE Salaah. What do we say in the last sentence?
اللھم مغفرلی . Oh Allah forgive me. و لوالدی . and my parents. والرحمھما کما ربیانی صغیرۃ . and have mercy on them. as they had mercy on me . during the period of my tarbiyyah. when I was young. Why is EVERY child being forced to say this in EVERY single prayer?. It is a reminder for every child to be grateful. and honor.  the rububiyyah of his parents. 
Some kids today. they do ALL sorts of nasty things in school with their friends. Just to fit in. Just to appear COOL. Just for some attention. They do things . that are completely against the TARBIYYAH of their parents. And then they so proudly plaster it all over the internet for the world to see. You have to understand. that when you're out in the world.  you are representing the tarbiyyah of your parents. When you and I do nasty things. in the name of whatever. the world does not see YOU behind those actions. they see the RUBUBIYYAH of your parents. You think you're just expressing your freedom. Being honest. Being who you are. But what you don't realize is that you are embaressing your parents in the process. and tarneshing what their rububiyyah represents. Because that is not what they have TAUGHT you. That is not what they have SLAVED over you for. You are DEFINITELY better than that.
And this is the most natural principle that you will find no matter where you go in life. You go to college and you don't represent the training. the tarbiyyah.  of your high school. what is the first thing your professor will say?. Did they not teach you anything in school?. Why?. Because you are a representative of their training. You start your first job . and you can't represent the skills your CV shows. what will your boss say?. Is this what your teachers have taught you in school?. What school did you go to?. The second anyone messes up. immediately their Rabb is questioned. You act crazy in life. the world will point fingers at your PARENTS rububiyah. not at you!.
Is that justice?. Is that fair?. Isn't that Zulm?. What did we learn about unjust people?. where do they end up?. And after EVERY thing they've done for you ALL YOUR LIFE. the VERY LEAST you can do. is not dishonor their Rububiyyah.

You know a tree is called a Rabb for the fruits it bears. The fruit represent the tree. In ancient arab. infact. even today in agricultural places like Pakistan. You go to one of these farms. and people will tell you. Don't pick from that tree. Stay away from that tree. It has the most horrible fuit. Pick fruit from THAT tree. THAT tree bears the sweetest fruit. The fruit represents the tree. It honors the tree by being sweet. YOU GUYS are the fruits of your parents. You REALLY need to think about that. We all do. We need to behave in ways that HONOR the tarbiyyah of our parents to the world. Not disgrace them. Not after EVERYTHING they did for us. right?. And this applies to you as kids. this applies to us as adults. this applies to us as Muslims. Because Islam is Tarbiyyah. Why do you think Islam has such a horrible status in the world today?. Because we. as Mulsims have disgraced it. We have dishonored the tarbiyyah of the ultimate Rabb. Because we represent Islam. whether we want to or not. People look at us and judge Islam. Just as people look at you and judge your parents.

This is really something we ALL need to think about.

Anyway. So Rububiyyah. or Murabbee is the one who is responsible for the maturity and the growth of someone or something. And how does the Rabb carry out his responsibilities?. With Rehma. Rehma is the primary component of Rububiyyah. If there is no rehma. then there is no rububiyyah. And what does the word Rehma mean?. Love, care, concern and mercy. remember?. So that's what rububiyyah is made of.

Have you ever seen people who take care of plants. very gently. with a lot of TLC?. They'll actually spray each individual leaf with water. and then clean gently them. THAT love. that care. that gentleness . that is the true image of Rububiyyah. It is not harshness. It is not beating. It is not psychological. emotional and physical abuse. It is not guilt tripping into submissing. It is love. it is patience. it is kindness. THAT is the islamic way of Rububiyyah. The islamic way of Rububiyah has ALWAYS been REHMA.
Our prophet (Salawaat).  took the most viscious people. he took the most barbaric people.  and without a SINGLE slap. without a single taunt.  without a single sarcastic remark. without a single insult.  He turned them all into رضی اللہ عنہ .  The greatest title possible for a human being. رضی اللہ عنہ. We don't mention the name of these sahaba without say RA. Our prophet did that. how?. With love. with gentleness. with kindness. forgiveness. open arms. patience. Akhlaaq. That's RUBUBIYYAH.

So these are the two sides of the coin. RUBUBIYYAH has to be with REHMA. And then the Marboob. the child has to show gratitude for that Rububiyyah. by honoring its Rabb. Just like the fruit honors its tree by being sweet. So from now on. everytime we recite Tahayyat. and we reach the sentence.
اللھم مغفرلی ولوالدی ورحمھما کما ربیانی صغیرا
let that be a reminder to us parents.  that REHMA should be the primary component of our Rububiyyah. especially when disciplining kids. And for YOU kids. let it remind you that you have to honor that rububiyyah. you have to make your parents proud. by displaying and reflecting their tarbiyah to the world around you.
And both will make mistakes. That's OK. You will mess up at times. and parents will mess up at times.  This religion does not demand perfection. All it demands is sincerity and effort. That's it. And this is why that sentence contains. اللھم مغفرلی ولوالدی. Oh Allah forgive me.  and forgive my parents. Forgive what?. Forgive me for the mistakes I make. for my insufficiency.  in reflecting the tarbiyyah of my parents. and forgive my parents for THEIR weakness in not being able to live up to YOUR name of Rabb. Forgive them for the mistakes they make in their tarbiyyah. because I know they are doing the best they can. And forgive me for the mistakes I make. in not being able to reflect their tarbiyyah. to level it deserves.

I hope nobody takes offense in what I'm saying. I'm just explaining what this word means as the scholars have explained it. I'll be the FIRST to admit that when it comes to the INABILITY  and INJUSTICE. in reflecting the tarbiyyah of my parents and my spiritual teachers. I find myself to be the WORST!. Both as a child AND as a parent. May Allah forgive me and grant me the ability to fulfill the requirements of this trust of Rububiyyah that he has honored me with.

So now what we've learnt so far. is that Allah as Rabb. He has COMPLETE ownership. He has ABSOLUTE authority. AND he takes care of ALL of his creation with REHMA. with love, care, concern and mercy.
Now at this point. you may wonder. if that's the case then how come there is SO much misery in the world. If Allah is such a LOVING and CARING Murabbee. why are people in such horrible conditions. We'll talk about that InshaAllah. when we study Malik Yaum AlDeen. There are ALWAYS rules.  and then there are exceptions to the rules. What we're looking at today. is the rule. We'll talk about the exception later. But just to give you something to think about. and hopefully this example will help you understand. Let's say you hear about this really AMAZING teacher. EVERYBODY who graduated from his class tells you. Man! You HAVE to get into his class. He is SO awesome. And you keep hearing this from a bunch of people about how AMAZINGLY AWESOME this teacher is. And you are intrigued. But then you also see. that a bunch of students fail his class every year. So you say. How come?. If he's such an amazing teacher. how come so many students are failing every year. right?. Well the question is. Is the failure because of the teacher. or is it because of the students?.
It couldn't be the teacher. because there are MANY MANY students. each year who ARE graduating the class. and they are RAVING about what an awesome teacher he is. So then it might not be the teacher that is the problem. it must be the students. And any teacher in this group can appreciate this.



The fourth meaning of the word Rabb. is Murshad. He is the one who sets in the right direction. puts one on the right path.  puts to proper use. that's Murshad. Murshad comes from the word رُشد. which in classical arabic means to RIPEN. which is the final stage for a fruit. That's why Rushd also means rationality. or reason. or maturity. because those are the final stages of intellect.
So Murshad is somone. who takes something raw . and works on it till it ripens. till it matures. and then puts it to its proper use. He sets it in the right direction. So let's say if you have a teacher who trains you in computer sciences. and then also finds you a job. so that you can now apply what you've learnt. that would be a Murshad. A murshad is not someone who just trains you to maturity. and then leaves you to rot. He actually puts you on the path. guides you forward FROM your point of maturity. so that you and others can benefit from what you've acquired.

So now Allah as Rabb . is not only someone who own us. who has complete authority over us. who nurtures us with love and care. He also creates opportunities for us so that we can put our training to good use. He'll train you. by putting people in your path that will help you develop. he'll find the perfect friend for you. who will help you grow. until you mature. and then he will also help you put that training to use. Even parents and teachers cannot do that sometimes. they will complete the tarbiyah of the children. but then they cannot always put them to proper use.  kids have to find their own path. But Allah as Rabb. goes the extra mile. and sets us on the right path AFTER our training is complete. SubhanAllah.






OK. The next meaning of the word Rabb. is Munim. Munim is the one who gives gifts. who gives blessings. The word مُنعِم  comes from نِعَم. or  نعمۃ.  which means gifts. or blessings. We don't have slavery today. But imagine for a second that we own a slave. Actually just think of your boss. cause he owns a slave. Hahah. So it is one thing to own a slave.  take care of it. put it to proper use.  but now. on top of everything. also give it gifts. And the word نعمۃ. suggests.  gifts and benefits. that are on TOP of what he deserves. Gifts are not deserved items. Gifts. by definition. are always beyond what is deserved.
Imagine that you own.  I don't know a goat. You own a goat. and so you take care of it. But you don't buy it gifts. You don't buy it jewellery. right?. I hope you don't buy it jewellery. You don't need to. it's a goat!!!!. its part of the property.  So in the old days.  slaves were no different than a goat or an animal.  they were barely taken care of. let alone given gifts.
Interestingly the arabic word. نَعَم. which means YES. also comes from the same root word as blessing!. Why?. Because what's the natural human response to the question. Would you like a gift? Would you like a blessing?. Its نَعَم. YES!. This is what I love about this language.

But Allah as Rabb. is an owner. who not only takes good care of its property. has complete authority over it. ensures its growth to maturity.  looks after it.  protects it.  sustains it. puts it on the right path. But then ON top of all of that.  He also gives it numerous gifts. Think about that for a second. He doesn't owe us anything. Therefore anything and everything he gives us. has to be a gift. It is not something he is obligated to give us at all. I didn't do anything to deserve my eyes. I did not pay for my hand. How much would you charge. if I asked you to sell both your eyes to me?. Forget both eyes. How much would you sell me ONE eye for?.  How much will you sell both your hands for?.  How much your legs. your ability to walk is worth to you?  . How much will you charge for your heart?. We can't. because these are priceless gifts. And He will question us on the day of judgment about these gifts.
ثُمَّ لَتُسْـَٔلُنَّ يَوْمَئِذٍ عَنِ ٱلنَّعِيمِ
On that day you will be asked about the greatest of ALL gifts. which is Eman. Naeem means the GREATEST gift of all. What is that gift?. It is THE GIFT. for which all these other gifts have been given to us. and that is Emaan. THAT is the ULTIMATE gift. Emaan. On the day of judgment he will ask about THIS Naeem. THE GREATEST BLESSING OF ALL. Otherwise what was the purpose of giving us these gifts?. So that we could see the creations. reflect on them. and get closer to Him.

That is why the Rabb is منعم . He gives نعمۃ. so we can نَعَم. to the  نعیم. We can affirm the the ultimate blessing of faith.  Oooh. there's a nice tongue twister there.

So now we understand that Allah as Rabb.  is someone who not only owns us. has authority over us. not only does nurture us. with love and kindness. and patience. Not only does he bring us to maturity. and put us on his chosen path. He also showers us with TONS and TONS of UNDESERVED gifts.






The final meaning is of AlQayyim. Rabb is also Qayyim. Qayyim is the one who makes sure that things stay together. they doesn't fall apart. Because when you don't take care of things. what happens to them?. They fall apart. Sometimes in gardening.  you have very very delicate plants. if you don't take care of them even one day.  they die. Some have fish for pets.  you don't feed it for one day.  you have Nemo kabaab for dinner. hahaha . that's horrible.

So Qayyim. or sustainer. or maintainer. is also embedded in the word Rabb. That's why the Quran says.
اللہ لا الہ ھو الحی القیوم
Qayyumm is the constant sustainer. the constant maintainer. I am not alive because I take care of myself. One breadth to the next.  is not because I eat healthy. exercise.  follow a good diet. I live in a healthy environment. That is not why I am alive. I am alive because he allows me to be alive. Not because of my efforts. There are plenty of ways I can cease to exist in a second. just crossing the road. one little earthquake. one snow blizzard. A guy in my office. his wife died picking up her kids from school. clot in the brain.  that's it. perfectly healthy woman. fitness trainer by profession. with no history of anything. She picked up her kids got to the car was reaching out for the door. and dropped dead. She probably had lots of plans for the evening just as I do. I'm sure she had lots of short term goals. long term goals. ALL GONE. in a second. We exist. because the qayyim is LETTING us exist. We are COMPLETELY and CONSTANTLY dependent on Allah.

Another thing. in this ayah. we see two attributes mentioned. AlHayye. and Qayyum. The ever living. and the constant maintainer.  Now why these two attributes together. It's together because the one that gives life. knows how to sustain it. how long to sustain it. what stages and steps to take it through. how to end it. when to end it. what happens after it ends. THE ENTIRE plan of action for each individual creation. not just human beings. ALL CREATION. is already and completely planned out.
That's part of the meaning of Qayyim. to have a plan. You can't start something or maintain something without a plan. can you?. When you decide to start a business. you don't just choose what business you're going to do by rock paper scissors?. You have to have an entire business plan right?. What your initial investment is going to be. how will you grow the business. cost and expense analysis. budget allocations. you plan the whole 9. And ALL of this is BEFORE you actually even begin the business. You think Allah just created us without a plan?. That's not possible right.

So now let's look at the complete definition of the word Rabb.
الرب ھو المالک  والسَّیِّد و المُرَبِّی والمُرشِد وَالمُنعِم والقَیِّم
Rabb is someone who is Maalik. who has ABSOLUTE ownership. At the same time he is Sayyed. has COMPLETE and UNCONDITIONAL authority. At the same time he is Murabbee. He esures growth. takes care. nurtures and protects. with love, care, concern and mercy. At the same time He is Murshad. who brings us to physical and spiritual maturity and then sets on his straight path. puts us to proper use. At the same time he is Munim. who showers us with undeserved and innumerous gifts and blessings. And at the same time is Qayyim. who sustains us for the extent of our duration.
Allah as our Rabb. is ALL of these things. ALL at the same time. This is something you ALWAYS have to understand. Rabb is not ONE of these things at different times of your life. He is ALL of these things.ALL at the same time. His ownership includes his authority. which includes his nurture. which includes his guidance. which includes his blessings. which includes his sustenance. ALL at the same time.  SubhanAllah.


This is why that person of sound essence. the one from the UlilAlbaab. this is why he called his creator Rabb. Because when he reflected on the creations of the heavens and earth. this is what he saw. He saw an absolute owner. who also has complete authority. who is nurturing and developing his creation. with love and care and mercy. who is setting everything to its purpose. who is bestowing every creation with gifts and blessings. and he is sustaining them through time. continuously. This is why he said.
رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا
OUR RABB. You did not create all of this without a purpose. And this is an EXTREMELY beautiful conclusion. because Allah matched that conclusion in his revelation. What is the VERY first ayah that was revealed to Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam)?
ٱقْرَأْ بِٱسْمِ رَبِّكَ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ ‎
Read with the name of your RABB who created you. Not ٱقْرَأْ بِٱسْمِ اللہِ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ ‎. Now this god introducing himself to his Messenger for the very first time. isn't it?. And when you introduce. how do you introduce yourself?. With your name or your attribute?. If I met you for the very first time. and I said. AsSalaamAlaykum. I'm the sunday session teacher. You'll be like.  WalaykumAsSalaam . You're also a weirdo. right?. Because that's not normal. When you introduce yourself. you use your name.
So I would imagine. Allah should have said.ٱقْرَأْ بِٱسْمِ اللہِ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ . Read with the name of ALLAH who created you?. isn't it? . huh!. He says. Read in the name of your RABB who created you. Allah chose to introdue himself as RABB. What does this tell you?.

When I introduce myself as Sunday Session teacher. what am I telling you?. What am I characterizing myself as. What am I saying.  is WAY more important to me than all my other attributes?. My being a teacher. right?. Even though Allah is glorious beyond comprehension. he is magnificent beyond comprehension. he is powerful beyond comprehension. What he's saying to Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). and to us THROUGH him. is that when I interact with you. the MOST important thing to me. The way I want you to think of me. is NOT Jaleel. NOT Azeem. NOT Qawee. NOT Kabeer. Not Mutakabbir. but what?. Rabb.

I just want all of you guys to take a moment. and let this sink in. When a king introduces himself. does he introduce himself in a humble way. Does he say. I'm your neighbour. I'm your dad's friend. I'm your caretaker. NO!!!!!. He says I AM YOUR KING. KNEEL. BOW DOWN BEFORE ME!. right?. If Allah did that would it befit him to do that?. ABSOLUTELY!. But what does he say instead?. RABB.

can you imagine how important this word must be to him. That he introduced his most beloved messenger with this name?.

So today let's see if we can understand this word Rabb.


I'll show you one more cool thing before we study this word. Let's look at the very first Ayah that was ever revealed to the messenger of Allah. and the very last ayah that was revealed. The first ayah we know is.
ٱقْرَأْ بِٱسْمِ رَبِّكَ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ ‎
And the very last ayah that was revealed to the messenger of Allah
ٱلْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِى وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ ٱلْإِسْلَمَ دِينًۭا ۚ
On this day I have perfected your religion for you. and I have completed my blessings on you. and selected Islam as the way of life for you.
فَمَنِ ٱضْطُرَّ فِى مَخْمَصَةٍ غَيْرَ مُتَجَانِفٍۢ لِّإِثْمٍۢ ۙ
Now here is the final part of the ayah.
فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ

No doubt about it . ALLAH is All forgiving and All merciful. He begins the revelation with the word Rabb. and ends it with Allah.
And also. what are two attributes he begins the Quran with?. بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم. and what does he end it with . غَفُورٌۭ رَّحِيمٌۭ. the constantly forgiving and the constantly loving. He begins with his intense and constant Rehma. and ends with his constant forgiveness and constant Rehma. SubhanAllah!
 

In the previous session we looked at the linguistic meaning of the word Rabb.  We learnt that a Rabb is.
المالک  والسَّیِّد و المُرَبِّی والمُرشَد وَالمُنعِم والقَیِّم
Rabb is someone who is Maalik. who has ABSOLUTE ownership. and at the same time has COMPLETE authority. And within that space of the complete ownership and unrestricted authority. he esures growth. he takes care of his creation. nurtures them . protects them. And then not only does he nurture them to maturity. he also sets them on his straight path. he puts each creation to it's proper use. Showering them with numerous . undeserved gifts and blessings along the way. And then he also sustains them. and maintains them. for the extent of their duration. that he has planned for us on this earth. And the MOST impotant ingredient in this recipie. is that all of these 6 meanings are grounded in that one fundamental emotion of rehma. of intense and constant love and care.الرحمن علم القرآن. The loving The merciful taught the Quran.  NOT . الجبار علم القرآن. So Rehma is the most important element of his Rububiyyah.

And so when this person of sound essence. when he reflected on the creations of the heaves and the earth.  he used the word Rabb to call upon his creator.
رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا
رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ مَن تُدْخِلِ ٱلنَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُۥ
رَّبَّنَآ إِنَّنَا سَمِعْنَا مُنَادِيًۭا يُنَادِى لِلْإِيمَنِ أَنْ آمِنُوا۟ بِرَبِّكُمْ فَـَٔامَنَّا

So he used Rabb. And he used that word because he saw the creations.  reflecting the rububiyyah of their creator. The existence of the Rabb. and his rububiyyah. is made evident by the murabbee. In other words. the murabbee.  the one being nurtured. he become a sign. pointing back to his Rabb. He becomes an Ayah for his Rabb. 
And this applies even to us. For example our parents. they take the role of a Rabb. of a creator. for our nurturing and training. And then we. as murabbee. as children. we  play the role of their creation. and then the same principle applies. WE as creations of our parents. then reflect the attributes and the training of OUR creator. So you can see this is a universal principle. It's not falsifiable.

I'll give you an example. Let's say you meet a person.  and you see that he is a very skilled electrician.  So from a rational stand point. just by observing his knowledge and skill.  you would HAVE to logically conclude that he went to a good electrical engineering school. or had a very skilled teacher.  who taught him this electrical work. Now you haven't actually seen the teacher. nor do you know the name of his school. but you are still able to conclude that. why?. Because this electrician. is his teachers creation.  And through his skill and knowledge. he is manifesting the attributes and the training of his teacher. Because that is what EVERY creation does. it manifests the rububiyyah of its creator. And if this is true at a microcosmic level. it certainly holds true at the macrocosmic level. That this universe too. being a creation. is manifesting the attributes of its creator. This SIGN. this AYAH. has been placed in the design.  in the DNA of creation. That it cannot help but reflect the attributes and the rububiyyah of its Rabb. And the more you think about this. the more you will be able to appreciate the reality of this design. You will ALWAYS be able to identify the creator THROUGH the creation. no matter where you look in the world.

Now even though Rabb is commonly translated as LORD in English. linguists agree that a more suitable one word replacement for the word Rabb. is Master. Because master not only represents ownership and authority and control. it also represents perfection of knowledge and skill. which is required to nurture and guide and maintain. So MASTER. is much closer in meaning to the word Rabb. than lord.  or any other English word that is available to us in the language.

Now once we understand the word Rabb. the next thing to understand. is that the word Rabb. implies a relationship. There are certain words that just automatically imply relationship. They need a counter part. For example when I say teacher. who does a teacher have a relationship with?. with students. It automatically implies that reslationship. I can't be a teacher if I don't have any students. right?.  When I say parent. who do they have a relationship with? . children. When I say boss or employer. it implies a relationship with employees!. There are certain titles that necessarily have a relationship. But when I say "Intelligent" it doesn't necessarily have a relationship with anyone. right?. When I say "tall" that doesn't imply a relationship with anyone.

Similarly Allah has certain names.  that do not imply a relationship. For example. Allah is lofty. He is الأعلی. It's a powerful attribute. but it does not imply a relationship . It's simply a fact. It is a description of one of his attributes. which is independant of anything else. But then he also has certain names.  which DO establish a relationship. For example. خالق. the creator. If he is a creator. there has to be. مخلوق.  there has to be creation. Similarly if Allah is غفور. He's forgiving. There has to someone TO forgive. Yes?. So there are some attributes of Allah that are relational in nature.  and then there are others that are not.

But when Allah begins his revelation with the word Rabb. اقرأ بسم ربک الذی خلق. When he introduces himself as Rabb. as master. to Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). and then by extension to us. what he's essentially doing is. He is putting all of those other relational attributes aside. and he's saying to us. When you think of me. the first and foremost relationship that you need to think of. The ONE relationsihp that you should never let go of. EVEN if you forget all the other relations I have with you. The one you should ALWAYS be mindful of. every single waking moment of your life . is that "I" am your Rabb. I am your master. You understand?.  He's saying. Above and beyond everything else.I want you know. that I am your Rabb.

Now if Allah is Rabb.  If he is master. then what does that make me?. and what does it make you?. It makes ALL of us his slaves.  and the Arabic word for slave. is عبد . So when we accept Allah as our Rabb. just by doing that. we automatically accept the fact. that we are his slaves.
 


عبد

So today I'd like us to understand a little bit about this word عبد . because understanding our place in this hierarchy. in this relationship. and accepting it. will complete our relationship with him. And its really important to do that. Because a teacher cannot benefit a student. until the student does not acknolwedge and accept that person as his teacher!. A student can ONLY benefit from the teacher. when he ACCEPTS that relationship. and submits to it. isn't it?. A doctor cannot help a patient. until what?. Until the patient accepts and submits to the cure of the doctor. If the patient has diabetes and the doctor is asking him to stop eating candy. but everytime he sees candy. he goes. Oh I know the doctor asked me NOT to eat it. but what does he know anyway. It's only a little bit. It's not like I'm eating the whole bag. or whatever. It doesn't make sense to me why I can't eat candy. After all what has candy got to do with diabetes.  Now if the patient does that. he's not accepting the doctor as his doctor. and he is not submitting to him as his patient. So will the doctor be able to benefit the patient?. NO. The patient needs to first accept that relationship and complete the process. and ONLY then he will be able to gain benefit. You understand?. Its a two way street. The doctor HAS  the knowledge to benefit the patient. the doctor WANTS to benefit the patient.  because he cares about the patient. and he is genuinely concerned about him. But he cannot do anything to help the patient. Why?.  Because the patient has not yet completed the relationship.

This means that even though Allah is my Rabb. Even though he is المالک؛ و المربی ؛ والمرشد ؛ والمنعم ؛ و القیم ; والسید. And even though ALL of these are REALLY beneficial attributes. But for me to gain the benefits from my Rabb. What do I have to do?.  I have to complete the relationship. How do I complete the relationship?. By submitting myself to him as his عبد . As his slave. you understand?

Now listen to this very carefully. The greatest CHALLENGE. The greatest DIFFICULTY. The greatest HARDSHIP. that you and I will CONSTANTLY face. EVERY single waking moment of our lives. is to accept Allah as Rabb.  I'll say that again. The greatest and constant challenge. you and I and everyone else in this world faces. is NOT in accepting our creator as Allah. Everyone is OK with that part. Even the jahilee Arabs accepted him as Allah. The REAL problem. is in accepting Him as Rabb. as master. You know why?.  Because if we accept him as Rabb. that means we have to become what?. We have to become slaves. we have to become عبد .  And do you know what a slave is?.  A slave is someone who no longer has a choice. He no longer has free will. He has to now obey the will of his master. He is nothing more than an extension of his masters desires. 
And we live in the times of choices.  We live in the times of free will. We live in the times where I am in charge. I am in control. I am the master of my own destiny. I am powerful. I am wealthy. I don't have to listen to you. You're not the boss of me. I can do whatever I want. whenever I want. I am the king of my domain.  This is MY life. If I wanna do it I'll do it. If I don't wanna do it. I won't!. In other words.  I AM MY OWN RABB!!.  I AM MY OWN RABB. I am my own god.  I am my own master.
And Allah is saying. No!.  I am your master. I gave you this life. I gave you this authority. I gave you these gifts of parents.  I gave you these gifts of children. I honored you with position and power. I gave you health and strength.  So don't abuse them. Because I can just as easily take them away from you. Don't forget. I am your Rabb!
ٱلْحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكَ.  فَلَا تَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلْمُمْتَرِينَ
The greatest challenge. that you and I will ever face in our lives.  The greatest challenge we will CONSTANTLY face. is to ACCEPT that Allah is my Rabb. and I am his slave. My master's will is my command. That is the signature action of a true abd. My master I am not going to make my own decision. You will make my decisions for me. If you tell me to do something. I will do it. even if I don't feel like doing it. If you tell me NOT to do something. I won't do it. even if I'm dying to do it.  I willingly and happily give up my freedom to become your slave. because you are my Rabb. And nobody can be a better Rabb than you.

Now here's the next question. Am I a slave ONLY if I accept Allah as master?. In other words. let's say I don't accept him as Rabb. Does that now mean. that I am NO LONGER his slave?. Well let's go back to the definition of Rabb. He is Maalik. He is owner. Forget all the other definitions. lets just stick with this one. Just by the fact that he is Maalik. he is the OWNER of EVERY SINGLE CREATION. THAT fact alone. makes EVERY SINGLE creation his property. His slave. Doesn't it?.Which means being his property. or his slave. has nothing to do with being Muslim or not. Because now that word applies to EVERY SINGLE CREATION. The sun is his slave. the moon is is slave. the galaxies. the entire universe and EVERYTHING within it is his slave. EVERYTHING is his property. So this means. when believers CHOOSE to submit to him. they are his slaves. and when disbelievers choose to disbelieve him. reject his ownership. guess what?. They are still his slaves. They are still his property. You understand?. So the question now is not that who is a slave and who is not. because in the last analysis EVERYONE and EVERYTHING is his slave.  The only difference now is. who is an obedient slave. and who is a disobedient slave. That's the ONLY real question.

So now who is going to TRULY benefit from the Rabb?. In some sense both will. Because this Rabb is AlRehman AND AlRaheem. The Rehman will benefit EVERY CREATION. obedient or disobedient. He is neutral in that respect. Just as the mother will feed all her children equally. the obedient and the disobedient. but when it comes to rewards. who will she reward naturally?. The obedient child or the disobedient child?. A good mother. even though she loves all her children equally. she will not reward her child for bad behavior. A teacher will teach all of his children equally. but the obedient and hard working student will attract the teachers favors and blessings MORE than the slackers. isn't it?. He will go above and beyond the call of duty in teaching the students who really want to learn. who have really submitted to that relationship. Similarly the Rehman will be a Rabb to both. the disobedient AND the obedient slave. But the obedient slave will receive special rewards. PERMANENT rewards from the Raheem.

And now if we go back to ayaats about this person of sound essence. we learn that when he uses the word Rabb for his creator. Not ONLY did he accept his creator as his Rabb. he also submitted himself as his obedient slave. Because a bit later. when he hears Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) calling out to this revelation. we see that he immediately accepts. 
رَّبَّنَآ إِنَّنَا سَمِعْنَا مُنَادِيًۭا يُنَادِى لِلْإِيمَنِ أَنْ آمِنُوا۟ بِرَبِّكُمْ

Even though the ayah is saying we HEARD a man calling (past tense). but the conversation is happening with the Rabb in the present tense (Rabbana). So he should have said Fanu'minoon.

Our master, indeed we have heard a caller calling to faith, saying, 'Believe in your master,'. فَـَٔامَنَّا. We have believED. The point I want you to understand. is WHEN the acceptance ACTUALLY took place. And this is why knowing Arabic grammar is so important to understand the Quran. The word فَـَٔامَنَّا . is in the past tense. It's not saying. فنؤمنون. we now believe. NO. فَـَٔامَنَّا. We have already believED. Why is he talking in the past tense?. Because the believing happened in the past. when he was reflecting on the creations of the heaves and the earth. that's when the belief in his Rabb took place. At this point its just affirmation. Another lesson we learn from these ayats. is that sincere reflection. makes accepting revelation. EASY!!!. The one who finds the teachings of the Quran difficult. is the one who has NOT YET taken the time to honestly and sincerly reflect on it. Because revelation. this Quran. it simply CONFIRMS what REFLECTION concludes. This persons reflections. they force him to CONCLUDE that his creator is Rabb. And then with revelation. Allah simply confirms his conclusions when He says. الحمد للہ رب العلمین. Praise and gratitude is for Allah. who is what?. Rabb Al-Alameen. Allah confimed. that Indeed. I am your Rabb. All the revelation did at this point. is give his Rabb a name. Allah.

Relationship between words Allah and Rabb

Allah is the one I worship?. The one I submit my will to?. What is the arabic for worship?. عبادۃ. and who does عبادۃ. the A'bd. the slave. By accepting Allah as our Rabb. didn't we just submit to being his slaves?. So Allah is Rabb. They're both related to each other.
Allah is the one I turn to protection. Isn't that one of the things that ownership, authority and nurture provides?. Protection?. When a child is scared. who does it turn to?. It's parents. It's Rabb. So Allah is Rabb.
Allah is the one I am completely loyal and devoted to.  Does a student become completely loyal and devoted to his teacher. his Rabb. in order to gain his knowledge?. He has to. Allah is Rabb.
Allah is the one who is so LOFTY. so beyond my capabilities of comprehension and understanding. that I would be dumb-founded. everytime I would try to approach Him. right?. Now if you think about Allah as Rabb. Is Allah just your rabb?. and is he just my Rabb?.  or is he the Rabb of EVERY SINGLE CREATION. Not just this world. but solar systems within galaxies and galaxies within universe. Parents have a couple of kids. and their needs drive them nuts. How many is Allah taking care of?. ALL AT THE SAME TIME?. If you JUST think of this ONE thing. This one SINGLE aspect of his Rububiyyah. I mean there are millions of other things to reflect upon. But even if you just think of this ONE thing. where does that leave you?. Dumbfounded!. GobSmacked as your English people say. right?. Once again. Allah is Rabb.
Allah is the one I can lean on. put my weight on. the one I can trust. Do we trust a Rabb?. Does a student trust his teacher?. Does a child trust its parents?. Is it completely dependent on the parent?.  Absolutely. Allah is Rabb.
Allah is the one I am passionately in love with. he is the one I am obsessed about. Do kids ABSOLUTELY LOVE their parents?. especially mothers?. My son Amir is 3 and a half years old. He can't stay a minute without his mother. She leaves him with me for 5 minutes. and he's like Mamaamama. I want mamaaaaa. That's the love for her rububiyyah. He can't stay away from her. Allah is Rabb.

You know this concept of the love of Allah in Islam. It is really such an incredible thing. Some of the poets. I mean . in my opinion. there is really NO poetry like Arabic poetry. Just because of this language. And the way some people have expressed their love for Allah. It's just.

فَلَيـتَكَ تَحلُو وَالحَيـاةُ مَـرِيرَةٌ . وَلَيـتَكَ تَرضـى وَالأنـامُ غِضَـابُ
وَلَيـتَ الَّذِي بَيـنِي وَ بَينَـكَ عَامِرٌ . وَبَـينِي وَبَيـنَ العــالَمِينَ خَـرَابُ
فَيالَيـتَ شُـربِي مِن وِدَادِكَ صَافِياً . وَشُـربِي مِن مَـاء الفُراتِ سَـرَابُ
إذا نِلتُ مِنكَ الوُدَّ فَالكُلُّ هَيِّـنٌ . وَكُـلَّ الَّذي فَوقَ الـتُّرابِ تُـرابُ

Rabb Alameen


The next things we find interesting. in this conclusion drawn by this person of sound intellect. is that he says.

رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا
رَّبَّنَآ إِنَّنَا سَمِعْنَا مُنَادِيًۭا يُنَادِى لِلْإِيمَنِ

OUR Master. He does not say. ربی ما خلقت ھذا باطلا. MY master you did not create all of this in vain. NO He says . ربنا. OUR master. He speaks in the plural. why?. Because he also realizes that he is not alone. He has been created to exist AMONG other creations. And Allah is not just HIS Rabb. He is also the Rabb of every other creation. And this conclusion is once again confirmed by Allah (Azza Wa Jal) . when he calls himself. رب العالمین. Master of Alameen.




Linguistic analysis of ALAM, ALIM and ALEEM
Now let's look at the meaning of this word. العالمین. It's singular form is عالَم  which is اسم مفعول بہ . it is an object for the subject which is عالِم. But forget the grammar part. I just want you to look at these two words. Aalam and Aalim. You can see they both have the EXACT same spelling. The only difference between Aal-a-m and Aal-i-m is the fatha and kasra. Other than that they both have the same spelling. And we've seen this science in Arabic a few time before.  that when two words share a common spelling. they have a deep connection in their meaning. Because they both also share the same root word . which is Ilm. knowlege.
عالِم is the one WHO KNOWS. And the عالَم  is THAT which he comes to know of. 
عالِم. the one who knows. is the CASUSE. And عالَم. this world.  is that WHICH IS KNOWN. its the EFFECT.

See human beings can know many many things. But even with all the knowledge we have gained. we still cannot know everything. We are knowledgable about certain things.  and at the same time we are ignorant of other things. As opposed to Allah who is علیم . Who is the one with ABSOLUTE knowledge of everything. But there is NO way for human beings to dirctly know Allah. We cannot know what god is. any more than we can know what god isn't. And the reason for that is. that we are speaking of Allah. we are speaking of the INFINITE creator of the heavens and the earth. And just the fact that we understand that Allah is infinite. Infinite means without limit. Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq AS said.  اللہ اکبر من ان یحد و یحسر. Allah is great in the sense that he does not have a boundary and he cannot be confined to comprehension. In other words. Allah cannot be DEFINED. Yet the ONLY way we human beings are capable of understanding things. is THROUGH definition. Because definition is what DEFINES. or gives FINITE-ness to a concept. It limits it. It puts it in a perspective. That is what Intellect or Aqal means. To set a boundary. to confine. So now we have a problem. How do we. as human beings. as creatures of FINITE-ness and DEFINITION. understand a creator who is INFINITE and cannot be defined.

So the ONLY way possible to do that. is by having an intermediary. Like an interpreter. If all you speak is French. and all I speak is English. Then for me to understand what you're saying. I need someone in the middle who understands both languages. Who can take your message in French and then translate that for me in English. right?. And so we human beings. we needed a third entity. that could act as that interpreter. between Allah and us. Something that is DEFINED. and CONFINED in its existence so that WE could understand it. YET reflect the infiniteness of its creator. And that is the عالَم  . That is this world.

Universe manfiests existence of Allah
So Allah created this عالَم. which is this universe. so that the  عالِم could come to know of the علیم . 
You understand?. The one who knows. which is the عالِم . He comes to know of Allah who is علیم . THROUGH this universe. the عالَم. In other words. this universe is the medium through which we Muslims have always understood Allah.  We believe in Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  because of the overwhelming proofs being manifested by this universe. And that's why to us. the ultimate proof that Allah exists. is because this universe exists. And the simple fact that every created thing needs a creator. A poet says.

وُجُودُہُ لَہُ دَلِیلُ قَاطِع . حَاجَتُ کُلِّ مُحدَثٍ لِصَانِع
The most convincing that he exists. is that every sculpture requires a sculptor
کُل عالَم.  لِی حَاجَّتاً الی العَالِم
Every world. REQUIRES the existence of a knower. Nothing can exist in a passive  state. And therefore the proof.  of how we know Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . that He exists. is through the Asaar. through the effects creation. Someone asked a beduin.
بِمَ عَرَفتَ رَبُّك؟ . How did you come to know of your master? He said.
 إن البِعرَةُ تَدُلُّ علی البَعِیر . والرَّوثَةُ تَدُلُّ علی الحمیر . و آثارُ القدم تَدُلُّ علی المَسِیر

he said. The camel dunk shows me that there was a camel there. The donkey dunk tells me that was a donkey there.  Footsteps in the sand tell me that there were people walking by.
فسمآءُ ذاتُ اَبرَاج. والارض ذاتَ الفِجاج. واَبحَرُ ذَاتَ الامواج
So when I look at the sky.  with its perfect constellations.  and the earth with its perfect valleys and travises. And these oceans with all of its waves.
الا تدل علی لطیف الخبیر؟
Doesn't all of this indicate the presence of the lateef and the khabeer?. SubhanAllah! It was SO simple to him. See. we complicate the heck out of things. But the truth is.  existence of Allah IS the MOST CLEAR and MOST MANIFEST truth there is. The athiest says. I wish there was a proof of the existence of ALlah. and the believer replies. I see nothing BUT the proofs of his existence.

So linguistically speaking. that's the meaning of the word عالَم. That which is known by the عالِم . in order for him to recognize the علیم . And that's why WORLD is not the best translation for Alameen. It limits the scope of meaning. If it meant world. then it would just mean nothing other than the world. And the plural form for that would have been العوالم.  not العالمین . The word العالمین . encompasses a much broader spectrum than just the physical world. Rabb AlAlameen means. that Allah is not just the master of worlds. he is also the master of all the different species. and all the distinct groups of creation. Every group and category that we can think of is an عالَم. Because again. that is how we human beings operate. we take a bunch of KNOWN things and group them. we classify them. So العالمین means. all categories . classifications. and groups that exist. It can be عالم الروحانی، عالم الجِرمانی، عالم الجسمانی.The spiritual world. the galaxies the solar systems . It can be this physical world.  Then if we just zero in on just this physical world. it includes the various sub-domains and kingdoms. for instance. عالم المعدنیات. the mineral kingdom. عالم النبتات. plant kingdom.  عالم الحیوان. All animal life.  including human beings. عالم الانسان . And then if you further drill down within the human category. it means ALL kinds of different races. different nations. These are all called.  عالمین . For instance says. Allah says in the Quran.
يَبَنِىٓ إِسْرَٓءِيلَ ٱذْكُرُوا۟ نِعْمَتِىَ ٱلَّتِىٓ أَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَأَنِّى فَضَّلْتُكُمْ عَلَى ٱلْعَلَمِينَ
I gave you preference over every other nation. and the word used for nations here is Alameen.  It can also means different generations across time.
قُلْ آمَنَّا بِٱللَّهِ وَمَآ أُنزِلَ عَلَيْنَا وَمَآ أُنزِلَ عَلَىٰٓ إِبْرَهِيمَ وَإِسْمَعِيلَ وَإِسْحَقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَٱلْأَسْبَاطِ
Say, "We have believed in Allah and what has been revealed to us and what has been revealed to Abraham and Ismaeel and Ishaq and Yaqoob and his Descendants. Now these are all separate and distinct generations. father after son. but collectively they ALL represent عالمین. So it also includes the meaning of different time periods. And so when Allah calls himself Rabb Alalameen. What he's saying is that no matter what category. what group. what sub-group. you come to know of. You will see my Rububiyyah at work. in ALL of them.

And this is a concept we also find in the English language. So I guess the translation "WORLD" is not completely wrong if you take it in the broader sense. For example. if you talk to a senior gentleman. whose 80 years old.  If you ask him. tell me what life was when you were young. and he will begin by saying. Oh! it was a different world. Ever here that?.  You visit a different country. People who lived all their lives in the US. when they visit third world countries for the first time. they say.  This is a different world.  had no idea people could live like this as well.
I work in NY and so I'm used to a certain type of culture. I visited TX a few years ago and even St. louis. People are actually nice. they're REALLY nice. It's a different world. They actuall say weird things.  like Good morning! and How are you doing today. It's VERY strange. In NY somebody walks up to you and say.  hey good morning. how are you doing?. YOU RUN!. MAN! You run like the wind. Or pull out your pepper spray and go psssss. or whatever. HAHA

In other words. doesn't matter what civilization you belong to. Doesn't matter which culture you belong to.  I am the master of ALL of them. I am Rabb Alalameen. I don't just have ownership and authority over YOU . I don't just nurture YOU. take care of YOU. protect YOU. with love and kindness. I don't just shower blessings and gifts on YOU. I don't just maintain YOUR existence and put YOU to proper use. I do that for ALL of my creation EVERY created thing.

 

Interpreations of Rabb Al-Alameen

Now scholars have given many many beautiful interpretations of this word. Alameen. and why Allah called himself Rabb Alalameen. I'll only share a couple with you otherwise we'll be talking about this for months.

The first is that by saying Rabb Al-Alameen. Allah points out. that because it is He who created different cultures. different creations.  diffferent civilizaitons. people of different languages. Because He alone is the master of all of them. you don't have to be like anyone else.  You can just be who you are.  You don't have to look a certain way. dress a certain way. walk a certain way. talk a certain way.  You can just be yourself. That's fine.  I love you JUST the way you are.  because you are MY slave just as much as the next creation.  I will gave you guidance. and as long as you accept yourself as my slave. and follow my guidance . you can be happy living in whatever culture or civilization or society or country you're in. Because all cultures. all civilizations. all nations are honored by Allah.

The second implication here. and the more important one. when you interact with the people in life. regardless of race or religion. Don't forget that Allah is Rabb AlAlameen. You know why that's important?. Because if you hurt them. if you break their heart with your words. If you torture them with the authority I have temporarily given you over them. You better not forget. I am Rabb AlAlameen. And not just human beings. Even animals. Even plants. Even this earth. Before you're cruel to them. you better remember . I am their Rabb too.
When a slave gets hurt by someone.  who gets insulted ultimately?. The master!.  In the olden days. wars would start because the member of one tribe unjustly hurt or killed the slave of another tribe. His master took that as a personal insult. why? Because he disrespected his property. Slave is his masters responsibility.  Even if the slave was in the wrong. and deserved to be repremanded. Who should the complaint be taken to? His master.
So Allah says. I am Rabb AlAlameen. be careful how you interact with my creation. No matter what group.  what religion.  what cast.  what belief system.  what country they belong to. No matter what your relationship with them is on this earth. Doesn't matter. Before he's your son.  he's MY slave. Before she's your daughter. she's my slave. Before he's your father. before she's your mother. they are MY slaves. Before she's your daughter in law. she's my slave. Before he is your son-in-law. he is my slave. No matter what the relationship. Don't forget.  I am here! and I'm watching. If you treat them unjustly. if you hurt them. if you mentally torture them. insult them. degrade them. If you misuse your authority over them. You will have to answer to ME!!!. Because I am Rabb Alameen. SubhanAllah!

Now here is the most beautiful meaning in my opinion. And this again connects back with the concept of us accepting and submitting to him as his slaves. Scholars say. what this title رب العلمین does.  is it bring us all down on the same level in the eyes of Allah.  ALL of us are slaves. No nation. No one group is better than another. And if it is better. it is ONLY by whose standards?. It is in the eyes of who?. In the eyes of the master.

Humility of Rasul Allah(Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam)

This is something I really want you to take away from today's session. If you forget everything else. I just want you to remember this. Because in todays world we are afflicted with this disease of superiority. and this feeling of having a chip on our shoulders whether we admit to it or not.

Superiority in ranks. can only exist through the eyes of the master. based on the servitude of a slave. NOT through the eyes of the slave. إِنَّ أَكْرَمَكُمْ عِندَ اللَّهِ أَتْقَاكُمْ. The most honorable in the eyes of Allah. is the one who is the most pious. That's it. Not by anything else. Because even the HIGHST ranking person is Allah's slave. and even the LOWEST ranking person is Allahs save.اشھد ان محمد عبدہ و رسولہ. I testify that Muhammad (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) is his SLAVE and his messenger. AllahuAkbar. The highest ranking person. who has EVER walked this earth. If we believe that we hold any superiority on the basis of our creed. THAT superiority has to be by the standards of Allah. NOT us!!. We can't make that judgment for other slaves. Allah is the master of a sulemani.  just as much as he is a master of a sunni.  of a shia. of a hindu.  of a christian.  of a jew. even an athiest. Allah is the ultimate master.

You are a disgusting person.  You are horrible. You are beneath me.  I am better than you because you drink and I don't. or I pray 5 times a day and you dont. Allah loves me more than you?.  NO. أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ . خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
I am BETTER than him. I am created from fire. he is created from clay. Do you remember who said that?.  Iblees! Iblees was an angel. from the عالَم of angels. And what do we learn in that story. What did his master do?. Because you have to understand. When you and I judge each other. When you and I as SLAVES. judge OTHER slaves in terms of superiority. what position do we place ourselves in?. یُریدُ أَنَّ یَبعَثُ أُمِیِّ مِنَ الأُمِّیِّن۔وأجعل السكينةَ لباسُهُ ، والبِرَّ شَعارُهُ ، والتقوى ضَميرَهُ ، والحِكمَةَ مَنطِقَهُ ، والصِّدقَ والوفاءَ طَبِيعَتُهُ ، والعَفوَ وَالمَعرُوفَ خُلقُهُ ، والَحقَّ شَريعَتَهُ ، والعَدلَ سيرَتَهُ ، والهَدِىُ إمامُهُ ، والإسلامَ مِلَّتُهُ ، وأحمد أِسمُهُ .  أَهدِي بِهِ بَعدَ الضَّلالَة ، وأعلَمُ بِهِ مِنَ الجَهالة ، وأَرفَعُ به بعد الخَمالَة ، وأعرِفُ به بعد النَّكِرَة ، وأكثَرُ بِهِ بعدَ القِلَّة ، وأغنِي به بعد العَيلَة ، وأَجمِعُ به بعد الفُرقَة .  وأُؤَلِّفُ به بين أممٍ مُتَفَرِّقَة وَقُلُوبٍ مُختَلِفَة ، وأَهواءٌ متشَتَّتَة

لَو یَمشِی عَلی القَصَبِ الیَابِس۔۔۔ لَم یُسمَع مِن تَحتِ قَدَمَیہِ مِن سَکِینَتِہِ
