وآخر الدعوانا عن الحمد للہ رب العالمین

Man gave Rasul Allah bottle of wine as gift

There was this man who travelled a long distance to meet Rasul Allah (Salawaat). and when he met him. he gave the messenger a bottle of wine. as a gift. He said Ya RasulAllah. I got this special wine as a gift for you. What would we do if someone did that?. If someone. very secularized. shows up at your doorstep with a bottle of wine. as a house warming gift. what how would we react?. La hawla wala quwwata. How dare you. Don't you know I'm a Muslim. Don't you know this is haraam?. Get the hell out of my house. never show me your face again. right?.
And who did this man bring the wine bottle to? . Rasul Allah!!!!. The MOST pious man we can imagine. And you know how he responded?. He smiled. He smiled and said. Brother. Did you not hear Allah's command that alcohol has been prohibited?. He said.  No Rasul Allah. I never heard that!. He immediately gives the bottle to his slave and says something in his ears. Rasul Allah says. what did you just say to him?. The man said. I told him to sell the bottle in the market. Rasul Allah smiled again and said. The one who has prohibitted the consumption of intoxicants has also forbidden its trade. So the man told the slave to dump it out. This is the character of Rasul Allah. This is his humility. This is the Tarbiyyah. his rububiyyah. SubhanAllah! . He didn't say. Don't you know who I am. How dare you bring this filth in my presence. He NEVER did that. Because hearts can NEVER be conquered with harshness. Hearts have always been conquered ONLY with love. and kindness. We should really study. and learn what kind of a Rabb. what kind of a parent. what kind of teacher our prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam)  was. SubhanAllah.

 

Meaning of wisdom
We're studying the second ayah of the basmallah. الحمد للہ رب العلمین.  We've looked at the words. Allah, Rabb and Alameen. Today I want to begin discussing the word Hamd. and how it is connected to the words رب العلمین. Hamd in classical Arabic means two things. It means GRATITUDE and it means PRAISE. Once again. Hamd means gratitude and it also means praise. There is a difference between the two. Gratitude is the quality of being thankful. when something nice is done for you. Praise is admiration for something  amazing or something brilliant. Hamd means both these things at the same time. We'll do a linguistic analysis of the word Hamd in later sessions. Today I just want to talk about gratitude.which in itself is a HUGE HUGE topic. So we'll only be able to cover a portion of this today. In the next session we'll pick up. where we leave off today InshaAllah.

Allah says in the Quran.
وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ.
And We had certainly given Luqman wisdom. "Be grateful to Allah!". Luqman is the wisest man of his time.
وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ
And whoever is grateful. no doubt his gratitude ONLY benefits himself.
وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ
And whoever is ungrateful. denies Allah's favor. then indeed, Allah is Free of all need and is praiseworthy.

Let's look at this first ayah. Allah says.
وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ
We have certainly granted Luqman wisdom.

Those of you who don't know the story. Hazrat Luqman was a black man from Sudan who lived before the time of Moosa AS. I think around 1100 BC. He was a very perceptive man. One day while he was asleep under a tree, an angel came to him and said. Allah wants to bestow a gift upon you. Either wisdom. or prophethood. And Luqman chose wisdom. When he woke up from his sleep. he realized that his senses were hightened. and his understanding had become sharpened. He suddenly felt in complete harmony with nature. and he could understand the inner meaning of things. beyond their physical reality. When he realized this. he immediately fell into sajda. and thanked and praised Allah for his wonderful gift. He did two things. He thanked Allah for the gify he was given. And he praised Allah for the things he was now becoming aware of by the use of his gift.

He was then later captured by slavers. and sold as a slave. Scholars say this was his first trial. His training in slavery and servitude.He was made a slave so that he could learn how to become the TRUE SLAVE of the divine master. And because of his servitude. his عبودیۃ. he gained such a status in the eyes of his Rabb. that Allah mentioned him by name in his final message. So Allah says.
وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ
We have certainly granted Luqman. حکمۃ .  wisdom. Now what is wisdom?. When we think about wisdom what kind of things come to our minds?. Someone very knowledgable. Someone old and with a lot of experience. like Gandof in lord of the ring. Or someone who says EPICLY profound things. that when you hear them. you go. WOAH. I don't even know what you just said. But that was so deep man!!. That sort of thing? . So most people have this fuzzy idea of what wisdom means. right?

One of the most amazing things about the ancient Arab culture. is that they loved to simplifying things . They loved simplicity. And they had this  super simple definition of the word wisdom. that I want to share with you. Their definition of wisdom was this.
You are wise. when you have correct knowledge. and you act upon it. That's it. Two simple parts to wisdom. Part one. Gain beneficial or correct knowledge. And part two. act upon it. When these two things come together. that actually means that you have wisdom. It's not something fuzzy or wooo hooo. It's not an epic quote. It is something practical. To the Arabs wisdom is a practical thing.

Now let's put that to the test to understand what they mean by that. Here's a correct or beneficial knowledge. Fire burns. That is correct knowledge. That is beneficial knowledge. So wisdom would mean. that you did not stick your hand in the fire. Based on your knowledge that fire burns. if you did not stick your hand in the fire. young man.  you have acted wisely. You chose wisely young samurai. Because you acted on the knowledge that you have.

Okay.  let's take it a step further. Smoking can cause all sorts of health issues. Eventually even lung cancer. This too is correct knowledge. As a result of this knowledge what do you decide to do?. You choose not to smoke. If you make that decision. you are acting wisely. Speeding on a highway recklessly can cause a crash. You can kill yourself.  your friends and other innocent people that have nothing to do with your ridiculousness. That's pretty good knowledge. So now if you're not cutting through traffic. not creating your own version of Fast and Furious 8. trying to cut past that bus when it's about to take an exit . That's a pretty wise decision.

Now allah says.وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ. We gave Luqman wisdom. which means Luqman has two things. On the one hand he has beneficial knowledge. and on the other.  whatever knowledge he has.  he puts it to practical use. He acts upon it. His knowledge somehow changes the way he thinks. It changes the way he makes a decision. And this is very important for us all to understand as well. Because at the end of the day what is most demanded by the Quran. especially from the youth. is NOT knowledge. It's WISDOM.  Because at your age studying is easier. memorizing is easier. retaining is easier. taking a test is easier. In fact if I had to go back to school and study the stuff that you guys are studying today. and try to take the same tests that you guys take. I will do horribly in comparison to you guys. why?.  Because I am not in student mode anymore. My mind isn't as sharp as it was when I was a teenager. So gaining knowledge is VERY easy for you guys. But what is hard to do?. Acting upon it. isn't it?. This means that even though knowledge can be acquired at an earlier stage. what takes time to develop. is Wisdom. Because you may learn a lot about the Quran. but you don't really know how to use it yet. Wisdom hasn't completely settled in yet. And so in order for us to develop wisdom. we need to start APPLYING the teachings of Quran in our practical day to day life. We need to start putting it into action. In these sessions we are gaining knowledge. Once the session is over. what do we have to do?. We have to find a way to ACT upon it. Otherwise what's the point?. If we just acquire this knowledge and we do nothing with it.
کمثل حمار یحمل اسفارا
as Allah says in Surah Jumuah. These people are like a donkey carries a huge load of books on its back. But do those books actually benefit the donkey?. No. So the goal of these sessions. or any knowledge for that matter. is not to carry its burden on our backs. but to actually benefit from it. And how do you benefit from it?. By putting it into action. which is the TRUE goal of the Quran. The goal of the Quran is wisdom!

Gratitude

Now Allah is saying. We gave Luqman  wisdom. And what is the pinnacle. wha is the climax of all of his wisdom?.  Check this out. أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ . Be grateful to Allah. Be grateful to Allah. I want you to understand this part. Allah did not say. We gave wisdom to Luqman TO BE grateful to Allah. or. We gave wisdom to Luqman SO THAT he could be grateful to Allah.  Rather. We gave Luqman wisdom. BE grateful to Allah!!. Now what's the difference between the two?. When your mom tells you. DO YOUR HOMEWORK!. Is it a suggestion?. Is it a request?. Or is it a command?. It's a command!. Allah. after granting Luqman wisdom. he's not suggesting to him to be grateful. He is commanding him to be grateful. Which means Luqman understood.  that being grateful is obligatory. It is not something that is just nice to do. it is not something you do once in a while. It's not something you kinda sorta should do. He realized this is something he ABSOLUTELY must do. That is captured grammatically inside  أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ. In other words. at the end of his life. At the end of all of life's experiences that Luqman had. He realized just one thing. That BEING GRATEFUL. IS THE ULTIMATE WISDOM. Gratitude IS the ultimate wisdom. SubhanAllah!.

You will find people in life. who have a LOT of knowledge about the Quran. But even though they have knowledge. they don't ACT upon it. which means they don't have wisdom. You can be super knowledgable. but still not be wise. And what lies at the heart of wisdom, is gratitude. So the idea is. the more knowledgable we get in this religion. the more wise we're supposed to get by acting upon that knowledge. And the wiser we get. the more Grateful we should become to Allah (Azza Wa Jal). That is the purpose of the Quran.

Then the ayah continues. 
وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ
The one who is grateful. is only . actually . truly grateful for himself. For his own benefit. If you are being grateful. who is it that you are benefitting?.  You!. You are becoming a more happier person. You're becoming a more satisfied person. You're making the most of what you have in your life. You're not constantly looking at what you did not get or what you do not have. Or what you could have had. You are actually taking advantage of what you actually DO have. The glass is never half-empty for you. it is always half full for you. In other words. being grateful. in a sense is now the same as being positive. And by being positive you are only helping yourself. you are only improving the quality of your own life.
There are numerous TED talks about the stuff today. That how becoming grateful and satisfied for what you do have. tremendously increases the quality of your life. You will lead a more happier fulfilling life. They are discovering all of this now. and everyone is like this is such an EPIC discovery. and the Quran is stating this 1400 years ago. Listen! if you are going to be grateful it is only going to help you.

This BTW. is one of the first and foremost things about beliving in Allah. Belief in Allah. is not just talking about our belief in his existence. Or a belief in someone with divine powers who does everything. who created the universe. who created us. who is controlling all things. That is not enough. That is just the knowledge surrounding belief. The fruit or the result of belief. is us developing certain kinds of attitudes. And the first attitude that the Quran talks about. is gratitude. We become someone who develop a positive outlook in life. We become appreciative. We always see value in the things around you. even in bad situations.

Hazrat Luqman's master. he was a very rich man. And he respected hazrat Luqman so much. that he treated him as a great friend and a companion. to the point. that he made it a practice. that whenever he had something special to eat, he would first feed Hazrat Luqman from it. and THEN eat the leftover. Is that crazy or what?. But you know what we learn from this?. Wisdom is such an amazing thing. that it can turn a slave into a master. and a master into a slave. Where on earth would you see a master. who would eat from his slaves leftovers?. But this is the kind of love and respect. hazrat Luqman generated in the heart of his master. simply through his wisdom.
Anyway. one day during watermelon season. someone gave his master a watermelon. He calls Luqman (AS). and then he slices the melon. and starts offering hazrat Luqman one slice after another. Luqman starts eating the slices with great pleasure. and as he's eating them he's expressing his gratitude to his master and singing his praises. The more he praised his master. the more his master gave to Luqman. Why is that?. In life. when you are grateful. when you are appreciative of someone. does that increase their affection towards you or reduce it?. It obviously increases it right?. When we are grateful to Allah for his gifts. when we are appreciative of Allah's gifts. will that increase his affection for us or decrease it?. Even though this is the story of a slave. hazrat luqman and his master. it contains a wealth of wisdom for us. about our relationship as slaves with our master.
Anyway. so the master is handing hazrat luqman the slices. and as he's eating them. he's praising his master and expressing his gratitude to him. Which in turn makes the master so happy that he keeps handing Luqman (AS) one slice after another. Finally when there is one slice left. his master thinks. Let me also try one slice of this delicious melon. So he takes a bite from that last slice. That slice was SO horribly bitter. that his master almost choked. Some narrations say that he passed out. When he gained back his senses he asked Luqman. How have you been eating these slices with such a smile on your face. praising me and expressing gratitude all this time?. This thing is more bitter than poison!!.
Hazrat Luqman replies. Oh generous master. from your hands I have received hundreds of beautiful gifts. The burden of your gratitude upon me breaks my back. So I felt ashamed. that the hand that granted me the sweetness of so many favors. if one day. some bitterness should come, how could I turn away from it?. O master!. the pleasure of knowing that it comes from your hands. changed the bitterness of the melon to sweetness!”. SubhanAllah! . You see. THIS. is true gratitude!!!.

At every single moment of our lives. we are surrounded by Allah's blessings. But when one thing doesn't go our way. we turn on our master. So Allah says. We gave Luqman wisdom. It is Allah who gave Luqman wisdom. He did not acquire it himself. Allah gave it to him. And then he commanded him.  أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ. Be grateful to Allah!.

Ingratitude


وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ
The one who is grateful. is only being grateful for himself. The true ESSENCE of belief. is gratitude. And by the way. guess what the opposite of gratitude is. in Arabic?. In English it is ingratitude.  Do you know what the opposite of Shukr is? . Its very interesting. It's Kufr. What is another meaning for that word Kufr?. Disbelief. So to the arabs. disbelief AND ingratitude. are one and the same thing. There's no difference between the two for them. Someone who is not grateful. he might as well not even be a believer. Why?. Because the first thing that happens as a result of you being a believer. is that you become grateful. you become positive. And this is why the first words of the Quran in Surah AlFateh are what?. Alhamdulillah. If we don't learn this one lesson. we haven't learnt anything from the Quran. We really need to internalize this. And then Allah continues and says.

وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ
And whoever is ungrateful. then certainly Allah is free of all need. and he is praised in and of himself. Now this is a very powerful statement made by Allah. So let's try to understand what he saying here. Allah is saying he does not NEED you to be grateful to him. In fact he does not need you for anything. People asked this silly question. Why does Allah need me to be grateful anyway?. Why does he constantly need my gratitude?. ACTUALLY. he needs ABSOLUTELY nothing from you. because he is غنی . غنی mean someone who is completely independent. who has no need of anyone and anything. In fact the only one who does actually have a need. is us!. We dont' thank him for every breadth. but he still provides it . We don't thank him for every single heartbeat. but he still allows it. We dont' thank him for every blood vessel that is filling up with blood. but he's still doing it for us. The fact that we are able see and blink. the fact that we are not overwhelmed with pain in every pore of our skin. ALL of that is from Allah.
And despite the fact that we not necessarily grateful to him. nor do we constatnly express our gratitude to him . but he still provides these things for us . So the fact of the matter is. if there is anyone who deserves gratitude. it's him. And no matter how much we think we pray to him. how much we try to carry out our religious duties. in the grand scheme of things. we CANNOT TRULY EVERY thank him. So we can't think . even for a second . that we have in fact done the job of thanking Allah. because that is not EVER going to be the case. We are NEVER EVER going to be able to thank Allah for what he does for us. Allah says.

وَآتَىٰكُم مِّن كُلِّ مَا سَأَلْتُمُوهُ.  وَإِن تَعُدُّوا۟ نِعْمَتَ ٱللَّهِ. لَا تُحْصُوهَآ
We give you everything that you ask of us. And if you were to try to fully understand. fully appreciate. even a single blessing of Allah. you will not be able to do so . You won't be able to fully grasp it . or fully appreciate it. it's just not humanly possible.
إِنَّ ٱلْإِنسَنَ لَظَلُومٌۭ كَفَّارٌۭ
No doubt about it. human beings are truly unjust. and extremely ungrateful.

Allah is saying. you can't even thank me properly. or thank me completely. for ONE SINGLE favor I have done for you. The favors that you actually see and experience. You can't even be TRULY grateful for that. So then what about.
وَأَسْبَغَ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعَمَهُۥ ظَهِرَةًۭ وَبَاطِنَةًۭ
Allah has unleashed his favors upon you. the ones that are obvious to you. and also the ones that you don't even see. There are so many unseen ways in which Allah is helping us. that we don't even realize. There are ways in which Allah is protecting us in our sleep. We are walking down the street. and around us are insects. that contain deadly toxins. One bite from them could kill us. They're carring deadly viruses and disease. and they buzz right by us by Allahs command. And they bite someone else and they die. and we dont'. And this was not something that was under OUR control. If that was decreed for us. there is nothing we could have done about it . So we don't even know the ways in which Allah is protecting us. He says in the Quran.
وَيُرْسِلُ عَلَيْكُمْ حَفَظَةً
We sent down guardian angels upon you. He literally put angels. that are on full time duty. just to watch upon you. just to take care of you. You're driving your car. perfectly fine. within the speed limit. within your lane.  and there is a drunk driver right next to you. and he can smash into you at anytime. out of no fault of yours. but Allahs angels are protecting you .  We can't even think of the ways in which Allah is protecting us. He's providing for us. He's doing us these constant favors we don't even know anything about. We create delusions of home security. job security. social security. All of which can crumble in a moment. We have seen it happen. All of this is simply a delusion of security. Allah is the one who is truly keeping us safe. So Allah says.
وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ
He does not need you . because he is ghanee. He is self-sufficient. In fact. YOU are the ones who need him. Then he adds the word Hameed. Hameed is somone who is praised. and who is shown appreciation. ALL on his own. In other words. he does not need YOU to show praise and appreciation to him. If no one in the entire world would praise him and show appreciation to him. he would still be worthy of praise. And he would still be worthy of gratitude. If Allah created absolutely nothing. If there were no human beings. no animals. no plants . If there was NOTHING at all in this world . Allah would still be worthy of praise. He would still be worthy of appreciation. He does not need creation to show him gratitude. The only thing OUR gratitude does. is INCREASE his favors upon us. which is simply a part of his justice. Because that's what justice dictates. Give MORE to the appreciative. Give MORE to the grateful. In school. you show appreciation to your teachers. they will automatically try to teach you more. Because you're showing that you appreciate and value what they're doing for you. It'll make them happy to do more for you. But not because they HAVE to!!. They don't. It's ONLY your gratitude. and your appreciation that is attracting their favors more.

Anjum apa once told me that she was teaching her students about how magnets attract metals. And she said that got her thinking. that Allah's justice must be like that. that if you contain certain qualities. certain metals within you. it will automatically be attracted to the magnet which are his blessings. I thought that was a REALLY beautiful example. Gratitude is that metal within us. that attracts Allah's favors. The more gratitude we have. the more strongly we will attract his blessings. Which means that if I feel I am not seeing his favors in my life. then what's missing?. My gratitude is missing.

Now what is gratitude?. We need to understand what gratitude or shukar is. There are two meanings in the statement. أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ . The first is. Be grateful TO Allah. And the second is. Be grateful THROUGH the intermediaries of Allah. I'll say that again. Be grateful TO Allah. And the second is be grateful BECAUSE of Allah. or be grateful FOR THE SAKE of Allah.

definition of lubb
So let's begin by talking about Gratitude TO Allah. in the context of the ulilAlbaab. people of sound essence. Once again. Lubb. the singular form of Albaab. is the kernel inside a nut. or the seed inside a fruit. And because a seed is always PROTECTED and covered from all sides. it's essence remains pure. It does not get influenced by external factors. In other words it maintains its original pure state. That's why UlilAlbaab. are called people of sound essence. because they have protected their hearts from statanic influences. and so they have been able to preserve their original purity. But that also implies. that they started off with some basic purity.right?.

You guys play video games right?. If you've played any RPG type games. Role playing games. The character always begins with some basic capabilities. He can walk. He can jump. He can kick . punch. but these are not at its maximum level yet. It's at a very basic level. And then as he progresses through the game. he posesses additional powers. new equipments. new weapons.  attack combos etc. So now he can jump higher. run faster.  have a three punch combo etc. And then eventurally you can buy. in-app upgrades. and synch everything up to 100%.  and now your character is like fully awesome. Now it's exactly what you always wanted it to be. right?
But when you started the game. your character is kinda weak. but there are still some basic capabilities your character poseses. in order for you to be able to play the game. you understand?  I'm sorry girls. I haven't played any princess games. so I can't make reference to those.


Fitrah
So according to Islam. EVERY ONE of us.  ALL human beings are created with some basic pre-programmed spiritual capabilities within the Ruh. the soul!. It's called Fitrah. It's those basic capabilities we're all created with in this game of life. That's why Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) said.
مَا مِنْ مَوْلُودٍ إِلَّا يُولَدُ عَلَى الْفِطْرَةِ .
There is not a single child. that is not born upon this pure state "Fitrah",
فَأَبَوَاهُ يُهَوِّدَانِهِ وَيُنَصِّرَانِهِ وَيُمَجِّسَانِهِ
You-havvi-danihi. wa Yu-nassi-raanihi . wa Yu-majji-saanihi
It is then his parents (i.e. external influences) that make him a Jew, Christian or a Zoroastrian. But the original state of a child is pure. You smile at a child. and it will smile back at you. You look at it in anger. and it will start crying. A child never lies. It'll just look at you in the eyes. smile and say. YOU FAT!. You do something nice for the child. it doesn't even know how to say thank you yet. but it'll hug you. or give you a toothless smile. or lick your face. or do something nice.  Because they're all. WE ARE ALL born with this innate capacity to be a decent person. Decency is not something you are upgraded into. Gratitude is not a power you download later. Kindness is not an inapp purchase you have to make later. These are abilities that every human being is born with. This is the stance that Islam takes with the first creation. See Christianity doesn't believe that. They believe that every human being is born in sin. But we Muslims believe. that the starting point of every human being is good. no matter what family or religion they're born into.

And so one of the fundamental proofs of having a sound essence. is that when something nice is done to you. For example. if I do something nice for you. or if you do something nice for me. At the very least what should I do?. I should be grateful to you. I should have that basic decency in me. to say Thank you. I should not require an upgrade for that!. right?. When someone does something nice for us. is kind to us. feeds us.  does us a favor. gives us gifts. we just naturally become grateful to that person.  and we thank him. So gratitude is from those fundamental emotions we are born with.
Another one is. that when we see something beautiful. when we see something amazing. like a beautiful waterfall. or a breadth taking view. when someone shows us something magnificent. we appreciate it. we praise it.  So gratitude and praise. these are from that basic decency that Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) created us all with.

This is how we saw. that when these people of sound hearts and sound minds. the ulilAlbaab. when they reflects on the creations of the heavens and earth. they become aware of the existence of their Rabb. And they become aware of his ownership and his authority over them. They witness how their Rabb is nurturing them. maintaining them. putting them to their purpose. And how everything within themselves. and outside of them. are designed as ENORMOUS gifts and blessing. from their master. So they accept him as RABB. and in doing so. they submit themselves to him. as his obedient SLAVES.

Taking blessings for granted
Now in the previous session I told you. that this act of submission. as slaves. is actually an EXTREMELY difficult task. That's why I said. The greatest challenge. that you and I are constantly going to face in life. every waking moment. is accepting that Allah is Rabb and that WE. ARE HIS SLAVES. It's not easy. Especially not in these times that we live in. and especially not for you kids. Why is that?. Because of the amount of luxury and convenience that we all enjoy today. There's no blame here. It's not a bad thing that you have luxuries and comforts. AlHamdulillah for that. I'm simply acknolwedging the fact.  that YES. It IS really very difficult in this day and age for us to TRULY submit ourselves as SLAVES. And that's because we are all surrounded in comforts. And when a master surrounds his slaves in comforts. It's REALLY easy for us to FORGET what?. That we are still slaves.
We have a lot of what we want. at the tip of our fingers. Literally. We can order things online. We can download things. We have the devices to do so. We have the constant connections to do so. And we have all become used to this kind of convenience. We're all slaves of instant gratifications for MOST things in our lives. When we want something. we want it now. And the problem is. MOST of the time. we even get it right now. And so to not have it is just becomes unthinkable. Look at us and phones. and this necessity to constantly be online.  We're literally enslaved to it. For us to spend one hour without internet. it's devestating. As a matter of fact. If I asked all of you kids to turn your phones off right now. some of you would literally go crazy. What?. Turn my phone off?. Are you nuts Asif mamu?. It's bad enough that my parents make me sit for an hour and listen to you. and now I can't even use my phone?. Oh I hate you so much. right?

And you know why this is a problem?. We have become so used to getting things. whenever we want them. that we start believing that we are actually entitled to them. We believe that we actually DESERVE everything that we have. So in moments when these gifts are given to us. it's feel like no big deal. WHATEVER!!!.  Today we live in a world. where our hearts are afflicted with this disease called. "WHATEVER". Your parents says to you. Look how much I love you and how much I do for you. I take care of you. I feed you. I buy you everything you need. And your response is. WHATEVER!. Your response should have been gratitude. but instead it's. WHATEVER!. Why?. Because you feel. so what if you do all this for me. It's NO big deal. You're supposed to do this for me. therefore. WHATEVER. 
Your friend shows you this amazing project he's been working on. This AMAZINGLY INSANELY INCREDIBLE gizmo he puts together. Hey dude! Check this out. What do you think?. You look at it and say what?. WHATEVER Dude! It's Ayee. Best Buy has a better version of that. Who cares!. The correct response should have been praise. considering the effort and design he put into it. but that would be SO NOT COOL to do. isn't it?. Your COOL FACTOR would take a plunge if GOD FORBID you said. WOW! That's awesome!.

So we are surrounded with SO many comforts. and in most cases we don't even need to lift a finger for it. It is done FOR US. CONSTANTLY. that we start thinking we're entitled to it. I DESERVE It. And we start believing we OWN things. This BELONGS to ME. We have developed this idea of MY STUFF. It's MY stuff. and I'm not going to share it with anyone. Because it is my stuff. Why you touching my stuff. Don't touch my stuff. It's mine. Mine Mine Mine. ma mine ma mine ma mine. You guys literally turn into that bird in  finding Nemo. Mineee Minee Minee. 30:30

This is us today. But the thing about these people of sound essence is. they don't believe that they own ANYTHING. They understand that they do not actually posess anything. WHY?. Because they are SLAVES. and slaves don't OWN anything. An not just that they don't own anything. they themselves ARE OWNED by their master. This realization. is what truly makes them grateful. Because they understand. that everything that they own. is not actually ownership. it is temporary posession. that has been granted to them by their Rabb.

So then who owns all of it?. The one that gave them existence. right?. These people of sound essence realize. that in the TRUE sense. they don't OWN or DESERVE anything. Because they are SLAVES. يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ كُلُوا۟ مِن طَيِّبَتِ مَا رَزَقْنَكُمْ

Complaint is the litmus test of ingratitude
Now if you want to truly test this concept. of whether you believe you're a slave or not. the litmus test for that. is to catch yourself complaining. Scholars say. COMPLAIN. is the PROOF of ingratitude. It is the physical evidence of ingratitude. I'm not talking about complain when someone is hurting you. or bullying you. or if you have pain in your arm or something. I'm not talking about that. I'm talking about complains we have. related to posessions. or desires. you understand the difference?. If someone his hurting you. and you inform your parents about it. that's not a complaint. That's just you being smart.

The complaints I'm talking about. are related to posessions and desires. That stem from ingratitude. and they're of two types.
The first is the complaint. when you don't get something you want.
and the second is the complaint. when the thing . that you have. that you're complaining about. is not good enough to you. X2

When you complain about something you did not get. you believe that somehow you deserved that thing. you believe you were entitled to it. Like for example. when you study hard and you do really well on the exam and your professor still gives you a C. You complain. Because you believe you deserved an A. But then when your parents are not buying you that THING. that you want. and you complain. you somehow think you're entitled to it. or that your parents somehow OWE you that. which is not actually true. They don't owe you anything. Everything they do for you is out of their love. their care. their concern and their mercy for you. And if they DO actually owe anyone. they OWE Allah. not you!. Because Allah has made them a Rabb over you. But they don't directly owe you anything!. That's the first type of complain.

The second complain is when you get something. you already posess something. and it's not good enough for you. I mean how obnoxious is that!. If someone gives you a gift and you complain about it?.  Lets say.  I buy my daughter a violin for her birthday. because I know she's been wanting it for a while. So I save up my money. and I get the one I can afford for her. Now she takes it in her hand. looks at it. and tells me. Babu. You know.  there is a better version of this in ths store. Is that obnoxious?.  Yes! Its unacceptable. and if she did that. what would I do with that gift?.  If I handed her the violin and she said. you know there is a better version. what would I naturally do?. I'd take it away. And if you know me at all. I'll not only take away the violen. I'll take away ALL the others things I've given to her as well. Because I'm sure there is a better version of all those gifts out there too. And when I do that. she'll be like. NOOO I didn't mean it. Hahaha.
But seriously. we human beings. we don't appreciate the gifts that we have. UNTIL they are taken away. Kids have so many complaints against their parents. sisters have complaints against brothers. brothers complain again sisters. A kid goes to school. someone asks him. Hey! tell me about your mom. . OH MAN!. She's such a pain in my butt. She's ALWAYS on my case. ALWAYS nagging me about homework. about my chores. She's ALWAYS yelling at me. Always bugging me about my prayers. I can't wait to turn 18 and leave this freaking house. I'm SO sick and tired of her. But then. god forbid something happens. and Allah takes away his mother. At that point you ask him the same question. He'll say. I had the PERFECT mom. She loved me so much. She always took care of me. She always made sure I was fed. She never let me go to bed hungry. She would wash my clothes. iron them and folded them for me. She made my bed everyday for me. When I fell sick she would constantly check up on me. She took SUCH amazing care of me. I MISS HER SO MUCH!.
What happened?. What changed?. Just yesterday you couldn't stop complaining about her!. What happened to you today?.

So be grateful to Allah for the parents you have. You don't OWN them. Allah OWNS them. Just like he owns YOU. And one day. the OWNER WILL take back what belongs to him. And on that day you will ONLY be able to remember how good she was to you. If you want to be among the wise. Be grateful NOW.
Same goes for parents. I have never EVER heard a parent complain about their dead child. I have NEVER heard a parent say. My son was iressponsible. he never completed his homework. never did his chores. he always argued with me. NEVER!. They only say one thing. MY SON WAS PERFECT. My brother was perfect. My sister was perfect. APPRECIATE the people you have in your life today. before you lose them.

Because NOTHING lasts forever in this world. THAT is the ESSENCE of wisdom.  Let's summarize what we talked about today. Wisdom means. to have knowledge. and then to act upon it. And the climax of all wisdom is. . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ . Be grateful to Allah!. The ultimate wisdom. is being grateful to Allah. THAT is ULTIMATE wisdom. Because ONLY the wise realizes. that being created. being given existence. is Allah's ULTIMATE gift.

وَٱللَّهُ أَخْرَجَكُم مِّنۢ بُطُونِ أُمَّهَتِكُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ شَيْـًۭٔا
And Allah has extracted you from the wombs of your mothers not knowing a thing. That's our original state. complete ignorance. right? And then what?.
وَجَعَلَ لَكُمُ ٱلسَّمْعَ وَٱلْأَبْصَرَ وَٱلْأَفْـِٔدَةَ ۙ
and He made for you hearing and vision and intellect. These are the three primary gifts. by which we acquire knowledge. By seeing and hearing things. and using our intellects. So that we can study the عالَم. and become عالِم . to understand the علیم?. Without these gifts. could we have a decent life in this world?. Absolutely not!. So Allah created us ignorant. He created us in an UNGRATEFUL state.  and then gave us 3 gifts. hearing.sight. and intellect. to help get us out of our ignornace. to help us move towards wisdom. And why did he do that?.
لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ
that perhaps you would be grateful. And he said .لَعَلَّكُمْ . MAYBE. Why maybe?. Because he knew that human beings are an ungrateful creation. And so we need to move towards gratitude. And gratitude is something that needs to be cultivated. It's a muscle that needs to be developed. And how do we do that?. By realizing that WE are SLAVES. We are slaves that do not deserve ANYTHING. We do not actually OWN anything. Everything and Everyone we have in life. these are all TEMPORARY posessions. They're all as temporary as our lives itself. These are all GIFTS and BLESSINGS. from our gracious and generous Rabb. who will take it back one day. انا للہ . No doubt about it. we belong to Allah. We are his posessions. و انا الیہ راجعون. And no doubt about it. we will one day return to him. One day the owner will take back his posessions. See. ingratitude happens. when we believe things are permanent. But if everything is temporary. the ONLY logical conclusion is to enjoy them while they last. and be grateful to the one who gave them.

An urdu poet says.

سدا نہ باغی بلبل بولے، سدا نہ باغ بہاراں

سدا نہ قائم حسن و جوانی، سدا نہ صحبت یاراں

This nightingale will not sing in this garden forever. nor will the beauty of this garden last forever
Beauty and youth do not last forever. nor does the company of the beloved last forever.

So be grateful to Allah while you have these things.

In the previous session we looked at the meaning of the word wisdom. and how the ancient arabs defined it. They looked at is as having beneficial knowledge and acting upon it. And the essence of that wisdom. that was being taught to Hazrat Luqman was. وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ . We granted Luqman wisdom. For that what should you do?.  أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ.  Be grateful to Allah. Allah is teaching us. that gratitude is the essence. it is the pinnacle of wisdom.

And this gratitude. this ability to praise something good. to appreciate good things. it stems from a basic decency that Allah created us all with. Gratitude is not something we learn in life. It's already there. There are people who lose this basic decency. and are no longer grateful for anything in life. They become completely selfish. They start thinking that all the good things that come to them. are purely because of their own efforts. They deserve the things they have. They are entitled to everything they have. They don't need to thank anyone for anything. They don't owe anyone anything. They are completely independent. To such people. this message will make ABSOLUTELY NO sense. You need to feel gratitude for the favors that are being done to you. AND.  you also have to have the ability to appreciate the design and the value of things. If someone doesn't have these two things. they're in the wrong place.

Because this is how the Quran begins its conversation.  It begins with the introduction of Allah. بسم اللہ. and then the very first attribute it mentions is his love. his care. his concern and his mercy. الرحمن الرحیم. That he is intensely merciful. consistently merciful. Because only the one who LOVES. who cares. who has genuine concern and who has mercy. ONLY someone with these attributes can be Rabb. Because only a Rabb can nurture, nourish, maintain, shower gifts. and elevate the one being nurtured. the marboob. from their present state to a higher state. Only a Rabb can do that. And that is why what immediately follows that introduction. is the idea of being grateful. الحمد للہ رب العلمین. Praise and gratitude to the Rabb AlAlameen.  It's THAT simple. It's that straight forward.

Then we learnt. that TRUE gratitude is cultivated in the soil of servitiude. In realizing and seeing ourselves. as who we REALLY are. That Allah is our Rabb. and we are his SLAVES. So that is one of the first things that sets this master apart. Not only did he provide his slaves with what was required. He went way above and beyond in his gifts.

Islam is not for ungrateful people

Lions eat deer. and they just rip through it. They don't stop and say. hmmm. This could use a little bit of. rabbit topping. Or maybe a turle on the side would be nice. It doesn't need to dip the cockroach in chocolate first. It'll just eat it. no problem.
Human beigns however. Allah gave us these strange taste buds didn't he?. So you have certain fruits you like. and then some you don't quite like. Some of us have a sweet tooth. We like sweet things. certain kinds of chocolate you love.  and certain you don't. There are certain restaurants you're obsessed with. there others you can't stand. I don't like that place. OOOOH that was gooood.!  We didn't have to do that.

So this master. he did not just give us life. he made life beautiful for us. This is something to be appreciated. This is something to be grateful for. Different kind of slavery

Is it for the masters benefit. or for the slaves benefit?. ALWAYS for the master's benefit. Isn't that true?. But is our slavery for the benefit of Allah?. Does he have a need for us?. Does he actually need our prayers?. Our efforts?. Our gratitude?. NO
وَمَن يَشْكُرْ . فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ
The one who is grateful. is only . truly being grateful for himself. He is ONLY benefitting himself.

وَمَن كَفَرَ . فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ
And whoever is ungrateful. then certainly Allah is free of all need. and he is praised in and of himself. This master has ABSOLUTELY NO need of slaves. He does not need our slavery. Also who pays money to buy a slave?. Every slave has a price, right?. Even in the old days. a MASTER would have to go to their local store. Slaves R Us. and PURCHASE a slave. right?. Every other slavery of the world. the master purchases the slave. But this عبودیۃ  to Allah(Azza Wa Jal). we desire it. we work hard for it. we strive for it. WE pay the price to become his slave. He doesn't hold a gun to our head.
لَآ إِكْرَاهَ فِى ٱلدِّينِ ۖ قَد تَّبَيَّنَ ٱلرُّشْدُ مِنَ ٱلْغَىِّ

So he thought. Let me humiliate Qambar publicly today. So he calls maulana Qambar out in the market. in front of everyone. He says. Ya Qambar! انت عبداً؟. Oh Qambar! Aren't you a slave?. Because slavery is considered a dishonor. an insult right?. So he says to Qambar. Aren't you a slave?.
So Maulana Qambar turns to this man. and he replies. Indeed I am a slave. But do you not know whose slave I am?. And then he starts reciting this praise of Maulana Ali. OMG. It's SO incredible. I can't even. Just the beauty of those words. He goes on and on and on.

أنا مُوَلِّى من ضرب بسیفین . و طعن برمحین . وصلى القبلتین . وبایع البیعتین . وهاجر الهجرتین . ولم یکفر بالله طرفة عین. 
أنا مُوَلِّى صالح المؤمنین . ووارث النبیین . وخیر الوصیین . وأکبر المسلمین . ویعسوب المؤمنین . ونور المجاهدین . ورئیس البکائین . وزَین العابدین.  وسراج الماضین . وضوء القائمین . وأفضل القانتین . ولسانِ رسولُ رَّبِّ العالمین . وأَوَّلُ الوصیین من آل یس . والمؤید بجبرئیل الامین . و المنصور بمیکائیل المتین . المحمود عند أهل السماء أجمعین . والمحامی عن حُرُمِ المسلمین . والمجاهدُ أعدائُہُ النَّاصبین .وأمینِهِ على المخلوقین . وخلیفةُ مَن بعث إلیها أجمعین . سید السابقین . وقاتل الناکثینَ والقاسطین . ومَبیَدِ المشرکین . وسَهمُ مِن مَرامِ اللهِ على المنافقین

World operates based on Rububiyyah

Now let's return to Hamd. which means gratitude and praise. I told you there are two types of hamd. There is gratitude to Allah. which we talked about last time. And there is gratitude to the intermediaries of Allah. that I want to talk about today.

If you look at how our physical world operates. you will find EVERY single thing in nature. operating under the blanket of Rububiyyah. If you keep those 6 definitions of the word Rabb in mind. you'll see rububiyyah in action all around you. The heavens have been made a Rabb over the earth. It nurtures it. provides it with rain. It brings the dead earth back to life.
ٱعْلَمُوٓا۟ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يُحْىِ ٱلْأَرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا
Know that Allah gives life to the dead earth.
So the sky or the heavens is a Rabb over the earth. which means the solar system. We know this earth is surviving. because of the rububiyyah of the solar system. Anything goes wrong with their rububiyyah. and game over for us. right?. Then the earth is a Rabb for all living things. It provides them with food and water. it provides nourishment for the survival of all species. Then in our day to day lives. you'll find rububiyyah. in every organized system there is.  Take your schooling for instance. There is a board of education. that is a Rabb over these various levels of Primary education, middle school, high school, college. right?. Then each one of these act as a rabb. individually over the teachers. Teachers are Rabb over students. Parents are rabb over kids. Doctors are rabb over patients. Governments are rabb over the country. CEO and board members are Rabb over their corporations. right?. So we see that this world operates under the blanket of rububiyyah. That's the first thing. The next thing to understand is. that rububiyyah. works through intermediaries. which are the cause and effects. required to get the job done. OK?. So two things to understand. First. Rububiyyah is a process. designed to provide a systematic. and progressive benefit to the marboob.  And the second is. that the process of rububiyyah is executed THROUGH various intermediaries. to get the job done.

Gratitude to intermediaries


Let's look at the example of a farmer. to understand this better. A farmer in classical Arabic. is a perfect example of a Rabb. Because he is responsible for cultivating his land. and growing crops. So he holds ownership of that land.  has authority over it. he nurtures the plants. maintains them. waters them. He protects them from bugs and animals. He does everything implied by the definitions of the word Rabb. So the farmer is the Rabb of his crops. But does he actually GROW the plant?. Does he make the plant tear out of the seed?. Does he actually pull out its roots. and spread it in the ground?. Does he shove his hand in the dirt. grab the plant by its neck. and then stretch it into a tree. NO!. He does none of those things.
The way he executes his rububiyyah. is by delegating these responsibilities. to certain intermediaries. which are the elements of nature. The soil, the water, the sunlight, the darkness. He controls them. and they in turn. fulfill their jobs of raising the plant. Does that make sense?. The farmer makes sure the soil has the right temprature. He makes sure water is provided in the right amounts. and at the right time. He makes sure enough sunlight is  provided. but not so much that it burns and kills the plant. He makes sure he uses the right fertilizer for the right kind of plant.  you understand?. So the farmer. as the ULTIMATE Rabb. is executing his rububiyyah. not directly. but THROUGH these intermediaries. He doesn't interact with the plant at all. Who does he interact with?. Who does he influence?. Who does he work on?. the intermediaries. which are the soil. the water. the sunlight. the minerals. They are the ones doing all the work. under his guidance. But intentionally speaking. who is it that the farmer want to benefit?. The plant, right?. His goal is the development of the plant. He is working on EVERYTHING else. so that the plan could receive the benefit.

Now the question is. these plants. these crops. Who should they be grateful to?. Should they be grateful to the farmer?. or should they be grateful to the intermediaries?. Let's think about it.  Granted that these intermediaries. soil. sunlight. water. minerals. fertitilizer. no doubt they have the potential. and the ability to make the plant grow. But was that potential enough without the farmers design and control?. Let's say the farmer.  just dumped the seeds in the ground. stamped on it a few times. and walked away. Now the soil is still there. the water is still there. sunlight is still available. But would all these things. make the plant grow?. NO. Of course not. Even though they all have the potential. the capabilities to make plants grow. but without the design and the control of the farmer. none of these intermediaries would be able to benefit the plant. Correct?. OK. Fair enough. The plant owes gratitude to the farmer for its growth and survival. But then would that growth have been possible. if the intermediaries did not do all the hard work that they did FOR the plant?. Had they not slaved for the plant day in and day out. week after week. month after month. would the plant be able to grow?. ABSOLUTELY NOT. Hmmm. the plot thickens. Who does the plant be grateful to now?.
What we're learning here is. that even though the plant owes its gratitude. its hamd. ultimately to the farmer. justice dictates. that it's not possible to be grateful to the farmer. without FIRST being grateful to the intermediaries. the asbaab. the wasaayel. that the farmer put in place for the plant. Because the PLANT is dealing with these intermediaries. NOT. the farmer directly. So it needs to FIRST be grateful to the intermediaries. And what does that mean?. What would be the gratitude of the plant?. To accept and submit TO the intermediaries. SO THAT they could benefit it. There is a relationship there right?. The intermediaries are now the master. and a master needs an ABD. to complete the relationship. So the plant needs to complete the relationship by submitting to these intermediaries. ALLOWING them to benefit it. That would be the plants gratitude to the intermediaries. and THAT would be the plants gratitude to the farmer.

Listen to this carefully. For this plant metahphore. The plant can ONLY be grateful to the farmer. by begin grateful to the intermediaries. The plants gratitude to the intermediaries. The plant submitting TO the intermediaries. allowing the farmer to do what he intendes to do. IS its gratitude to the farmer.

BE GRATEFUL TO THE INTERMEDIARIES. IN ORDER TO BE GRATEFUL TO THE RABB.

Chain of gratitude
Now let's look at an example closer to hom. For us human beings. when it comes to Rububiyyah. the closest thing we have. in the seen realm. right in front of us. is our parents. So now as decent human beings. we realize that our parents. ESPECIALY our mothers have done an enormous amount of good for us. So basic human decency dictates. that we be grateful to our moms. Not as a muslim. just as a basic decent human being. Why?. Because she almost died giving you birth. She almost killed herself. so that you and I could be alive. That's a pretty big deal. You and I wouldn't be breathing right now. if our mother's didn't bleed for us. That's just a fact. So basic decency dictates that we be grateful to our parents especially our mothers.

Now when I say. I REALLY want to thank my mom. I TRULY want to be grateful to my mom. I realize. that my mom wasn't opening up her stomach and putting spoons of food in my mouth.  Some automatic thing was happening inside my mom that when she ate food. I was getting fed. It was all automatically getting taken care of. for me inside her. There was a predictable. systematic design of cause and effect that was taking place within my mothers womb. which was feeding me. developing me and allowing me to grow. And all of that was through the noursihment coming to me from my mom. Which means that if my mom didn't eat. I would not have been fed. right?

This means that in order to TRULY be grateful. I have to now also be grateful to the one who was feeding her. so that I could be fed. Mabye she didnt have the means to earn money at that time. Maybe it was my dad who was making the money. that bought the groceries. which fed her. which in turn fed me. So maybe I should thank my dad who was providing the food for us both. So now I don't just want to thank my mom. but also my dad for making that living. But then I think about my dad and mom. and I realize that my dad wouldn't earn this living. if he hadn't received a good eductation. which probably my grand parents got him. Because it is that education. that led him to earn a living. so that my mom could eat. so that I could get food. You see what I'm doing here?. So now I realize that I need to be grateful to my grandparents as well. on both sides. for the food I'm getting in my mothers womb. you understand?.  But then I realize that my grand parents only exist. because their parents existed and raised them. who then raised my parents . etc.  So now maybe I should not only thank my parents. but also my grand parents and their parents . and their parents. and so on. Because IF all of that didn't happen. I wouldn't be having this meal in my mothers tummy. you understand?

When you really start thinking about THANKING someone. and I mean TRULY feeling grateful for someone. does it end with the person you are about to thank?.  Cause they could not have done what they did for you. if someone else didn't do something for them. And if you go further back. someone who did something for them. someone ELSE must have done something for them. and you keep going back. And if you are TRULY TRUYLY grateful. then you realize. This all had to start somewhere. It all had to start somewhere. and that's how you reach who?.  You reach Allah!!.  I am grateful for being born of my parents. who are grateful for being born of their parents. who are then grateful of being born of their parents. And it keeps going back till you get to the first parent. which is adam and hawwa (Alayhim AlSalaam). who were grateful for being created. by. Allah.  So it all goes back to Allah.

When I was inside the fetus. which was my ENTIRE world. my ENTIRE universe. Inside that world. I was being taken care by a process of rububiyyah. executing through cause and effects. which was designed by Allah. Now that I'm outside the fetus. in the real world. I am still being taken care of. by the same design. by the same process of rububiyyah. executing through cause and effects. So when you think about TRUE gratitude. it's not just gratitude to the person right in front of you. it's also for all the cause and effects put into place. so that this benefit could reach you. And when you truly reflect and traverse that chain back. the one you find. HOLDING this rope. is Allah (Azza Wa Jal) . This is in the physical sense. The physical rububiyyah.

Now let's talk about spiritual rububiyyah. I am grateful to my teacher.  my spiritual Rabb. Javeed bhai. who taught me everything I know today. I am truly grateful to him. Because I owe my spritual existence to him. But I cannot be truly grateful to him. until I am grateful to his teachers who taught him. why?.  Because had they not taught him. I would have remained ignorant. So in a sense. Allah put him through all of his training. so that he could train me. So now if I want to be TRULY grateful to him. I must also be grateful to his teachers and their teachers and their teachers and so on. And if I go back all the way. where will I eventually reach?. I am grateful to my teacher. Javeed bhai. who learnt from and is greatful to manaseeb. who learnt from and are grateful to Duaat. who learnt from and are grateful to Aimma. who learnt from and are grateful to Maulana Ali AS. the source of all true knowledge. And when I get there. who do I find Maulan Ali grateful to?. انا عبدٌ من عبید محمد. He is grateful to Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). who is grateful to. Jibraeel AS. is then grateful to. Allah(Azza Wa Jal). Once again. even at the spiritual level. the buck stops with Allah. You understand?. This is why Allah says in the Quran.
أُو۟لَٓئِكَ ٱلَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ. يَبْتَغُونَ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمُ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ
Those whom they call upon. they too seek MEANS. Intermediaries. to access their Rabb
أَيُّهُمْ أَقْرَبُ
Each one of them closer to their master. Closer in what?.
وَيَرْجُونَ رَحْمَتَهُۥ وَيَخَافُونَ عَذَابَهُ
In their hope for His mercy.  and they fear of His punishment.

This is why in every dua that we recite. we mention the names of Rasul Allah. Maulana Ali. Aimma Tahireen. BEFORE we begin our conversation with Allah. Why is that?. Why can't we just directly pray to Allah. Why do we have to place these individuals in between us and Allah?.We have to do that. because Allah HIMSELF placed these intermediaries in between. We came to know of Allah. THROUGH their rububiyyah. And so now justice dictates. that we have to be grateful to them first. we have to honor them first. We have to do what they ask us to do FIRST. And then we have to use them. as waseela. as means. to approach Allah.

يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ ٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَٱبْتَغُوٓا۟ إِلَيْهِ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ
O you who have believed. fear Allah and seek the INTERMEDIARIES to approach Him. Don't just directly come to Allah. come to Allah THROUGH his means. through his intermediaries. What does this mean?. If its gratitude. BE grateful to them FIRST in order to be grateful to Allah. Obey them FIRST. in order to Obey Allah. LOVE them FIRST. in order to love Allah. Acknowledge them. honor them. APPRECIATE them first. in order to acknowledge and glorify Allah.  وَٱبْتَغُوٓا۟ إِلَيْهِ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ. These intermediaries are the milestones for us on the path to Allah. This is where the training of gratitude begins. And the VERY FIRST milestone for us. are parents.

This is why. the Quran's argument is not that you just have to find a creator.  No No No. That comes much much later. The Quran's argument is. Don't you want to be grateful?.  Aren't you a decent person?. Isn't gratitude something I built inside of you. And if you ARE a decent person. and you DO want to be grateful. Be grateful to the Rabb right in front of you. the one who exists in the seen realm. Because if you're not going to be grateful to your parents. your immediate Rabb. How are you going to be grateful to me?. If you can't see your parents as Rabb. How will you EVER be able to see me as Rabb????. Because Rububiyyah. just like anything and everything else in the world. is a progression. It's a training. You want to be TRULY grateful?. Be grateful to you parents. Be gratefuly to your grand parents. Be grateful to your teachers. Be grateful to your teachers teachers. Be grateful to the Imams. Be grateful to Maulana Ali. Be greateful to Rasul Allah. Because being grateful to ALL OF THEM. will be your gratitude to your ultimate Rabb. 

Interpreation of drinking water
See. I'll tell you something. What are the ettiquettes of drinking water?. We muslims. following the teachings of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . when we drink water. we hold the glass in our right hand. and then we sit and drink the water. right?. Now why is that?. It is to honor. to show gratitude. to the greatest blessing there is for human life. which is water. It is the ULTIMATE blessing for all living things. We would DIE without water. An arrogant person doesn't even think about this. But a true ABD. an obedient ABD. he remembers and appreciates this fact. every single time he has a drink. The fact that had his master not provided him with water. and made it SO accessible for him. he would not be able to survive. So how does he show gratitude to his master for that blessing?. He makes himself humble before Allah FOR that blessing. And he displays that humility IN ACTION. by lowering himself before it. By sitting down and drinking it.
But then this slave ALSO realizes that he would not be able to drink the water. unless it was not confined in a glass. Of course.  he could dunk his face in the sink and drink like an animal. But to be able to drink in a civilized.  honorable way. he needs to use a glass or a cup. Now is WATER the real blessing of Allah. or is the glass the real blessing of Allah?. Obviously it's the WATER!. The glass is just a means. an intermediary. to a goal. which is to drink the water.
But look. Our prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) in his vast wisdom. he made it compulsory to pay respect to the glass as well. And this is why we hold it in our RIGHT hand and not our left hand. to honor it. to express our gratitude to it. Because we Muslims. we use our right hand ONLY for honorable things. and we use our left hand for foul things. So  Rasul Allah made it obligatory. that when you drink water. hold the glass in your RIGHT hand. to show gratitude to the glass. to honor it!!!. Now notice which honor comes first?. Do you hold the glass first?. or do you drink the water first?. You hold the glass first. So you have to honor. and show gratitude to the means. to the INTERMEDIARY. BEFORE you can show gratitude to the blessing. Isn't that interesting?. Even though the real blessing is the water. you have to honor the glass first. And then you have to lower youself before the glass. and elevate it. in order to drink from it. I want you all to think about this action of drinking water. You've already lowered yourself. humbled yourself before Allah's blessing. You've honored the glass by holding it in your right hand. But that's not enough. As you're drinking the water. you are continuously ELEVATING the glass. Because you HAVE to elevate the glass to drink more water. isn't that the case?. Its not possible to drink more. if you don't keep lifting the glass up. The MORE blessings you want. the MORE you MUST elevate and honor the glass. the intermediary. SubhanAllah! . This entire structure of gratitude is placed as a reminder. for every single time we drink a glass of water.  AllahuAkbar. There is NOT a single thing in our religion. not a single hadees. not a single action. commanded by our beloved prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) that is not filled with immensely beautiful.  and profound meanings. SubhanAllah!

Parents are immediate intermediaries
So what I want you to understand. is that your parents are the glass.  through which you are enjoying the blessings of Allah. You have to honor them first. you have to be grateful to them continuoulsy. IN ORDER to be grateful to Allah. Because parents are the FIRST of all the intermediaries. between us and Allah.  He says in the same surah Luqman.
وَوَصَّيْنَا ٱلْإِنسَنَ بِوَلِدَيْهِ
And We have made it obligatory upon man to care for his parents.
حَمَلَتْهُ أُمُّهُۥ وَهْنًا عَلَىٰ وَهْنٍۢ وَفِصَلُهُۥ فِى عَامَيْنِ
His mother carried him. which increased her in weakness upon weakness, and his weaning is in two years.
أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ إِلَىَّ ٱلْمَصِيرُ
Be grateful to Me and to your parents. To Me is your final destination.

أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ. Be grateful to Me and your parents. This is SO beautiful. If you notice. Allah joined the twe extreme ends together. He says be grateful to ME. Allah is the furthest link. ALL the way at the other end. And he joins it with . وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ . and to your parents. who are the closest link to me. Notice when he talks about gratitude he mentions himself. but he doesn't use the word shukar again for parents. He doesn't say.
أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَ اشکر وَلِدَيْكَ
Be grateful to me and be grateful to your parents. No he only uses the word shukr ONCE. with himself. . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ. Be grateful to me AND your parents?. Why?. Because being grateful TO your parents.  is a PART of your gratitude to me. You can't be grateful to me if you're not grateful to your parents.

We were brought into this world by Allah. But in the seen world.  in the seen sense. we were brought into this world by our parents.  Allah provides all of our food and sustenance. but in the physical sense. who did Allah make the means to provide us with food? Our parents. Allah protects us. but who has he given that responsibility to in the physical sense? To our parents. You know today. when you are older and you get scared. you say. اعوذ بالله. but when you were a child. and you got scared.  when a two year old get scared. what does he say?.  mama.  mama. They do that or not?. Because everything that Allah is to us in the grand scheme of things. when we are a child. we don't see Allah. we don't even understand the concept of Allah.  the only thing we understand is what?.  mama. parents. SubnhanAllah. Allah clothes us. but in the physical sense our parents  clothe us.  Allah teaches us. علم الانسان مالم يعلم. He taught the human being what he did not know. علمہ البیان. He taught the human being how to speak. but technically who teaches us how to speak?  our parents.
In other words. ALL of what Allah did for us.  he did it for us. through our parents. The most important entity for a child is its parents. Their refuge is the parents. Their source of love is parents. Protection is parents. Provision is parents . EVERYTHING that you can think of later on with Allah.  in the beginning of your life.  as a child. its your parents. Parents are GREATEST GIFTS and BLESSINGS of Allah. Because they are doing the WORK of Allah. that he wants done for us. Parents are actually the ambassador of Allah in raising you.  They are Allah's ambassadors. They represent him. They represent his work. And do you know what Allah's goal is for you and me?. You know what he's using parents for?. To make us RABB. That's what a parent is doing. They're nurturing you to elevate you from the status of Murabbee. and turn you into a Rabb. How?. So that your SOUL now becomes the Rabb of your body. They elevate you from the pathetic. helpless state of a child. to an elevated intellectual state. of a Rabb. Look at a child. the parent needs to make all the decision FOR it. From that state. your parents got you to the state. where you are now able to handle your own Rububiyyah. If you honestly reflect on it. that's no small task. that's not a small favor. That's an INCREDIBLE favor. And if you are a decent person. if you haven't lost that decency that Allah created you with. you will feel immense gratitude for your parents.

Because if you don't feel gratitude for them. you'll never get to the next stage. You won't be able to be grateful to the spiritual parents. who are going to now raise you. from this pathetic. and helpless state of mortal physicality. to the glorious and immortal state of spirituality. If you can't be grateful to your parents. you'll never be grateful to your teachers. and you'll never be grateful to Rasul Allah. and you'll never be grateful to Allah. Becuase it's all a chain of command. This is why he says.
وَٱعْتَصِمُوا۟ بِحَبْلِ ٱللَّهِ
Hold strongly to the rope of Allah. وعتصمو. comes from. عصم. which means. You know that sport of bull riding?. When you're on the bull and you're holding that rope. and the bull is trying to throw you off. How would you hold that rope?. What kind of a grip would you have to maintain?. A REALLY strong one right?. That kind of a hold is called عصم. Allah says.  وَٱعْتَصِمُوا۟ بِحَبْلِ ٱللَّهِ. Hold tightly to the rope of Allah. What is this rope of Allah?. It is these intermediaries between us and Allah. Imagine this. Imagine a rope is hanging down from the heaven. and its coming all the way down to you. Now you have to climb this rope all the way to heaven. How will you do it?. You'll grab what's closest to you with one hand, right?. And then where will your other hand go?. Directly to Allah?. No. You'll grab the rope right above your other hand. Isn't that how you climb a rope?. So what does this mean?. You'll grab the first intermediary. which is your physical parents. and that intermediary will nurture you. life you. help elevate you. from your current rank. to the next higher rank of knowledge. which are your spiritual parents. And then your spiritual parent. will lift you to the next parent. until you reach the final parents. There is a hadees of Rasul ALlah.
انا و انت یا علی. ابوین المومنین.
Oh Ali. You and I are the parents of all believers. But if you can't love your physical parents. you'll never be able to love your spiritual parents. It's just a natural fact. If your relationship is not good with your parents. then I guarantee you that your relationship is not good with Allah. You can see this for yourself. And so the ONLY way to rectify your relationship with Allah. is to rectify your relationship with your parents.




 





Definition of Hamd


OK. so we're talking gratitude. Hamd. which means two things. It means gratitude and it means praise. Let's start by defining these two things. and understanding how they are related?. Gratitude and priase are emotions. that are generated in the heart. when one realizes that an undeserved gift. or an unearned benefit has been provided by a benefactor. In other words. when someone does something nice for you. you feel this emotion of love in your heart. for two things. Love for the person providing the benefit. and love for the gift itself. You understand?. Love for the person who gave you the gift. and love for the gift itself. The love for the gift is experienced as praise. And the love for the giver is experienced as gratitude. I'll give you an example.

Your dad buys you. your brand new dream car.  and hes dangling the keys before you. What do you feel?. For you dad. Oh Thank you thank you thank you. you're the BEST dad ever. I love you so much. I can't believe you did this for me. Thank you dad. Thank you. So for your dad. you feel gratitude. And when you look at the car. checking out the leather interior. the shiny rims. you go. WOW!. This thing is DOPE. This thing is freaking AWESOME. So for the car. for the gift. you feel praise. You understand?. So gratitude towards your dad. and priase for the car.
Now does your dad just hand you the keys to your new car?. NO. Obviously not. You know there is a lecture that comes with that. You know it. Dads going to say. Listen. you need to stop at stop signs. You need to stay under the speed limit.  You have to not be out after 9pm.  you need to. you need to. you need to. Hes not gong to give you a 1000 things. He'll most likely give you 10. He'll say here are the 5 things I don't want you do.  And here are the 5 things I DO want' you to do. Keep it clean. Make sure you change the oil. etc. etc. He'll say. Listen. You din't buy this car. I did. and I'm giving it to you. Its hard earned money that I worked for. that I am using . to buy this car for you. You absolutely have no share in this. You do not deserve this car. You did not earn this car. I am not asking you to pay me for it. The only reason Im giving it to you. is because I love you. But in return. all I expect from you. all I ask of you. are these 10 things. please don't do them. And BTW. these 10 things I'm telling you. are for your own safety. Obeying me doesn't benefit me. it benefits you. Please don't speed. you'll get a ticket. Please don't crash into a tree. you'll get hurt. I don't care about the car. I care about you. For the car I have insurance. Please don't let your friend drive the car. right?. So he sets these few rules for you. Is that fair?. With undeserved gifts. comes responsibilities. Because the gifts are being given to you for a reason. And you can fulfill that reason. or you can ignore them. You understand?

Allah has given us numerous UNDESERVED gifts. Allah says I'll give you 5 fingers on each hand. use them wisely!.  I'll give you 2 nosrills. I'll give you functioning lungs. Ill give you a heart that beats. I'll give you 2 legs. all the toes on every leg. I'll give you a stomach that works. I'll give you a chest. I'll give you bones. bones that don't break upon contact. You know there are people who have very brittle bones by the way. they could break very easily. Just a regular hand shake can break the bones in their hand. Allah gave us eyes. ears. hands. feet. But with these gifts came responsibilities.

So hamd. in the truest sense. is appreciating the value of the gift. when you appreciate the value of a gift and the benefit it provides. what generates in the heart is PRAISE for the gift. and that praise moves out of the heart. and comes onto the tongue and it is articulated. in the form of . AlHamdulillah. and SubhanAllah. That is the hamd of the heart and the tongue. And there is the hamd of the jawarih. of the body parts. In other words the gratitude and praise does not just remain confined to the heart and the tongue. it then moves to the limbs. and they get busy in the execution of the purpose they were given for. In other words. it is not simply lip service. it's not just on the tongue. it actually becomes manifest in the actions of the human being. and this is why. شکر نعمت العین….  خِفضُ البَصَر. The eye itself is a blessing. and the gratitude for the eye.  the way we thank Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for the blessing of the eye. is to lower it from the forbidden. We do not look at the things that Allah has prohibited to see. The gratitude for the blessing of hearing is to not listen to the forbidden. the gheebah. gossip. backbiting. Because of the Day of Judgment the hands and the eyes will bear  witness.  against the human being. 
بَلِ ٱلْإِنسَنُ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِۦ بَصِيرَةٌۭ . . وَلَوْ أَلْقَىٰ مَعَاذِيرَهُۥ ‎
The human being knows what he's up to.  even if he starts giving excuses.  This is why the arabs say. 
العُزرُ اَقبَح مِنَ الذَّنب
The excuse is uglier than the wrong action. Because we all have excuses. Life is just filled with excuses. And so HAMD. is the manifestation of the praise and the gratitude. within action. and this is why the Prophet said. 
لا الہ الا اللہ المفتاح الجنۃ……. وَلِکُلِّ مِفتَاح اثنان.
La Ilaha Illa Allah is the key to jannah….  but then he said. Every key has teeth.  you have to have the locksmith fill in the teeth so that it can fit the lock. And the teeth of La Ilaha Illa Allah  is acting according to it.  it is entering into the circle of the people of La Ilaha Illa Allah. Because it is a circle…. And when you bind yourself within a circle…. You are leaving everything that is outside the circle…. So entereing the circle of La Ilaha Illa Allah …. Means leaving all bad stuff outside…. This is TRUE gratitude.

This is why we find every creation that Allah created in a state of constant gratitude. What does that mean?. Does that mean they're saying Thank you all the time?. NO. It means they're DOING what they were created for. They are fulfilling their responsibilities.
أَلَمْ تَرَ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يُسَبِّحُ لَهُۥ مَن فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ
Do you not see that Allah is praised by whomever is within the heavens and the earth. This is true praise. doing what you were created to do. The sun is in a state of hamd. the moon. the solar systems. the galaxies. animals. birds. plants. minerals. EVERYTHING is in a state of hamd. Everything is doing what it is supposed to do. This is the ESSENCE of Hamd. Isn't this also the meaning of wisdom?. To gain knowledge and then act upon it?. This is why Allah said. We gave Luqman wisdom. Be grateful to Allah. Because they're both connected in meaning.

and us being grateful to my parents is indirectly as being grateful to Allah.  Allah provides us from the unseen.  Allah protect us from the unseen.  physically I got the check in the mail or deposit in the bank.  but we know as part of our faith.  who is actually paying you?.   Allah is.  but that is in the unseen you cannot physically see it.  and you cannot trace the deposit at bank transfer directly back to Allah.  but what the parents did for you is that in the unseen or is that something that you can see and experience.  that you physically carry you in her stomach. did she physically deliver you  . . did she physically feed you. did your father physically raise you. they did. that is not some matter of faith. that you have to believe it even though you haven't seen it. you've experienced it for yourself. if you can't even be grateful for what you experience in the seen world. how can you be expected to be grateful to Allah who does everything for you from the unseen world. that doesn't make any sense. that is why Allah mentioned the parents first.

AlRehman and AlRaheem.

Now you can say. if its these intermediary Arbaab doing all the work. then its the intermediaries and not the Rabb
So now if I ask you. who does the plant owe gratitude to?. it obviously owes gratitude to the farmer. but how?. by being grateful to the intermediaries. By accepting and submitting to the rububiyyah. the training. the nurturing.  of these elements. they are in fact. expressing their gratitude to the farmer.  You understand?. Their gratitude to the farmer will ONLY be expressed. by their doing. what they're SUPPOSED to be do. Because if they don't do that. Let's say the roots refuse to absorb the water and the minerals. the leaves refuse to absorb sunlight. What will be the result?. The plant is not going to grow and develop. which is going to waste the ENTIRE effort. and the ENTIRE plan of the farmer. isn't it?.


Now does the plant see the farmer?. Does it know anything about the farmer?. Does it know the farmer is its true Rabb?. NO!. Who is the Rabb from the plants point of view?. The soil. right?. The soil. the water. the sunlight. the fertilizer. the minerals from the earth. All of these things are making it grow. The plant has absolutely NO knowledge of the farmer. what farmer?. To the plant. the natural elements. that are a series of cause and effects. that's what is making it grow. What the plant then fails to see. is the design. the planning. and the control.  that is being executed during each and every stage of its nourishment.
So now the question is. who does the plant owe gratitude to?. Obviously it owes gratitude to the natural elements. soil water sunlight etc. Because they are the immediate benefactors for the plants.
