But who does the plant. in the TRUEST sense. owes its gratitude to. obviously to the farmer. Why?. Because even though the causes and their effects. like soil. sunlight. water. Even though these intermediaries. they have the potential to make the plant grow. it was whose design and control. working behind the scenes. that ACTUALLY made it grow?. The farmer. If the farmer put the seeds in the ground and just walked away. The soil is still there. the water is still present in the world. sunlight is still available to the world. But would all these things. make the plant grow?. Of course not. Even though they all have the potential. the capabilities to make plants grow. but without the farmer. none of these causes would have mattered. Correct?. So the plant owes two types of gratitude. First to the immediate causes. the intermediaries in the seen realm. which are the sunlight. soil. fertilizer. water. etc. But then more importantly. to the designer. and the controller of those intermediaries. working behind the scenes. in the unseen realm. who is the farmer. You understand?



 

In the last couple of sessions. we looked at praise and gratitude for Allah. and praise and gratitude to the intermediaries of Allah. and how they're both connected. Today I want to attempt to explain this often confusing topic. of why does Allah needs praise and gratitude?. In the previous session. someone asked. It seems like Allah doesn't need us at all.  and he created us just for worship. So then. if he does not need. us and we didn't really need to exist. nor did we ask for it. So then why even create human beings. It seems like Allah could have saved himself and everyone a lot of trouble. And its a valid question because we do come across such contradictions in the Quran. One one hand the Quran tells us that Allah is LOFTY. He is so majestic. He has the ultimate power. He's able to do anything and everything. He is absolute and complete in himself.
قل ھو اللہ احد. اللہ الصمد
He is unique and absolute. He doesn't need anyone or anything.
الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ
Everything in the heavens and the earth sings his praise and is grateful to him. and not just today.

وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ
Even in the future and the after life all praise and gratitude will belong to him.
يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ أَنتُمُ ٱلْفُقَرَآءُ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ
Oh people. You are the ones who needs Allah. and Allah has no need of you.
وَٱللَّهُ هُوَ ٱلْغَنِىُّ ٱلْحَمِيدُ
Allah is praised in and of himself. He does not need your praise. nor does he need your gratitude. All these ayats indicate that he is a master. completely disconnected from his creation. because he is too great. Which is fine. Fair enough. I can understand that. I mean I don't expect the president of the united states to be interested in what I'm having for dinner. So I get it.

But then there are also ayats in the Quran. in which he clearly asks us us to praise him and be grateful to him.
وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلّهِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ وَلَدًا وَلَم يَكُن لَّهُ شَرِيكٌ فِي الْمُلْكِ
and say: "All praise and gratitude is for Allah. who didn't take a son. and has no partner in His dominion
وَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ.  سَيُرِيكُمْ آيَاتِهِ فَتَعْرِفُونَهَا
And say: “All praise and gratitude is for Allah. He will soon show you his signs and you will see that he is your master.

Wait. I thought you said you don't need us. you're too majestic. too lofty to need us. We are the ones who need you. But now you're saying.  you DO want me to be grateful?. You DO want me to praise you?. Why?. You don't need it. Besides. everything else in the heavens and earth are already praising you. and is grateful to you. so then why do you need MY praise and graitutude. Doesn't seem like you have a shortage of that. What difference does it make to you whether I praise you or not. And then on top of that he says.
وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ
I did not create jinn and man except for my worship. So which one is it?. You love me or you don't love?. If you love me how come you don't need me?. If you don't need me. then how can you love me?. And not just love me. but love me like a mother loves her child in her womb. It doesn't add up right?.

Understanding how Allah does not need us
Now why are these questions so important to us?. Well. it's important. because to love. and be loved. is a VERY VERY important thing for us human beings. Right from our birth. I mean think about it. Why are we attracted to Allah more by love. instead of punishment?. The Quran talks about both. and both methodologies do work. But we naturally want to gravitate towards Allah. through the emotion of love. and not fear. Isn't it?. Because love is a really important thing to us. So when we hear things like Allah does not need us. cause everything else is praising him. what happens. is that we listen to that message with our human ears. and we then confuse it with our own experiences of rejections. and end up responding in the same way. It's like someone saying. I have SO many friends. I have so many people that love me. I really don't care if you're my friend or not. I really don't care if you love me or not. right?. And when we hear this. we naturally get hurt. and we say. FINE!. WHATEVER. Go get your praise and gratitude from THEM. نعوذ باللہ.

Yes it is an egotistic response. but then we are egocentric creatures.

So I'll try to explain this concept to you with an example. But first I wanna reiterate something about examples and anologies when it comes to Allah. This is one of those topics that make me REALLY nervous. because I'm talking about MY master. that I know I have. neither the capacity. nor the capability to talk him. But then to understand things. all we have is examples. All we have is.  شئی. Things. And if you look at the word شئی . it is the masdar.  it is the verbal noun of . شَاءَ ، یَشَاءُ،شَئیً. In other words. it is Allah's مَشیئا. his will. that brought forth the اشیاء into existence. Every THING. ever CREATION. is a manifestation of his divine will. That's why its called شئی. because it represents Allahs مشیئا. his will. This is what the Arabs called analogies. تقریبٌ الافھام . means of nearness or closeness in understanding. This is why. 
َضرب اللہ مثل
Even Allah strikes examples for us in the Quran. See. a مثال . or an example. is an analogical symbol for something that we know. which can help us understand something that we do not know. If you already understand something. then using that example. a person can explain to you something. that you don't know. And you say. Ahhh I got it!. it's LIKE. this. right? . But when it comes to allah.
لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِۦ شَىْءٌۭ
There is no شئی. There is NO THING. LIKE him. Not in essence. not in attributes. So its always a challenge to explain divine relationship through creation. Therefore we have to keep in mind. that even though we use human emotions and experiences. to understand a relationship with Allah. we cannot reduce Allah. down to the level of our human emotions and exeperiences. He is too exalted for that. OK?. These examples and anlogies are just a tool to help us get an idea. It's no where close to the real relationship or experience with Allah. When it comes to Allah. things get amplified and intensified. beyond our imginations.  We always have to keep that in mind.

Understanding "Need"

So now what does Allah mean when he says. he does not need us. The word NEED. in the context of these ayaats. it have to do with existence. and it has to do with survival. So when Allah says. that he does not NEED us. what he's saying. is that his existence. his essence and his attributes. His Zaat and his Sifaat. they are not dependent on us. His omnipotence. His being ever living. His being glorious. kind. forgiving. His being an Ilah. they are not dependent on OUR existence.

But that does NOT mean. that he does not care about us. or he does not love us. There is a BIG difference here.

I'll give you an example. AlHamdulillah I have two kids. and I LOVE my kids. (most of the time).  I love them. I care about them. I am ALWAYS concerned about them. I am always merciful in my interactions with them. But I do not NEED them for MY survival and MY physical existence. even in the biological sense. See the need to procreate. to have a legacy. to have love. those are all benefits of procreation and having a family. But they are not a necessity. Not having kids. is not a threat to my own existence or survival. If I don't have a child. I'm not going to die.  It may be a threat to my future. My name. my legacy will not continue. But it's not a direct threat to my own existence or survival. In other words. in order to exist. I don't NEED my kids AT ALL. in both the physical as well as spiritual sense. You understand?. I NEED oxygen to survive. I NEED food to survive. I NEED water to survive. I need a beating heart. a functional brain to survive. But KIDS. as AWESOME as it is to have them AlHamdulillah. I technically do not NEED them for my existence. There are people who never have children. as a conscious choice. and they live a good happy life. There are people who WANT children. but can't have them. They too live and survive. There are people who have children. and then معاذ اللہ. they lose them. and even though they miss them every moment. they still survive. They still live out their entire lives. You understand my point?

So when Allah says.
يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ أَنتُمُ ٱلْفُقَرَآءُ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ. وَٱللَّهُ هُوَ ٱلْغَنِىُّ ٱلْحَمِيدُ
People you are the ones who need me. I don't need you. what Allah means is. My existence. my essence and my attributes. are NOT dependent on your existence. You are dependent on me for your existence and surivival. both physically and spiritually. I don't need you to survive. You need ME to survive. Just as I don't need my kids to exist and survive. My kids need ME to exist and survive.
But not needing. is NOT the same. as not caring. Its not the same as not loving. I don't NEED my children. but I DO love my children. INTENSELY. I DO care about them. A LOT!. You understand?. When Allah says he does not need my praise and my gratitude. what it means is. him being someone worthy of hamd. is not dependent on my action of Hamd. He is praised and will continue to be praised regardless. But that in no way means. that he does not LOVE my praise. That my gratitude does NOT make him happy. It doesn't mean all my efforts go wasted. or unappreciated. ABSOLUTELY NOT. He LOVES my praise. He loves my gratitude. In fact he appreciates it LIKE NOBODY else can appreciate it. BUT. he does not need it. Hope you understand the context now.

And the reason he emphasises this in the Quran. is because ONLY the one who does not NEED love. CAN TRULY love. I'll say that again. ONLY the one who does not NEED love. CAN truly love.

See. there are three levels of love. There is the love. where I NEED to BE loved. I need somebody ELSE to love me. Then there is my NEED. TO love somone else. As human beings. we don't just NEED love. we also NEED. TO love. But notice the word "NEED" in both sentences. I NEED to BE loved. I NEED TO love someone. And both these NEEDS are selfish in nature. It's not BAD that we have these needs. It's just part of our genetic makeup. But the thing with love that is diven by NEED is. that as long as the NEED exists. the love will exist. When my need for love gets fulfilled. or I find someone else who can love me. the one I was attached to previously. will no longer hold value for me. Similarly when my NEED of loving someone or something is fulfilled. the one I love. will no longer hold value. This is why marriages break apart. This is why lovers breakup. friends fall out. This is why we get bored of the last toy we once loved. Because that NEED of the self is gone. You understand?.

But then there is a third level of love which is love itself. There is no NEED for love here. It is simply PURE LOVE. FREE from all needs. Allah does not have a NEED to BE loved. Allah does not have a NEED TO love. Allah IS love itself. He is Samad. absolute. in each and every one of his attributes.  And ONLY the one who IS love. who is FREE. of the NEED to love. WILL love continuously. constantly. and unconditionally. you understand?. Because Allah is free of ALL NEEDS to love us. And he is free of all OUR needs to love him back. This is why Allah LOVES no matter what.
You know sometimes we feel. rather Shaytan whispers to us. How can Allah keep forgiving you for the same act over and over again. You make tawba. then you break it. You make tawba again. you break it again. How many times do you think he'll keep forgiving you?. Or you've done such a HORRIBLE act. You've wasted your entire life. Now its too late. You're DONE!. You're DOOMED. When we think like this. look what we're doing. We're reducing the forgiveness of Allah. down to the levels of human forgiveness. Because we will not keep forgiving over and over again. We will not forgive a HUGE trangression. But because Allah is free from all needs to forgive. Because he is absolute in his forgiveness. He will forgive in an instant. No matter what you did. No matter how many times you did it. No matter how big the sin. IF you SINCERELY repent. He WILL forgive. He has no problems. The ONLY condition is SINCERITY of heart. TRUE repentence. And part of TRUE repentence. is not committing the crime again. walking away from it. If we keep committing the same sin over and over again. then we are not sincere in our repentence. But forgiving is not a problem for him at all.

So the concept of TRUE love in Islam. is a love that is FREE of all needs. In fact. this is also the definition of true Ibaadah. The kind that is free of all needs and attachments. It is purely based on LOVE. and that stems from the purity of HAMD. A deep sense of appreciation and gratitude for his blessings. This is why Maulana Ali would say in his prayers.
یا الہی. ما عَبَدتُک بِشَوق جَنَّتِک. ولا مِن خَوف نَّارِکَ. بَل وَجَدتُّ مُستَحِقًّا لِعِبَادَۃ فَعَبَدتُکَ
Oh Allah. I do not worship you because I desire your heavens. nor do I worship you because I am afraid of the hellfire. I have found you TRULY worthy of my worship. and for THAT reason alone. I worship you. THIS is true Ibadah. free of the need of jannah. free of the need of protection from fire. A deep sense of appreciating and gratitude.

And Allah has given a fraction of this selfless love. as a symbol. to mothers. Even the worst child in the world. his mother can never stop loving him. She can be extremely unhappy with him. she can be disgusted by his actions. She may never want to see his face again. But she can NEVER stop loving him. She can never stop praying for him?. Now if a mother cannot stop loving her child. that she ONLY gave birth to. Do you think Allah can stop loving you and me. who created us with his own hands?. Sure Allah gets angry. Allah gets super angry and he punishes with SEVERE punishments. but that is to establish justice. which we'll talk about later. But not out of hatered. not out of vengence. There is a different context for that.

Messenger of Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) was once going somewhere with a bunch of companions. and on the way. he saw a woman sitting under the shade of a tree. gently feeding her infant. He looked at the sahaba and asked. Do you think this mother. would want to. or be OK. with throwing her baby in the fire?. They all said. No Rasul Allah. It's unthinkable that she would ever want to do that. So the messenger said. then how can Allah want that?. How can the one who holds 70 times more love for his creation. than this mother holds for her child. how can he want to throw his creation in hellfire?.

So that's the first thing. We have to separate the word NEED. from the word LOVE and CARE in our minds. These are two completely separate things. Allah does not need me. but he still loves me. and cares about me. He does not NEED my praise and gratitude. but he LOVES to hear my praise for him. and he loves to see my gratitude. OK?

Why Allah cares about praise and gratitude?
Now the next question is WHY does he care about praise and gratitude?. OK fine. I can understand that he does not need me. but he still loves me. and he cares about me. because I am his creation. And there is not a single creator. who does not love his creation. So I get that. But why does he care about my praise and gratitude. If he loves me unconditionally. why do I need to praise him and be grateful to him?. He should love me anyway. Right?.

Now let's talk about that.

I'll give you an example to share with you how "I" understand this. but hopefully you'll connect this. with your own experiences InshaAllah. Because we now understand. that everything in life is an ayah. every thing. every experience. every interaction. every emotion. They're all ayaats. They're all meaningful. they're all valuable. they're all signs that points to something else. They're all in the SEEN realm. to teaches us something about the UNSEEN realm. right?

So I was thinking about my interactions and my experience with Affifa khala when I visit Pakistan. And you can think about your moms for this example.
Most of you might know my Afifa khala and Dilawar chacha are on these sessions. I've noticed that whenever they find out I'm planning a trip to KHI. Even before my plane lands. they start doing these things for me. They make sure the fridge is stocked up with ALL the things that I like to eat. Khala knows I love these kachoris and cutlets and certain kinds of sweets. So she'll have them prepared in advance. and then freeze them for me. She'll think about the kinds of foods I like to eat. the restaurants I always wanna go to. She knows the things I will want to buy while I'm there. and so she plans all THAT out. But then she doesn't stop there. She'll even plan for little little things nobody else would even think of. Like if I sleep over at her place. she knows because of jetlag I'll be up in the night. so what if he wakes up and he's hungry. So she leaves snacks in the fridge for me. in case I get hungry during the night. Not just that. she even stocks up on ANTOX and antibiotics for me. in case I get an upset stomach or whatever. She'll plan THAT far ahead for me. And I have not even landed in KHI yet.

Yes. I DO have an AWESOME khala and chacha! AlHamdulillah.

Now the question is. Did she NEED to do that?. If she didn't do that. would it make any difference in HER life?. It would certainly make a difference in my life. I wouldn't enjoy all these benefits of HER hard work. But she has no benefit in doing that?. So why is she doing it?.  I'm not paying her for this. I didn't even ask her to do this for me. And there's no promises of returns or rewards here either. There's no agreement that if you do this for me. I'll do that for you. So she has nothing to benefit by doing all this for me. Quite the opposite. Chacha has to drive in the heat. in horrible traffic. they go from shop to shop. tire themselves out in the process. It's not easy. They actually go through a lot of effort and discomfort. to do these things for me. And there is NO need for that. but they do it anyway?. Why?. There could only be one explanation. Because they love me. They do all of this for me. because they love me. they want to benefit me. they want my trip to be pleasant. they want me to be happy. You mom does things for you. little little things. she does not need to. but she does it anyway because she loves you.

Similarly. we've talked about how Allah did things for us. Things we didn't ask for. Things we didn't work for. Things we didn't pay him for. But he did them anyway. He prepared this world. and all of its pleasures and comforts for us. even before we were born. even before we landed on earth!. Why?. Because he loves us. That's the only possible explanation. Because he loves us. and he loves us INTENESELY. You know linguistically. the word نعمۃ means something smooth and soft. something that slides easily without friction. something pleasing. something enjoyable. something that provides comfort. those are all the images of نعمۃ. Who created نعمۃ?. Allah did. Then he created me with the necessary senses. to ENJOY those blessings?. Would these blessings of the physical world mean anything. if Allah had not given me these 5 senses?. NO. So think about this. Allah created the blessings for me. AND. he gave me the senses to enjoy those blessings. He did both things for me. What did I do?. What did you do?. Nothing. Absolutely nothing!.

Now let's take the example of one single blessing. One single نعمۃ.

Those of you who don't know. Khala makes this KILLER Raan. She makes this roasted Leg of lamb. that is to die for!. IT'S AMAZING. I've never gone to Karachi and not have her make raan for me. But that takes a LOT of effort to cook. Chacha always goes and buys it fresh. Then khala has to marinade it with all these spieces. She tastes the spices to make sure that the combination is just right. make sure its not too spicy. or too salty. Then she has to cook it at the right temprature. There's a lot involved in the process. There's like a whole rububiyyah process that has to take place here. And then she cuts all these millions of things to garnish it. It's a LOT of work. I've seen her do it. But you know what. she does it with a smile. she does it happily. She's not going. Ullo ka pattha. Kya museebat hai. jab aata hai museebat ho jaatee hai. She doesn't do that. Because she loves me. so she does not mind doing ALL that work FOR me. and BTW I do absolutely nothing. Who is going to ultimately enjoy the raan?. Who is going to benefit from it?. I AM. But who does all the hard work preparing it?. She does. Can you buy ready made food in KHI?. Can you buy cooked Raan in Karachi from a restaurant?. Absolutely. So khala could just get it ordered or delivered for me right?. Make her life easy. But no. SHE cooks it for me wih her own hands. Why?. Because she loves me.

Allah is constantly working for us. These cause and effects of nature. someone is controlling them. Nature is not an intelligent entity. As much as it has the capability and the potential to cause things to happen in the world. it has no intelligence of its own. Just as the soil. water. sunlight. fertilizer. may have ALL the potential of growing the plant. but it is the farmer. who is managing these things to enable the plant to grow. So even though he's not directly interacting with the plant. he's controlling the various intermediaries FOR the plant. and the farmer is CONSTANTLY at work. He's constantly conerned about his crops. So is Allah.
يَسْـَٔلُهُۥ مَن فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ
Everything in the heavens and the earth turn to him for their needs.
كُلَّ يَوْمٍ هُوَ فِى شَأْنٍۢ
Every moment he is busy in hard work for them. Why?. because he loves his creation.

OK. so khala prepared this meal. this blessing. this نعمۃ for me. Now come dinner time. when the food is all ready. she doesn't just take the cooking pot off the stove. and dump it in front of me and say. Yeh le khaa. mar. Agayee bhooka America sey. No. She makes this whole BIG DEAL about presentation which I never understand. She'll put it in a nice beautiful tray. Arrange all the garnishings on it.  She'll then make ALL this extra effort to present it in the most beautiful way. Why?. It already looks AMAZING. It already smells amazing. I'll happily eat it right off the pot. Why does she need to decorate it on top of that?. To make it look beautiful. make it look pleasing. For who?. For me.

In the last session I pointed out. Allah gave us sight. but he also gave us the ability see color. black and white would have worked just fine. but he went above and beyond. and gave us color. He could have given us the ability to see just the 7 primary colors. That in itself would have been awesome. But NO. he gave us the ability to see and enjoy every spectrum of color in between.  SubhanAllah!. He went way above and beyond of what was just necessary. He gave us the ability to hear. and he created amazing sounds of nature. the sound of winds. birds chirping. waves of the ocean. sounds of a waterfall. rivers flowing. rain falling. AllahuAkbar.
He didn't give us the ability to feel. until he first created the warmth of the sun. the coolness of the breeze. the sensation of water. the sensation of sand on the beach.
He didn't give us taste. until he made delicious foods for us to enjoy. Just look at fruits. Look at the variety of tastes that exist within fruits. All the way from sweet to sour. and everything in between. The skin of the fruit has its own taste and texture. the meat of the fruit has its own taste and texture. the juice of the fruit has its own taste and texture. To eat one fruit by itself is one taste. to mix it with other fruits. and have a fruit salad is another taste. To have one single fruit juice is one taste. to mix a combination of fruit juices is a different taste. AllahuAkbar. I mean do we ever take the time to reflect on these things? 
فَبِأَىِّ آلَآءِ رَبِّكُمَا تُكَذِّبَانِ
How many blessings of Allah will you then deny?. SubhanAllah! . Allah didn't just give us things. he made them over the top amazing for us.

Now.  imagine I eat this raan. and I say. SubhanAllah Khala. This tastes amazing! Its so good. I love it. you're the BEST!. Did khala NEED that praise?. Is that why she went through ALL of that hard work. so that she could hear me say YOU'RE THE BEST!!!!. NO. But after enjoying that dinner. when I told her. This food tastes amazing. you're the BEST khala. I love you!. did that made her happy?. Yes. It did. Why did it make her happy?.

This is the part I want you to understand. It made her happy. not because I said those words. but because I appreciated. WHY. she did all this for me. She did ALL of this to show me what?. That she loves me. she cares for me. she values me in her life. I am someone special to her. and she showed it to me by slaving over a dish "I" wanted. to make ME happy. to benefit ME. And when I praised her. I didn't JUST see the food. I saw her love behind it. I recognized and appreicated the PURPOSE of her hard work. you understand?
And BECAUSE I appreciated it. because I recognized its VALUE. what did I do?. I dropped whatever I was doing. and I rushed to receive the benefit. to enjoy it. My appreciation of her cooking. motivated me. to benefit from it. And after I ate her cooking. After I enjoyed the benefit of her hardwork. I felt gratitude for her. I felt love for her. my heart drew closer to her. And so what was the next thing I said?. Thank you khala!. Thank you so much for loving me. for caring about me. for doing this for me. Even though you didn't have to. and you didn't need to do this. You did it for me. and I love you for that. THAT is what made her happy. Not just my words of praise. not my eating her food. but my recognizing and appreciating her love. And once I did that. my NATURAL response to her love. was to love her back. This is why Allah asks us in the Quran.
هَلْ جَزَآءُ ٱلْإِحْسَنِ إِلَّا ٱلْإِحْسَنُ ‎
Is the reward of something good. anything BUT good?. Allah asks us in Surah Rehman. Where's my appreciation?. Again. Not because he needs my appreciation. Hope you understand that now!. Not because he NEEDS us to reciprocate. But because he WANTs us to reciprocate. I did so much for you because I love you. Won't you love me back?. Won't you even give me that much?. Isn't the reward of something good. to reciprocate in kind?. هَلْ جَزَآءُ ٱلْإِحْسَنِ إِلَّا ٱلْإِحْسَنُ ‎

Hamd has to be both - Praise and gratitude

Now let's understand why Hamd. is a combination of appreciation and gratitude. Why can't it be one or the other. Lets look at some scenarios. And I'm talking about the rule here. not the exceptions. We'll talk about the exceptions some other time. Let's first just understand the rule. OK?

Khala cooks this delicious raan. and calls me for dinner. I come to the table and I say. Oh khala. this is so AMAZING. this looks SO tasty. OMG you did all of this for me?. You really love me so much!. You are awesome! I love you. BUT. I don't really feel like eating. It's GREAT that you did all this for me. and it DOES look REALLY good. But I'm not going to enjoy it. Do you think that would make her happy?. NO. Why not?. I appreciated her effort and her love didn't I?. I did praise her!!. So whats the problem?. The problem is. I did not benefit from it. I did not eat it. That was the REAL reason she did all the work. isn't it?. She didnt just do all this work. preparing something I LOVE. just so that I can praise it and then NOT eat it. That means. I do not really appreciate what she did for me.

My not taking advanatage of a benefit. is PROOF. that I do not TRULY APPRECIATE it. Because appreciation should lead. to desiring and taking the benefit.

Now let's look at the other side of the coin. Khala calls me for dinner. and I eat the whole thing. I actually do receive the benefit. but then I don't say a single word. I finish the meal. I go. BURRRRP. And then I get up and walk away. How do you think khala feels now?. Would she feel sad?. Would she feel disappointed?. Why?. Can't be because I didn't eat it. Cause I did. I wolfed that bad boy down. So I took the benefit. I PROVED that I appreciate it. Now what's the problem?. The problem is I did not feel gratitude for what she did for me. She did ALL this for ONE single reason. to show me how much she loves me. and I ate her food. I enjoyed all her hardwork. I benefitted from it. yet I failed to feel. or acknowledge. my gratitude towards her. I completely took her for granted. So yes. she would be justified in being disappointed.

So you see. It's not one or the other. It's BOTH. HAMD. is when I appreciate something. benefit from it. and let the benefit drive me to being grateful for it. You miss any part of this. and it's no longer hamd. It's incomplete. its ناقص. its imperfect. defective.

Now what if I repeatedly kept doing this to her?. Everytime I visit her. she keeps making raan for me. And either I don't eat it. or I keep wolfing it all down. and never express a word of gratitude. Eventually what's going to happen?. She'll beat me to death with that same raan. right?. LOL. Proably not. But she'll defintely stop making raan for me?. why?.  For two reasons. Justice and tribulation.
Justice. because I have proven to her. that I'm not worthy of that blessing. Her hard work is getting WASTED on me!. Why?. Because I'm either not appreciating it. or I'm not being grateful for it. and therefore I don't deserve it. And when you give a blessing to someone who doesn't deserve it. you're denying that blessing from the one who DOES deserve it. Someone else could be enjoying and appreciating khala's hard work instead of me. She could be showing her love to someone else. who would then respond back with the same love. right?. That's one reason blessings are withheld.
The second is to cause tribulation. I'm used to khala making raan for me everytime I come to KHI. The first time she refuses to make it for me. I say khala. when are you making raan?. She says. I'm not making it for you anymore. You don't deserve it!. How am I going to feel?. I'll feel pain. I'll feel upset. It'll cause some tribulation, right?.
Trials and tribulations. are wake up calls. It shakes us up. How come Khala?. What did I do wrong?. You've always done this for me. why not now?. It'll force me to think. OMG. I've been unappreciative. She's been doing this for me all this time. and I've been taking her love for granted. IF I'm a person of sound heart and a sound intellect. that's what tribulation is supposed to generate in me. Repentence. On the other hand. if I'm a self involved. conceited. ungrateful jerk. my response will be. FINE!. WHATEVER!. I knew you never loved me to begin with. You're NOT MY khala anymore!. You understand?.

When I constantly and continuously deny and reject Allah's blessings. When despite one blessing after the other. I neither appreciate them. nor do I benefit FROM them. and when I do. I'm never grateful for them. When I keep taking his blessings for granted. He withholds them from me. Why?. The first reason is justice. Because someone ELSE could be benefitting from these blessings that are being wasted on me. And second. MAYBE. just MAYBE. the absence of this blessing now. might make me realize. the errors of my ways. And once I do that. hopefully I will repent. and make an effort to return to him. Now when do you want someone to return to you?. When you love them?.  or when you hate them?. When you love them!. Why?. Because you want to restore that lost blessing back for me. I have to show you I've realized what I've done wrong. apologize. fix my ways. and you'll give me back the blessing you took away. right?.
One of the many reasons. There are many reasons for trials and tribulations which InshaAllah we'll cover in a future session. But one reason is that when someone is ungrateful. unappreciative of Allah's blessings. he puts them through trials and tribuations. So that they can realize what they're doing wrong. fix it. and return back to him. And do you know what the word for returning back in classical Arabic is?. TAWBA. Tawba means. to return. or to retreat. When we move towards haraam. we move away from Allah. When we realize our sin. and quit that haraam. we return back to him. we retreat. That is the meaning of TAWBA. That's what retreat is. When armies retreat. where do they go?. They return back to their homes. back to the source.

This is the philosophy. the design. behind praise and gratitude. Allah doesn't NEED me. but he does LOVE me. And he has manifested his love. physically. through the عالم. Remember what I told you in the session on Alameen.  عالَم is what is known. عالِم. is the one who knows. علیم. is the ABSOLUTE knower which is Allah(Azza Wa Jal). So Allah created the عالَم. so that the عالِم. could recognize the علیم. Recognize what?. His love for his creation. To show. that even though YOU don't contribute in any way shape or form to his existence or his attributes. he still loves you. he cares for you. he's concerned for you. he has mercy for you. He has Rehma. The physical world manifests the love of the Rehman. The spiritual world. manifests the love of the Raheem. Because he is the RABB of both. and that's why. الحمد للہ رب العالمین.

The Rehman created external blessings. The Raheem creates the ability to experience and enjoy those blessings. All that is being asked of us. is to recognize it. and appreciate it. Because appreciation is praise. And praise will create the desire to benefit from that blessing which we appreciated. Think about it. Let's say you see a new phone that your friend just bought. What's the first thing you do?. OH MAN THIS IS SO COOL!. I gotta have one of these. Why do you want it?. Because you appreciated something about it. and now. you want to benefit from it. right?. Would you buy a phone you don't like?. would you buy a car. would you buy a house. would you buy anything you don't like. that you don't appreciate?. Of course not. And when you DO buy it?. What's the purpose of that?. To benefit from it. right?. So all benefit. begins with appreciation.
And so when we benefit from the blessings of Allah. it lead us to the gratitude of Allah. And what happens when we are grateful to Allah?. He increases his blessings on us. Why?. Because we PROVED to him. that we are worthy of his blessings. We're ready for the next level. This is again part of Rububiyyat that we talked about. When a child completes his education in the 4th grade. and passes the exam. What does passing the exam mean?. He appreciated the knowledge that was taught to him. that's why he studied hard in acquiring it. His hard work. is his expression of gratitude for that knowledge. And so what happens next?. He is promoted to the next grade. and the cycle of appreciation begins again at a higher level. If he does not appreciate it what happens?. He fails his exam. and has to repeat the same class right?. or eventually get kicked out of school.
So when an ABD. proves to his master that he has appreciated his masters blessings. and is grateful for it. As a reward. his master gives him a greater blessing. But a greater blessing. obviously requires a greater appreciation. more praise. more gratitude. So we push ourselves further. And as we push ourselves further. he keeps increasing his blessings further. and the cycle goes on and on and on. And the ABD keeps advancing towards the love of his master.

And what is greatest of ALL blessings?. FAITH!. EMAAN. That is the GREATEST blessing of all. Emaan comes from the word. أمن. which means security. It also means peace and tranquility. Because the closer we get to Allah. The closer a ABD gets to his master. the more secure. the more peaceful and the more tranquil he become. And the means. the intermediary. for achieving that closeness. is Ibaadah. Worship. All forms of worship. especially salaah. These are all means of achieving that proximity with Allah.

Now what did Allah say he created us for?.
وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ
And I did not create jinn and human beings. EXCEPT for Ibaadah. Meaning I did not create jinn and human beings. EXCEPT to witness my love. and get closer to me.  SubhanAllah!. This is the true meaning of لِيَعْبُدُونِ . Appreciate my gifts. benefit from it. be grateful for it. express your gratitude through Ibaadah. and get closer to me. And the closer you get to me. I will increase my blessings upon you and you will continuously increase in Emaan. You will become more secure. you will become more peaceful. you will find more tranquility. And the cycle will go on and until. until you come and meet me one day.

Hamd of Allah unlocks his blessings
And this is why Allah loves our hamd. Our praise and gratitude. Not for himself. FOR US. To UNLOCK his blessings. while maintaining justice. The fact that I'm praising khala in today's session. recognizing. acknowledging. appreciating her love for me. Openly declaring. that my khala loves me. And the fact that I do see her love. I AM grateful to her for EVERYTHING she's done for me. How do you think  she's feeling right now?. Is she happy or sad?. I bet you she's happy. Why?. Because I saw. what she wanted to show me all this time. I'll get a bigger better raan the next time. LOL. But think about it. if Khala is happy by my appreciation of her work. You think Allah is not going to be happy. when his Abd calls out to him with praise and gratitude?. And the way in which to express that praise and gratitude. is Salaah. What are we constantly repeating in Salaah. Every single Rakaa?.
سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ
ربنا لک الحمد
سبحان ربی الاعلی و تعالی
Constant praise and gratitude. And then Surah AlFateha in every rakaa. الحمد للہ رب العالمین. X3

You know Shaytan comes to us and says. Whats the point of your prayer. You don't even understand what you're saying. Look you can't even focus on prayer. Do you think Allah is going to accept such prayers?. You're wasting your time. He doesn't need you anyway. What are you praying for?. You don't know Arabic. You don't even understand WHY you're praying. What's the point of this kind of useless prayer?. Right?. Does that happen or no?. Happens to all of us. Happens to the BEST of us. But Allah hasn't asked for perfect prayer. he has only asked us to do the best we can. All he's asked us. is to show up. Just show up!. with praise and gratitude in the heart. That's it.
Look. this is something you kids need to understand. these physical forms of worship. Prayer, fasting, hajj, zakaat. these are all the mechanics of worship. these are all reactions and responses to HAMD. The real thing is recognizing Allah's blessings. and appreciating Allah's blessings. feeling gratitude after benefitting FROM them. Once you do that. worship and obedience are just natural responses. The problem is we make prayer the PRIMARY thing. NO. praise and gratitude. HAMD. is what's truly essential. Worship will naturally follow.
In fact. I challenge all of you. Just once. TRULY TRULY appreciate Allah's love in your heart. Just once TRULY feel gratitude in your heart for Allah's blessings. And then I challenge you NOT to pray when it comes time for Salaah. It'll become IMPOSSIBLE for you NOT to pray.

اِذا ھَلَّۃِ الحمدُ قَلباً . نَشِطَت فِی العِبَادَۃِ الاَعَضاءُ
When hamd penetrates the heart.  the limbs naturally respond in the worship of allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). Now you can't wait to stand before him.  to express that appreciation and gratitude to Allah. This was the way of the aslaaf. the sahaba. Not that they were born EXTRMELY pious. They just TRULY and COMPLETELY witnessed the love of Allah in their hearts. That's why for them. not to pray was just unthinkable. How do I NOT do salaah. I need to praise and thank my master. I'll tell you another thing about salaah.

You know Khala is listening in these sessions. But when I'm praising her. expressing her gratitude to her she's not the ONLY one listening. Her husband. Dillu chacha is listerning. Her sister Annu khala is listening. Her 2 daughters. Naveen and Nabila are listening. her grand children. her nephews and neices are listening. Tell me. When I am praising khala. Did it not make all of you HAPPY to hear her praise?. Did you not feel proud to be related to her?. I bet you did. Why is that?. I'm not praising you?. I'm not talking about you?. What are you happy about?. You're happy. because I am praising the one YOU love. Right?.
When you and I stand for Salaah. and we call out.  حی علی الصلوۃ. حی علی الفلاح. Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) says in a hadees. We get surrounded by angels. We get surrounded by angels listening to every word of praise. coming out of our mouths during our salaah. You may not understand Arabic. But guess what?. They do. And they LOVE it.  Rasul Allah said. that when a believer stands in salaah. all the angles listening to the praise of their beloved master. they get into a state of ecstasy. وجد. And they start praying for the musallee. saying. Ya Rabb. we testify. we bear witness that this slave praised you. We bear witness that this expressed his gratitude to you. And then one angel comes. and puts his mouth on the mouth of the Musallee. and he takes in every single world. every single letter. every single syllable of every single word. until the moment the musallee says his salaam. And then he rushes back in the presence of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). and repeats the entire praise before him. testifying. that this person. praised you. he repented on his sins. he seeked your forgiveness. Oh Allah. I plead to you on his behalf to forgive him.

So you know what. don't you dare think that your prayers are going unappreciated. Even if you don't understand a word you're saying. it is being appreciated. Your effort. just the fact that you're showing up. The fact that you're dropping whatever you were doing. and showing up before Allah. The fact that you are making Allah's praise and gratitude a PRIORITY for you. believe me. Wallahee. I swear to you. it counts. It counts WAY more than you can imagine. 

The only time. a human being gets to ACT like an angel. is during Salaah. Allah says in the Quran. that if we look at the throne of AlRehman. what we will see.
وَتَرَى ٱلْمَلَٓئِكَةَ.  حَآفِّينَ مِنْ حَوْلِ ٱلْعَرْشِ.  يُسَبِّحُونَ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّهِمْ ۖ وَقُضِىَ بَيْنَهُم بِٱلْحَقِّ
You will see the angels circling the throne of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala).  and you will see them praising Allah. And how will they be praising Allah. what will they be saying?
وَقِيلَ ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ
They will be saying الحمد للہ رب العلمین . As they are walking around the throne of Allah. As they are expressing their servitude to Allah. There will be one single buzzing around the throne. and that is. الحمد للہ رب العلمین. All praise and gratitued belongs to Allah. the master of all universes. 
And this is also what the people of Jannah are constantly doing. This was Vaqars question many sessions back. He asked. What will we be doing in Jannah?. And I waited for this day to answer his question. so everyone can fully appreciate it. Allah tells us about it in the Quran. 
دَعْوَىٰهُمْ فِيهَا.  سُبْحَنَكَ ٱللَّهُمَّ . وَتَحِيَّتُهُمْ فِيهَا سَلَمٌۭ.  وَآخِرُ دَعْوَىٰهُمْ أَنِ ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ
SubhanAllah what a beautiful verse! There will be only one statement being declared in the heavens. There is only one acknowledgment. that will resonate and echo in the heavens.
سُبْحَنَكَ ٱللَّهُمَّ
My mater is perfect.
وَتَحِيَّتُهُمْ فِيهَا سَلَمٌۭ ۚ
And people will be greeting each other with messages of peace.
But the final statement . after every single conversation. after every single interaction. their final statement will ALWAYS be the same.
وَآخِرُ دَعْوَىٰهُمْ.  أَنِ ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ
Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah. the master of the alameen. The people of jannah. will be people of HAMD. They will be people of praise. and they will be people of gratitude.
اللھم جعلنا من الحامدین. May Allah make us among these people.

This is the status we are elevated to during Salaah. We turn into angels. and we turn into people of Jannah. for that duration. Doing what they're doing. What was that narration about that Baddu praising Allah.

Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) and Hazrat Bilaal. they walk into Masjid Nabwee. A baddu was busy in prayer. So Rasul Allah and Bilal went and sat behind him. The Baddu has no idea that the messenger of Allah is sitting behind him. He finishes his prayer. does salaam. raises both hands. and starts praising Allah.
یا من لا تراہُ العیون.  ولا تُخاَلِطُہُ الزُّنُون . ولا یَصِفَہُ الواصِفُون . ولا تُغَیِّرُہُ الحَوادِث . وَلا یَغشِی الدَّوَائِر .  یعلم عدد قطر الامطار . و عدد وَرَقِ الأشجار . وعدد ما أَظلم علیہ الَّیل  . و أشرق علیہ النَّھار .  یعلم مَکائِیلَ البِحار . وَ مَثَاکیِل الجبال.  لا تُوارِی مِنہُ سماءٌ سَمآءَ . ولا أرضٌ أرضا. ولا بحرٌ ما فی قَعرِہِ.   ولا جَبَلٌ ما فی وَعرِہِ .  أِجعل خَیرَ عُمری آخِرَۃ.  و خَیرَ عَملِ خَواتِیمَ .  و خَیرَ أیامِ‏ یومَ القاَکَ فِیہِ
What was he saying?. Oh the one. that eyes cannot see. Oh the one. that the flights of imaginations cannot reach. The one who is above and beyond the praise of all those who praise him. There is no one who can do justice to you in praise and gratitude. Time cannot influence you. Space cannot confine you. You know the count of every drop of rain that fall on the earth. You know the count of every leaf that grows on trees.You know the count of everything that the night hides. You know the count of everything that the day reveals. Oh the one who knows how much salt there is in the oceans. and who knows the weight of all mountains. The ceiling of the sky cannot hide anything from you. the floor of this earth cannot hide anything from you. you see what the ocean hides in its depths. You see what the cave hides in its belly.
أِجعل خَیرَ عُمری آخِرَۃ
Make the rest of my days. the best days of my life.
و خَیرَ عَملِ خَواتِیمَ
Make my last action in this world. the one that is the BEST in your eyes.
و خَیرَ أیامِ‏ یومَ القاَکَ فِیہِ
And make the day I finally meet you. the BEST day of my life.
He's saying all of this and Rasul Allah is sitting behind him. listening to his Hamd. and he gets so excited. he asks Bilaal. Do you have something I can give as a gift to this man?. Imagine. how happy Rasul Allah is listening to the praise of his master. He does not have anything to give. so he asks Hazrat Bilaal if he has something?. Hazrat Bilaal says. I have this small piece of gold. The messenger of Allah take it as a loan from Bilaal and gives it to the Baddu. The Baddu gets really surprised. He asks. Ya Rasul Allah. why are you giving me this?. He says.
بحسن ثنائک علی اللہ
For this beautiful praise you just recited for Allah. Now imagine this. This is the messenger of Allah. getting into a euphoric state listening to the praise of his master. and can't help but reward him. even if he has to take a loan. When he dies and stands before. What reward do you think his master will give him?.


What do we say in that dua Motee suwalaat when we open our fasts?
یا معطی السؤالات.  یا ولی الرغبات.  یا منفس الکربات.  یا کافی الھم والغم 
Oh the one who answers needs. Oh the one who is a custodian of all my desires. Oh the one who removes suffering from me. Oh the one who takes care of me in my anxieties and sorrows .
یا حنان یا منان یا ذاالجلال والاکرام
Oh the kind. the beneficent. Oh the mighty. the generous
یا من اعطیٰ خیر ما فی خزائنہ الایمان بہ قبل السؤال
Oh the one who gave us the BEST thing from his treasures. which is Eman. which is faith. without our asking.
لا تمنعنا اقل ما فی خزائنک العفو مع السؤال
Do not prevent from me. the least important thing from your treasures.  which is forgiveness. that I am now asking you for.

SubhanAllah! Such a beautiful Dua. Ya Allah you gave me the BEST thing from your treasures. which is faith. without my asking you. Why would you prevent the lowest. the cheapest. item for you in your treasures. which is forgiveness. that I am ASKING you for. doesn't make sense.




 

This is a continuation of the previous session. I broke down the concept of Hamd. as it relates to us in two parts.  We covered the first part last time. in which I explained what hamd means. types of hamd. there is hamd for Allah. and hamd for the sake of Allah. which is the hamd of his intermediaries. We talked about the fact that even though Allah does not NEED us. he still DOES love us. He does not NEED our praise and gratitude. but he DOES love and appreciate it. We also talked about how HAMD is a mechanism. designed by the Rabb for the progression of his ABD. It facilitate his physical and spiritual growth. and brings him closer to his Rabb. And this ability to appreciate and be grateful. has been placed within the core essence. the LUBB. of all human beings. Every child is created with this ability of Hamd.

In fact it is narrated in a hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) in which he tells us. that when Allah fashioned his first creation. Adam AS. And he blew his ROOH into him.
ثُمَّ سَوَّىٰهُ وَنَفَخَ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِهِ
This ROOH was blown into Adam from the head down. And the hadees says. when the rooh reached his nose. it tickled him. and when something tickles your nose. what happens?. You sneeze!. So Adam AS sneezed. And appreciating the fact that he has been giving the blessing of life. that he is now alive. he instinctively appreciated the gift of life and became grateful for it. And so his immediate response to that sneeze. WITHOUT anybody teaching him anything. The first words that came out of the mouth of the the first human being. was AlHamdulillah!. Allah did not teach him that. And this is very interesting. because when it came to proving himself before the angels. وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا. Allah TAUGHT Adam all the divine names. When Adam and Hawwa made the mistake of reaching for the forbidden tree. they were punished. But they wanted to seek forgiveness. فَتَلَقَّىٰٓ آدَمُ مِن رَّبِّهِۦ كَلِمَتٍۢ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ. Their master taught them certain words through which they presented their repentence. So on every stage we find that Adam needed training. But not when he sneezed. Not when he recognized. appreciated. and was grateful for the blessing of life. He instinctively said.  AlHamdulillah. Because HAMD is something that Allah had ingrained it within him. within his inner nature. within his Lubb.
When Allah heard these words. he was so happy. that his slave appreciated his blessing. and he expressed his gratitude to him.that he responed back saying. Yarhamakul Allah Ya Adam. Your Allah will ALWAYS have mercy on you Oh Adam. Think about this for a second. This is the very first conversation that is taking place between the very first ABD. and his RABB. And what is this conversation?. An exchange of Hamd and Rehma. This is the first rule that is being set between the Rabb and the ABD. You come to me with HAMD. I will respond back to you with love, care, concern and mercy. Rehma!.
This is why today when we sneeze. we say AlHamdulillah. and the one who hears us sneeze says. یَرحَمَکُ اللہ. May Allah have mercy on you. It's a reminder of this relationship that we have as ABD. with our Rabb. And this is why even in Surah AlFateha. immediately after الحمد للہ رب العلمین. what comes next?. الرحمن الرحیم. And notice there is no other word attached with it. It's now part of a sentence. It stands all on its own. Just pure REHMA. The more Hamd the ABD does. the more mercy. the more love. the more blessings. the RABB responds with. SubhanAllah!. What a beautiful relationship this!
Linguistic meaning of Kausar

Then I explained why hamd has to be both elements. It has to be praise AND gratitude. We talked about why it cannot be one or the other. And then finally we talked about the relationship between Hamd and Salaah. which is a physical manifestation of Hamd. We find in Surah AlKausar. Allah says to his beloved messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam).
إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ ‎
No doubt about it. we have granted you Kausar. Most translations will explain Kausar. as abundant. No doubt we have given you abundantly. But that word doesn't even come close to capturing the meaning of Kausar. The word Kausar. it belongs to an Arabic pattern. فَوعَل.  and this is one of the patterns of hyperbole in Arabic.  it's called صیغۃ المبالغۃ. AlKausar comes from kasra. or kaseer. WHICH actually means to have in abundance. to have plenty. to have lots. But AlKausar is then a hyperbole of Kasheer. It means INCREDIBLE amounts of something. When you have lots and lots and lots and lots. then you don't call it kaseer.  you call it کَوثَر. Allahs  says I have given you lots and lots and lots and lots. and I can keep repeating the lots as much as I want. because it is کَوثَر.
Then کَوثَرis not just about huge quantities. It also implies something extremely valuable. For example. If someone owns a huge quantity of hay. or TONS and TONS of grass or straw. they would not use the word کَوثَر. That would still have to use the word kaseer. For کَوثَر. it not only has to be huge in quantity. it also had to be enormous in its value. That's another implication in the word Kausar. No doubt we gave you huge quantities of blessings. and each and every blessing that we gave you.  is extremely valuable.
Now when you  say a LOT of something and a LOT in value. it is possible that it could be all good. or it could be all bad. or it’s a mix of both. For example. having a lot of drugs. lot of ammunition. centuries old wine cellars.  These can be in huge quantities. and they can be very expensive. but they're not good. So it is possible to have huge quantities of expensive stuff that is bad. Or some is good and some is bad. In all those cases. you would still have to use the word Kaseer. Because the word kaseer. can be used for both good and bad things. but the word کَوثَر.  can ONLY be used for good things. it is مُتخَصَّص.  It can only be used in the context of THAT which is good.
Then there are several other meanings which I'll skip. For our discussion today. in this ayah Allah is saying to his messenger.  انا اعطیناک الکوثر. We have given you enormous amounts of invaluable blessings. and each and every one of them. are incredibly good. Now let's quickly look at some of these incredible gifts that Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) is referring to.

 EXAMPLES
Allah says to his messenger in the Quran.
مَا وَدَّعَكَ رَبُّكَ وَمَا قَلَىٰ
We did not leave you. nor are we displeased with you…  تَودِع.  in Arabic is when you say goodbye. That's where you get the word. الوداع. And you say الوداع. when you are leaving someone.  So Allah is saying to his messenger. Your Rabb is not saying goodbye to you. nor is he displeased. There is a special gift in this verse.  because the expected sentence should have been. ما ودَّعک ربک و ما قلاک. There should have been a "KA" at the end of Qalaa. the English translation of that would have been. Your master did not say goodbye to YOU. and he is not displeased with YOU. but with goodbye. with ودَّعک .  the messenger is mentioned. but with displeasure. the messenger is not mentioned. and that is a gift of Allah to his beloved messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Cause it shows Allah's extreme love for his messenger. The word goodbye does not have any negative connotation associated with it. But the word displeasure clearly does. and so Allah does not mention his beloved messenger next to that negative word. This is how careful Allah is when addressing his messenger. And of course the lesson of the ayah is. the Allah is never going to EVER be the one to abandon his beloved messenger. 

Then he says to his messenger . ولا الاخرۃ خیر لک من الاولی. No doubt about it. what is coming at the end. is better for you. than what is at the beginning. What an amazing gift to the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Allah is saying to him. You're being honored right now. only a few people are becoming Muslims right now. But in times to come. Islam will spread like wild fire. and your name will be honored more and more as time passes by. So what's coming later in terms of your honor. is way more than what you're seeing right now.
Then on top of that.ولسوف یعطیک ربک فترضی.I will give you so much that you will be pleased. You know when you tell someone. I'm going to give you a gift. The verbal or non-verbal response to that is always. What are you going to give me?. how much? . What's it going to be worth?. How valuable is it going to be for me?. I bet it's the new iPad Pro because he knows I want that. And then when you unrwrap it. its a nailcutter. LOL. (True Story).
But the real question is. how WOULD would you place a VALUE on a gift?. Look at the value that Allah put on his gifts for His Messenger. he says. فترضی. The quantity. the value. and the goodness of the gift has been described in such a way. that I will give you SO much. I will KEEP giving you SO much. and I won't stop. until YOU yourself say it's enough. Until you say. Ya Allah I am pleased. You can stop now!. And look at the love of this amazing messenger for us (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). فدا امی و ابی.  He said I will not be pleased until every single person from my Ummah is saved from the hell fire. This is the value HE. (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) placed . OUR freedom. Our salvation. This is the kind of love he had for us.

And even when it comes to the rewards that Allah is going to give to his messenger.
وَإِنَّ لَكَ لَأَجْرًا غَيْرَ مَمْنُونٍۢ
My beloved messenger. You have a reward that can't even be quantified. It cannot have any brakes on it. it cannot have any limits on it. Think about it. When it came to giving the messenger blessings in this world.  the limit on it was set at what?. Until the messenger HIMSELF says enough.  and when it came to giving the rewards for his work to his beloved messenger in the after life.  Allah says. وَإِنَّ لَكَ لَأَجْرًا غَيْرَ مَمْنُونٍۢ. No doubt about it. I will give you SO MUCH reward that there is no number that can possibly define it. and my reward will never end. it will only keep increasing for all eternity. AllahuAkbar.

Then another gift from AlKausar. is that Allah elevated Rasul Allah beyond the seventh heaven. and spoke to him directly on the night of Meraaj. This was a gift that was not given to any prophet. any messenger before or after him. Then during their conversation. Allah bestowed another gift on his messenger. ان لا ذُکرتُ الاَّ ذُکرتَ معی. Allah said. My name shall not be called upon without the mention of your name along with it…… We say. اشھد ان لا الہ الا اللہ. And immediately what comes next?. اشھد ان محمد رسول اللہ. This is an incrediby valuable gift given by Allah to his beloved messenger. Name one other human being on the planet. who is being mentioned in this way constantly. Constantly.  And instead of the mention going down over time.  what happens?.  it keep going UP over time. It keeps on increasing. SubhanAllah! . And then on the same pattern Rasul Allah said the same thing for Maulana Ali. That I will not accept my name called upon until your name is mentioned along with it. And that's why immediate after the mention of the prophet. we have. اشھد ان مولانا علی ولی اللہ .

Another gift is that Allah made it obligatory on Muslims to remember and send praises upon the Prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). So a believer is constantly looking for opportunities to do so. But not just that. Allah himself sent his praises and blessings on his beloved Prophet.
إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ وَمَلَٓئِكَتَهُۥ يُصَلُّونَ عَلَى ٱلنَّبِىِّ
No doubt even Allah and his angels. CONSTANTLY send praises upon His messengers. 
يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ صَلُّوا۟ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلِّمُوا۟ تَسْلِيمًا
So those of you who believed. you need to realize this and you need to send praise and blessings on my beloved messenger as well. And there is something really very interesting about this ayah. There are so so many ayaats in the Quran in which Allah begins with . يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ . But in this verse he did not beging that way. Allah did not begin by saying Oh you who believed. He began by first talking about himself and his angels. then he said. يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ .  Why?. Because he's saying. I want you to realize that what I'm telling you to do.  is something I do myself.  and my angels do it too.  How  can the mention of this amazing messenger not be elevated?. And this is why we never say his name. Muhammad. without saying (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Because Allah curses the one who says the name of his beloved without praising him.

Then Allah swears by the city he lives. لا اقسم بھذا البلد.  he swears by the city in which the messenger is born. He honors the city of Mecca. Why?.  وأنت حلٌّ بھذا البلد.  only because YOU. my beloved messenger. because you are living in it.

Then another gift from AlKausar. Allays says.الم نشرح لک صدرک. . Did we not open your chest for you?. And what a magnificent opening that the entire Quran can fit into it. The same Quran which would shatter and exploded mountains if it was revealed on them. 
لَوْ أَنزَلْنَا هَذَا ٱلْقُرْآنَ عَلَىٰ جَبَلٍۢ لَّرَأَيْتَهُۥ خَشِعًۭا مُّتَصَدِّعًۭا مِّنْ خَشْيَةِ ٱللَّهِ
But this same Quran  fits into the heart of the messenger. 

Another amazing gift to Rasul Allah. is an obedient ABD like Maulana Ali. When Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) had to migrate to Madina. he needed a decoy. He needed someone to sleep in his bed while he escaped to Medina. And only Maulana Ali agreed to do that. And this was the night when the kuffar were planning to assassinate Rasul Allah. And Maulana Ali knew this and he chose to sleep on his bed that night. And much later he confessed. He said. I swear! I never slept SO peacefully in my ENTIRE life.  as I slept on that night of Hijra on Rasul Allah's bed. Imagine that. People are coming to assassinate him. and he says. I never slept MORE peacefully than that night. That night was the BEST sleep I ever had in my entire life. What a gift to have an ABD like Maulana Ali. My nana. Mulla Shafaqaut Hussain. in one of his poems he referes to this incident. he says.

شب حجرت شجاعت کی، علی کی دیکھئے منظر
نڈر ہو کر باطمینان سوئے تان کر چادر
گواہی دے رہا تھا یہ رسول اللہ کا بستر
علی حیدر، علی صفدر، علی داور، علی یاور
علی ایماں ، علی قرآں، علی سلطاں ، علی آقا

Then another gift is the never ending chain of Imamat that will be from the progeny of Maulana Ali and Maulatina Fatima. And Rasul Allah compared these Imams to the arc of Nooh AS.
مثل اهل بيتى فيكم . كمثل سفينه نوح
The example of my progeny among you. is like the ark of Noah.
من ركبها نجا . ومن تخلف عنها . غرق وهوى
Whoever climbs aboard it will be saved. and whoever refuses to get onboard. will drown in this ocean of ignorance and be destroyed. And the door to that ark is AHAD Shareef. Through Ahad shareef we climb aboard this ship of Imamt. Imamat is the guarantee of salvation for his Ummah. Another incredible gift.

And there are thousands upon thousands of such gifts mentioned in the Quran and hadees. Innumerable. Invaluable gifts that Allah bestowed upon his beloved messenger. Without even him asking in most cases.
You know Ibraheem AS  made so many prayers for the Qibla. He prayed day an night to Allah. to make Bait Almaqdis the qibla for believers. To turn the hearts of the people towards it.  make this a place that is full of virtue.  and a place of peace. 
وَإِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَهِۦمُ رَبِّ ٱجْعَلْ هَذَا بَلَدًا آمِنًۭا وَٱرْزُقْ أَهْلَهُۥ مِنَ ٱلثَّمَرَتِ مَنْ آمَنَ مِنْهُم بِٱللَّهِ وَٱلْيَوْمِ ٱلْآخِرِ
He made SO many prayers. and then after all those requests. Allah made Masjid AlAQSA the qibla for Ibraheem AS and his followers.
But when Allah changed the direction of the Qibla. from AlAqsa to Masjid Haraam.  Do you know why he did it?. He explained his reason in the Quran. And that reason was. Listen to this.
قَدْ نَرَىٰ تَقَلُّبَ وَجْهِكَ فِى ٱلسَّمَآءِ
My beloved messenger. We saw your face turn towards the sky. 
فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ قِبْلَةًۭ . تَرْضَىٰهَا
and so we. are changing the Qibla  for you.  No doubt about it. فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ . then we swear that we are for sure. changing the qibla for you. Why?. Because you simply looked at me with that desire in your heart. SubhanAllah! . He didn't ask Allah. He did not pray to Allah. He did not make dua. He just had a sad look in his eyes. and he looked at the sky. and that very instant. the ayah comes down. Look we're changing the Qibla. تَرْضَهَا. To make YOU happy!.تَرْضَهَا. so that you would be pleased. SubhanAllah!
This one action. that Rasul Allah looked at the sky with a desire for the qibla to change to Bait AlHaraam. it changed the entire world's history. Billions of people today are praying in a different direction. for one reason alone.  تَرْضَهَا. So that the messenger could have a smile on his face. (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . This is an incredible thing to appreciate. The love that the creator has for his beloved messenger.

Prayer is expression of gratitude
So now when Allah grants such gifts. on his beloved messenger. How you do you think Rasul Allah must have felt?. What did we say is the natural response for any decent human being. for any blessing no matter how small it is?. Praise and Gratitude. Right?. So then what would you imagine. would be the response of someone like Rasul Allah's.  for something like AlKausar?. Immense Praise. Immense gratitude?. right?
But how should he express that gratitude?. How does a humble. incapable. ABD. a slave. How can he express his gratitude to such a benevolent. such a merciful. such a self-sufficent. SUCH a loving Rabb?. Because the gratitude needs to be acceptable to the benefactor right?. When someone does something incredible for you. What is your reaction towards that person?. Tell me what can I do for you in return!. YOU tell me what will make you happy?. cause there is absolutely no way I can think of repaying you for this. Please tell me if there is ABSOLUTELY aything in the world that I can do for you. Does that happen?.
In history we study that people when they received an audience with the king. they would take these expensive gifts. jewels and precious stones. or something of great historic value. to gain his pleasure. Why is that?. It was to show appreciation and gratitude for that audience. The chance to stand before the king. And obviously the gift or the gratitude has to reflect the level. the status. the position of the king!.
So how do we. as ABD. as slaves. express our gratitude to the king of all kings. To the Rabb of All Rabbs?. right?.  And so now Rasul Allah has to show gratitude for not just any gift. he has to show gratitude for AL-KAUSAR. For uncountable, invaluable, blessings each one better than the next. So who can possibly dictate the terms of that gratitude?. Who is going to tell him what level of gratitude will be acceptable to him?. Obviously Allah has to set those terms. Ya Allah. with everything that you've done for me. what can I do now. to express my gratitude to you?. A praise and a gratitude that would be acceptable in your eyes?. And Allah answers that question in the very next verse as the surah continues.
فصل لربک ونحر
We have given you ALKAUSAR. We have given you gifts that are more valuable than the entire treasures and sovereignty of this world combined. with all of its assets and its wealth. So now what do you do to express your gratitude?. You establish Salaah for your master. Present your appreciation and your gratitude to your Rabb. How?. فصل لربک ونحر. Establish salaah for your Rabb and sacrifice. Sacrifice being a reference to Hajj. when we HAVE to sacrifice an animal. Again. Allah joins two ends together. Remember I explained to you previously he said. اشکر لی ولوالدیک
Be grateful to me and your parents?. He combined two ends together. Allah is on the furthest end for us. parents on the closest end for us. So he mentiones the two intermediaries. but the implication is. and all the intermediaries in between. This is a typical style of classical Arabic. Here also he says.فصل لربک ونحر . Prayer. which is obligator EVERY single day. 5 times a day. and Hajj which is obligatory only ONCE in a lifetime. You want to be praise me and be grateful to me?. Then establish Salaah which is every single day. and Hajj which is once in a lifetime. and everything in between. So the 7 دعائم. is the format that Rasul Allah set for us to express our gratitude to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). and it begins with Salaah. 

FA is a connective particle in arabic. It is used to show response.  I did this for you. SO. you do this for me.
إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ.  We gave you AlKausar. ف. SO. صل لربک ونحر. Pray to your master and sacrifice.

And we know that anything that Rasul Allah is taught in the Quran. that teaching automatically applies to us. Because he is the intermediary through which Allah speaks to us. He not only gave Rasul Allah ALKausar. He also gave US ALKausar. What greater blessing to us than Rasul Allah himself (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Through this man we got the Quran. we got the means of our salvation. the recognition of our master. his love. his mercy. protection from hellfire. promise of heavens. And then the gift of Maulana Ali. and the panjatan. and the Imams and the duaat. and the manaseeb. teachers. parents. And so weven when we look at our lives. we have uncountable. invaluable gifts within us. And so Allah mentioned the rule in Surah AlKausar. You feeling grateful?. Salaah and Hajj and everything in between.


Heart, tongue, limbs
 

With that understanding. I now want to take a more granular look at Hamd. and explain its various forms of manifestation in us human beings. All of human activity. is divided into 3 parts or 3 components.  First is the heart. which is where intention (نیت), will (ارادہ), and belief (ایمان) resides…… Then we have the tongue. which is called ترجمان القلب. The interpreter for the heart. Because it articulates what the heart feels. In other words the tongue. puts forth a claim BASED on an intention. And then finally we have the limbs. which are tools for ACTION. Action for what?. To PROVE the CLAIM. that the tongue made. BASED on the intention of the heart. I'll say that again. ACTION of the limbs. is the physical PROOF. for the CLAIM that the tongue makes. about the INTENTION of the heart.

Intention is unseen. it is invisible. It is spiritual in nature. If I am feeling thirsty and I want to drink water. that feeling is something that is in my heart. There is no way for you to know that. Because there is no hard core evidence for that intention. But then that unseen intention. is given life. THROUGH a claim. which is speech. So I articulate that feelings to you. by saying the words. I AM THIRSTY. Now. THROUGH my claim. you came to know of my intention. But the thing with claim is. it can be true. or it can also be false. And that is why the claim. then needs to be followed by an ACTION. which serves as a SOLID. substantial proof. of what the speech CLAIMED. about the INTENTION of the heart. So now if I am thirsty. and I claim that I am thirsty. And then I back that up by drinking a glass of water. My ACT of drinking water. becomes a proof. that my claim was true. and that I really was feeling thirsty. Not only do YOU become a witness to my act. I myself become a witness to it.

This is why. one of the attributes of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala).  is الشھید. And Shahada means two things. It means witness. and it also means testimony. Now you can't testify. until you've actually witnessed something. right?. So when it comes to this entire universe. it is divided into two parts. عالم الغیب و الشھادۃ. The world that is unseen (الغیب). And the world that is seen (الشھادۃ). Allah exists in a realm that is beyond the spiritual and physical worlds. because he is the creator of both worlds. From that unseen realm. he puts forth certain claims ABOUT himself. about his essence and his attributes. How?. Through the Quran. Through this reveleation. Why is it called revelation?. Because it is revealing to us what is hidden from us. And so Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) is making claims about himself. I am Rehman. I am Raheem. I am Azeem. I am Ghafoor. There is a reward for good deeds. There is punishment for bad deeds. I will reward you. I will punish you. right?. He is revealing himself and his intentions to us through this Quran. which is serving the purpose of a tongue. Because that's what the Quran is. It is speech. It is a لسان. Language.

وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَهُوَ ٱلْعَزِيزُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ‎
وَإِنَّهُۥ لَتَنزِيلُ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ
نَزَلَ بِهِ ٱلرُّوحُ ٱلْأَمِينُ
عَلَىٰ قَلْبِكَ لِتَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنذِرِينَ
بِلِسَانٍ عَرَبِىٍّۢ مُّبِينٍۢ

So Allah is making all these claims. revealing all these things about the unseen world!. Where is the proof?. What is the evidence for all these claims?. This physical world. The Rabb AlAlameen created this عالَم . as a witness. and a testimony. for his attributes and existence. And this is what we learnt in the session on Alameen. He created the عالَم . so that the عالِم could witness the attributes of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) manifesting through his creation. and TESTIFY that whatever Allah is saying through the Quran. is in fact true. And that truly. there is no ILAH except Allah. لا الہ الا اللہ. Allah himself gave us PHYSICAL evidence for ALL his claims. to set an example for us. that ULTIMATELY it is ACTION. and not words or intentions. that hold value. And this is why if you look at the famous hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) on intentions. what does it say?
انما الاعمال بالنیات
No doubt Actions are based on intentions. There are several meanings of this hadees given by Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq AS. I'll explain ONLY one meaning today which is line with the context of our conversation today. انما الاعمال بالنیات. No doubt. if you TRULY intended something. your ACTIONS will prove it. And what's really interesting. is the sequence of words in this hadees. Which word is first?. Amal. or Niyyah?. انما الاعمال بالنیات. Amal is first. But we know that intention happens first. then why is it being said this way?. He could have said. انما النیت محرک العمل. No doubt intentions drive action. NO. He brought action FIRST. Because this physical world. is a world of Action. It is دار العمل. The house of ACTIONS. Akhira is دار النیۃ. the house of intentions. So anything that will be proven in this world. will be proven THROUGH action. Therefore no doubt ACTION is based on intention. If there is NO action. then you have NO evidence for your intention. and your claims of your intention are false.  In fact notice. claim is not even mentioned in the hadees. There is only action and intention. Because those are the two things that really matter. Claim is just the middle man. connecting the two things. right?
Now of course there are cases when we intend to do something. are then are not able to do ACT upon it because of certain circumstances. But those are exceptions. But the general rule is. if you truly intend something. you WILL prove it through your ACTION.

So these are the three components of an عالَم . Any عالَم . The heart (قلب). The tongue or the claim (لسان). and finally the limbs(جوارح). And in the final analysis. it is the physical ACT which becomes the CLEAR EVIDENCE . for a claim. that was based on an intention. Just like this physical world manifests and testifies for the realities and the truths of a spiritual universe. Physical actions testify FOR the realities and truths of the soul.

Distribution of Hamd on 3 components

So now lets look at Hamd. and how it applies to these three parts of human activity. Hamd begins with the appreciation of a blessing. إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ ‎. We have granted you innumerable. invaluable blessings. ALL of which are good. The ABD recognizing these blessings from his Rabb. he develops an appreciation FOR them. Where?. In his heart. He then articulates that appreciation through his tongue. he says subhanAllah! What an amazing gift. And then his limbs come into ACTION. in order to RECEIVE the benefit of that blessing…… This is the process of praise. that occurs through these three components. the heart. the tongue. and the limbs.

So this is how praise takes place. BEFORE the benefit is received. which motivates us TOWARDS the benefit.

Now once the benefit is received. what gets generated in the HEART. is gratitude for the benefactor. That feeling of gratitude. is then articulated by the tongue with words of gratitude. And then the limbs come into ACTION. to take advantage of that blessing. to put that blessing to its proper use. This is VERY important to understand. Gratitude of the heart is the recognition of a blessing. that somone did something nice for us. Gratitude of the tongue is verbalizing that feeling by saying "THANK YOU". But the gratitude of the limbs. is actually USING the benefit FOR its intended purpose.

Let's say your parents buy you a phone. which YOU don't pay for. THEY pay for it. But they buy it FOR you.  so that they can always make sure you're safe…… So that they can reach you when they need to. So that you can contact them in case you're running late. or in case of an emergency. That is why parents buy their children a phone. Now its OK. if you use that phone to talk to your friends. play games. text them. chat with them. use it as an alarm. All of that is fine. 
But if you do all those other things. but you never call your parents when you're supposed to. to let them know you're safe. If you don't answer their call when they are trying to reach you. If you don't call them when you have an emergency. then you are NOT being grateful for that phone…… You may be feeling gratitude in your heart for you. you may be saying thank you. But PHYSICALLY. PRACTICALLY. you are not showing gratitude for that phone. You understand?. Why?. Because TRUE gratitude manifests in ACTION. when you fulfill the purpose of that blessing. And this is why

الشُّکرُ نِعمتُ العَین. خِفضُ البَصَر
The eye is a blessing.
