The ability to see itself is a blessing. and the gratitude for the eye. the way we thank Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for the blessing of the eye. is to lower it from the forbidden. We do not look at the things that Allah has prohibited to see. The gratitude for the blessing of hearing. is to not listen to the forbidden. the gheebah, the nameemah, the bohtaan. all this type of things. The gratitude of the tongue. is to speak the truth. and not engage it in lies. in gossip. in back-biting. Because every single part of the body is a blessing that has a specific purpose. Understanding that purpose. and fulfilling it. IS the true HAMD for that blessing.

This is what Allah means when he says.
تُسَبِّحُ لَهُ ٱلسَّمَوَتُ ٱلسَّبْعُ وَٱلْأَرْضُ وَمَن فِيهِنَّ.  وَإِن مِّن شَىْءٍ إِلَّا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ. 
The seven heavens and the earth and whatever is in them exalt Him.  And there is not a single thing that does not exalt his Hamd.
وَلَكِن لَّا تَفْقَهُونَ تَسْبِيحَهُمْ.  إِنَّهُۥ كَانَ حَلِيمًا غَفُورًۭا
But you do not understand their ways of exaltation. No doubt he is Forbearing and Forgiving.

What does it mean everything in the world is doing his hamd?. Have you seen the sun saying Thank you Allah!. Have you seen the moon. the starts. the sky. the earth. praising Allah?. How are these things showing their gratitude to him?. They are praising him. and they are showing gratitude to him. BY FULFILLING THEIR PURPOSE. That is what SHUKUR means. To fulfill its purpose. And we find the evidence of this in EVERY SINGLE creation in this universe. in nature. Every organ . ever cell within our body. knows what its supposed to do. which is praise. and then it is DOING exactly what it is supposed to do. which is gratitude.
وَإِن مِّن شَىْءٍ إِلَّا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ
There is not a single thing that is not doing his Hamd. If there is a creation that is in fact NOT doing Hamd. it is us human beings. The ONLY creation for which this entire universe was created in the first place!

False Praise
A praise that BEGINS in the heart and ENDS on the tongue. And does not translate into the ACT of benefitting from the blessing. is false praise…… It's hypocrisy…… Because you're saying one thing. but then you're doing something contrary to what you're saying. You believe Allah is your Rabb. You admit that Allah is your Rabb. But then you don't want to do what he asks you to do. That's false praise. Similarly a gratitude. that begins in the heart and ends on the tongue.  is a false gratitude. It is a delusion of gratitude. It is gratitude that has no physical. no tangible evidence. Not for you, not for anyone else…… You're just kidding yourself that you're grateful.

See. I can believe I love Allah. I can claim that I love Allah. But if I am not obeying Allah. then I am deluded about my love for Allah. Because true love is doing what the beloved asks. Even in the worldly sense.
َزعَمتُ حُبُّ الاِلٰھِی وَ تُعصِیہُ
You claim that you love Allah and then you disobey Him. 
ان کان حُبُّکَ صَادِق .  لَطاَعَتُہُ
If your love was real. you would obey him
لأِنَّ المُحِبَّ لمِنَ یُحِبُّ.  مُطِیعُ
Because the one.  who loves somebody is always obedient to them. Otherwise its just lip service. which means nothing. And this is why in Surah Yaseen Allah says.
ٱلْيَوْمَ نَخْتِمُ عَلَىٰٓ أَفْوَهِهِمْ وَتُكَلِّمُنَآ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَتَشْهَدُ أَرْجُلُهُم بِمَا كَانُوا۟ يَكْسِبُونَ
On the day of judgment. we will seal their mouths. And their hands will speak to us and their feet will testify. about what they have earned. Why?. Isn't the tongue the organ of speech?. Why is Allah sealing my mouth?. and making my limbs speak?. Because on that day. ACTION is all that is going to matter. ACTIONS will litreally speak louder than words on that day. And look in this ayah. the word used is کسب. earned. Why earned?. What is an earning?. It is something you GET. in return for labor or services. Earning is not something you get on good intentions. Earning is not something you get on verbal claims. Earning is ONLY based on action. right?. Blessings are always earned through the ACTION of hamd.
This is the most natural phenomenon that exists in this world. Right from birth. When a child is born in this world. its mothers milk is the first blessing it tastes. Not even milk. what the baby gets is colostrum. which is not even sweet. But even to get that. Does the baby just get it. or does it have to work for it?. The baby literally has to suck it out?. But then that's how it grows. right?. The muscles get engaged. they get stronger. And when its shows gratitude for it. which is to demonstrate that it can digest it. Because that's gratitude. To demonstrate that it is able to use the benefit for the intended purpose. What happens next?. Allah gives it the blessing of milk which is better and sweeter than colostrum…… When it can digest that. that is. show gratitude for it. they start eating semi solid foods. then solids. and then a world of different tastes open up for the child. So the benefits keep increasing. as the child demonstrates that it is grateful for the previous blessing…… and EARNS the next one. In other words. it is the HAMD of the child. that advances it through the various level of his feeding.


Salaah is Hamd in action

OK. Let's recap. What did we talk about so far?. HAMD is a response to a blessing. That response has been divided between three components. The heart, the tongue and the limbs. ACTION of the limbs. is the proof for the claim made by the tongue. about the intention of the heart.

Which means. proof of sincere praise. is that it generates in the heart. it is articulated by the tongue. and it is ACTED upon by the limbs in receiving the benefit. And proof of sincere gratitude. is that it generates in the heart. articulated by the tongue. and then the limbs start USING that gift. for the purpose it was given for.
انا اعطیناک الکوثر
We gave you ALKAUSAR. So now what do you do?. Appreciate all those blessings. and be grateful for them. And how do you express that HAMD. physically?.
فصل لربک والنحر
The first step is. Pray to your master. Now if you look at Salaah in this context of Hamd. It is a perfect manifestation of Hamd. through the heart, tongue and limbs. The ABD when he hears the AZAAN. already having recognized the glory and the blessings of his Rabb in his life. he drops whatever he is doing. to answer the call of his Rabb. The hamd is already in his heart. which physically gets him on the Musalla (Janemaaz) in order to receive the rewards of salaah. That was praise right?. the desire to receive the benefit?. And then once he begins his salaah. it is all an expression of his gratitude. And so salaah demonstrates this perfect harmony between action speech and belief. The body is doing what the tongue is articulating. and the tongue is saying what the heart believes. There is absolutely no contention. no contradiction between any of them.
Another thing which I find incredibly beautiful about Salaah. is that it is composed of two states. rest and motion. All the duas that are recited in the state of rest. are either praise of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) or it is listening to revelation. Notice our state when we are reciting the Fateha or a surah. Physically we are supposed to be completely at rest. There should be no movement in the body. why?. Because our master. our Rabb is speaking to us through the Quran. So we stand there attentively listening to his speech. And then as soon as revelation ends. we get into motion. in obedience to what the Rabb commanded us to do. And in every movement after that. we do not recite Quran. we recite a tasbeeh. And what is tasbeeh?. It is affirmation of the Rububiyyah of Allah(Azza Wa Jal). And what you believe in your heart and affirm with your speech. you HAVE to back it up with action. So we bow down before him in rukoo. with the affirmation of.
سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ
We say. my Rabb is great and is truly deserving of my Hamd. and then in order to prove that bgelief and claim. we bow down before him in Rukoo. physically expressing our humility. our servitude. while at the same time expressing our beliefs.
سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ.
Then سمع اللہ لمن حمدہ. Allah listens to the HAMD of those who praise him and show their gratitude to him. and as we're saying that we lift our hands to our ears. because we have the ability to listen as well. And we have heard his message. that's how we know that he listens to our hamd. Once again you can see this perfect harmony between heart tongue and limbs. And now that we believe and affirm. that Allah does listen to our Hamd. therefore what comes next?. ربنا لک الحمد. Our Rabb. we praise you. and we are grateful to you. and with that affirmation. we fall into sajda. which is a GREATER form of humility. It is complete physical submission. And then in that state of submission we express why we are submitting.
سبحان ربی الاعلی و تعالی. because my Rabb is lofty and almighty. And what do you do before someone who you believe is lofty and almighty?. You submit your essence. your intellect to them. which is the act of placing your forehead on the ground. because the head contains the essence of all 5 senses. If you remember the word Sajda. it means when a camel lowers itself before its master. submitting and relinquishing control of its movements to its master.
And then if you notice. sajda. is the MOST vulnerable state from a physical stand point. Because our head is on the ground. we can no longer see who is around us. who is behind us. If somebody attacks us. we have no way of knowing. If someone is talking to us. or about us. we cannot know. because our face is on the ground with both hands on the side. Why is that?. Because سبحان ربی الاعلی و تعالی.  My Rabb is lofty and all might. He is lofty. so I don't care about anyone talking to me. or about me. I am not going to be distracted by the enticement of this world anymore. He is almighty. so he will protect me from my enemies. my troubles. my sorrows. my anxieties. I don't have to worry about it. My Rabb will take care of me. Its complete physical submission. So Salaah is the perfect expression of hamd. unifying belief of the heart. speech of the tongue. and actions of the limbs.  Its incredible.

Now if you take this same analogy and apply it to life. take it to the next level. the entire salaah is a state of rest. and the time BETWEEN the two prayers. is the time of motion. Salaah is like a charger for the soul. When you charge your phones. ideally you're not using it while its charging. right?. But why are you charging it?. So that you can USE it when its off the cradle. Isn't that true?. So Salaah is charging the soul. It is reminding our soul of our Hamd at all three levels. At the level of belief. at the level of speech. and at the level of action. But when salaah is over. its now time to put all of that energy to use. in our daily activities. During salaah I say.
سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ. سبحان ربی الاعلی وتعالی. اللہ اکر. ربنا لک الحمد
These are all claims aren't they?. I'm making all these claims standing before Allah in Salaah!. But where am I going to prove. that I really believe what I'm claiming to believe?. In the world. in school. in my house. at my job. in my dealings with people. with my parents. with my teachers. in my dealings with my own self. That's where I'm going to prove it.

But then when I'm in the world proving my beliefs. I am incurring MORE blessings of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . Not just that . because this world is an extremely challenging place for a believer. to ACT out our beliefs. because of all these distractions around us. So despite our best efforts. we make mistakes. and our soul becomes weak by the constant challenges. our battery gets drained. And so what did Allah give us after a few hours?. Another salaah. Time to recharge again. Time to be grateful again. Remind ourselves of our purpose again. Revitalize our beliefs. make those same claims again. And then when that salaah is over. get back into the world. and start proving those claims true again. And it goes on an on.  It's really amazing.
And this is why a true momin. is ALWAYS in the state of salaah. When he's not before Allah. affirming his beliefs and making claims. he's in the world proving those claims to be true. And when he is not ACTION. he is reminding himself of HAMD through Salaah. This Salaah is an amazing gift to us. this is why Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) says.

إِنَّ ٱلْإِنسَنَ خُلِقَ هَلُوعًا
No doubt about it. Human being has been created in a state of anxiety. He's always anxious. His heart is never at rest. He is easily disturbed.
‏إِذَا مَسَّهُ ٱلشَّرُّ جَزُوعًۭا
The moment a hardship touches him. he screams
‏وَإِذَا مَسَّهُ ٱلْخَيْرُ مَنُوعًا ‎
And when something good happens to him. he becomes miserly
‏إِلَّا ٱلْمُصَلِّينَ
Except the ones who pray.
‏ٱلَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَىٰ صَلَاتِهِمْ دَآئِمُونَ
Except the ones who are CONSTANTLY in the state of prayer. They are in the state of salaah during prayer. they are in the state of salaah when they're out in the world.

In the last session. we took a granular look at HAMD. I explained how appreciating a blessing. praise. makes us desire the benefit. And then when we benefit from the blessing. we feel the need to be grateful to the benefactor. And TRUE gratitude for a blessing. is to use it for its intended purpose. Then I explained how HAMD is split between the 3 parts of human activity. the heart. the tongue and the limbs. In today's session. I want to take a step back. and talk about how we get to actually get to appreciation. Because if we are unable to appreciate something. we cannot praise it. which mean we will be unable to benefit from it. and therefore never be grateful for it.


Scholars say that the recognition of a blessing begins with knowledge.العلم. And knowledge is defined as. Understanding the true reality of something. معرفتُ الحقیقۃ. Being aware of the true reality of something is knowledge. Now appreciation begins with the knowledge of 2 things. Knowledge of a NEED. and knowledge of THAT. which fulfills the need. When these two pieces come together. we develop what is called. a TRUE appreciation for that thing. Scholars then make a further distinction between superficial appreciation. and TRUE appreciation. For example. We KNOW. that HUNGER indicates a NEED for the body. And we also know. that FOOD will satiate that hunger. That is why we appreciate food as a blessing. But then despite that knowledge. why do we waste food?. Because we're certain that there will be more food tomorrow. So what? if I throw away half the stuff on my plate today. I know I can buy more tomorrow. But if you go to one of these starving countries. I guarantee you they don't think that way. Why?. Because even though they have the same NEED as I do. they have VERY limited resources. If *I* skip meals. its because I'm dieting. When they skip meals. its because they're starving. So to them. HUNGER is VERY REAL. and that's why FOOD. is a TRUE blessing to them. But for me. Hunger is NOT that big a deal. Therefore FOOD is not such a big deal. So you can see how NEED. drives appreciation. And you can apply this to all aspects of your life. It holds true for anything in life. You go to school to learn. If that NEED to learn is REAL. If you have that THIRST for knowledge. you'll naturally appreciate your teachers. you'll appreciate the education. because they are instruments that can fulfill your need. Same applies to work. friends. to parents. and it certainly holds true for Allah and his religion. 

And so this reality has been placed in this verse we're studying الحمد للہ رب العالمین. Who is the Hamd for?. It is for Allah. Why?. because he is Rabb. Rabb of what?. العالمین. Because a Marboob NEEDS his RABB. Remember our conversation about relationships?. Children NEED parents. for parenting to take place. Students NEED teachers for learning to take place. Slave NEEDS a master for direction. Every effect NEEDS its cause. So in this verse. Alameen is the effect. that necessitates the existence of a RABB. a cause. And this why the the ALEEM created the AALAM. to manifest and reflect his attributes so that WE could become aware of the reality that HE is our Rabb. And this is why if you look at these three words. ALAM. ALIM. and ALEEM. they all share the same root word. علم .

Now just like all human activity is divided in 3 components. the heart. the tongue and the limbs. Knowledge also has 3 levels. The first is the knowledge of operation or function. How does a THING operate?. How does it function?. Then the second level. is knowledge of structure. What are the different components involved in the function of this entity. and how do they all come together. in a very particular order. to accomplish its function. And then finally there is knowledge of INTENT. WHY?. WHY are all these components designed this way?. What were the factors that led to the creation of this entity?. Why this material?. Why this shape?. These are all questions related to essential knowledge. INTENT.
From an Islamic theology stance. these 3 levels are called. Islam. Iman and Ehsaan. But I don't want to get technical. I want to keep keep things really simple. We'll call them. Functional Knowledge (which is Islam). Structural Knowledge (which is Eman). and Essential Knolwedge (which is Ehsaan).

Lets look at a very simple example to understand this. Let's use my usual example of a phone. It all has to begin with a NEED. So I realize this NEED. to communicate with my friends and family. I walk into Best Buy and I explain my need to the salesman. I tell him. You know. I don't know what it is. But I have this strong urge to talk to my friends across the world. And this need is keeping me up at nights. I don't know what to do. Please help me. And so he takes me to the phone section. hands me this rectangular device and says. THIS is what you need. it's called a PHONE. And I'm like huh?. Really?. This THING is what'll help me communicate with my friends?. How do I use it?.
Now when I say. How do I use it?. What level of knowledge am I seeking?. That's operational knolwedge. right?
So he turns the phone on. and he starts demonstrating how this device works. Now when he's teaching me how to use this phone. if we simplify things. what are the broad categories his teachings fall under?. The Requisites. The How To's. and Dos and Don'ts. That's it. right?
What are the Requisites?. You are absolutely required to charge your phone before you can use it. In order to do that you have to have a power outlet that uses a specific type of socket. that outputs a certain amount of voltage. You HAVE to have that to use this phone.
Second. This is how you use it. This is how you turns it on. This is how you turn it off. This is how you dial a number. This is how you download an app.
Finally. These are the things you do and these are the things you don't do. Keep the phone dry. don't take it swimming with you. It's delicate so don't use it as a door stopper. don't try to hammer a nail into the wall with it. Keep the phone clean. don't use it as a dinner plate. especially if it is PLUS size. If it gets dirty. wipe it with a clean cloth. You don't have to put it in the washing machine and then the dryer. twice. So that's dos and don'ts.
That's it. Those are the 3 categories of operational knowledge. The Requisites. How to use it. and the Dos and Donts. If you do these things. this instrument will satisfy your need. to communicate with your friends and family.

Now we know. that internally. every phone is made up of certain components that are structurally placed a certain way. There is a battery. a circuit board. a camera. microphone. memory. CPU. Now these are all completely different. completely independent components. Yet they are arranged in a VERY specific manner. to accomplish one single goal. Allow me to use the phone. If I change anything in that structure. the phone will no longer work. right?. So this is all structural knowledge. or component level knowledge. 
Now do I need to know any of this to operate the phone?. NO. I just need the operational knowledge. right?. How to turn it on. how to dial a number. and talk. I don't need to know the techincal details of how things are working under the hood.
Who needs to know those kinds of details?. The phone repair guy. a technician needs to know that. right?. So that when it stops working. he can fix it. Because that is the level of NEED. he operates at. He NEEDS to have the knowledge of structure. what goes where!. how each individual component works. But you and I don't. Because we're operating at the consumer level. The repairman on the other hand. is operating at a higher level of knowledge. But when he makes calls. despite his additional knowledge. does he use the phone EXACTLY the same way as me?. ABSOLUTELY. But at the same time. does he have a much greater appreciation for how the phone works?. Of course. Hes has a much greater awareness. and a much greater appreciation for it.
Where I'll say things like. look how beautiful the icons look on this phone. He'll say things like. Actually. these are 24bit pixels being illuminated from this light source in the back. and each pixel is capable of showing 10 million colors. right?. Completely different levels of appreciation. My point is. EVEN though he and I will use the phone in EXACTLY the same way. because of his knowledge of structure and components. he can appreciate things about this same phone which I cannot.

And then there is the designer. The guy who actually designed each and every component of this phone. This is the guy who designed the circuit board. the camera. the microphone. the screen. and then puts all these things together in this particular order. Now this guy is operating a COMPLETLEY different level. He has an appreciation of the phone. which you and I can't even imagine right?.
If I say. look how beautiful the icons look on this phone. and the technician says. these are 24bit pixels being illuminated. THIS guy says. let me tell you WHY I designed it this way. Why I used 24 bit colors and not 32 bit colors. Let me tell you why I used copper here. and a plastic there. Let me show you all the things I put into place just to get this one component working. Let me tell you how this technology evolved from here. and what I'm planning to do 10 years from now.
This is the level of INTENT. Where the designer is actually letting you enter his head. And when we understand his thought process. now we have an appreciation like never before. And who do we actually appreciate THROUGH the appreciation of the phone?. The designer himself right?. DUDE! You're a genuis. This is such PERFECT design. It's AMAZING.
But now when it comes to using this phone. Does the DESIGNER also use the phone. EXACTLY the same way as the technician does. and as we do?. ABSOLUTELY.

So you see. at the operational level. at the level of Islam. functionally. we are all the same. We all do the EXACT same things. From  Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) to Maulana Ali. to Imams. to Duaat. to Manaseeb. we ALL perform salaah EXACTLY the same way. We're all the same on the level of function.
But when it comes to the inner realms of knowledge. at the structure and design level. what we get are ranks. or MARAATIB. one technician will know more than the other. But no matter WHO knows HOW much. all levels of knowledge exist to serve one. and one purpose alone. OPERATION of the instrument.
Think about it. What was the INTENT of the designer when he was designing the phone?. Was it just the design of the phone. or was it its USE?. It was usage right?. If he put this AMAZING. MIND BLOWING. design together. Used the BEST possible material for the components. Arranged it in the BEST possible way. But nobody used it. Would any of it matter?. NO. So INTENT and STRUCTURE. are all geared towards one single purpose. its USE. Because it is ONLY the actual USE of the device. that will bring about the benefit. Only by USING the phone. will I satisfy my NEED. to communicate with friends and family. You understand?. So if I have ALL the knowledge that exists about the phone. But I don't actually USE the phone. I will not benefit from it. And on the other hand if I ONLY have the operational knowledge of phone. and I know nothing more than that. I will still benefit from it. IF i put it it to use. So in the end what it boils down to. is ACTION.

Isn't that what we said about our existence?. There is the heart that holds the intent. the highest level of knowledge. Then there is the tongue. which provides structure to the intent. How?. See a thought. a desire. or an intention. These are all just mental images. They don't have any particular structure. But when we speak. we give that intent. the structure of words. Isn't that what speech is?. It is structured words. in a particular sequence based on grammatical rules. You break that structure. and you can no longer deliver the intent. And then finally. there are the limbs. which are tools of operation. They are the dos and donts of the intent. they are the prerequisites to EXECUTE the intent. They physically execute the intent. And in the final analysis. it is ACTION. and not words or intent that is considered EVIDENCE. It is ACTION. and not words or intent that provides BENEFIT. right?. It is the ablity to communicate with the phone. and not its structure or its design that matters.
AND YET. intent and speech. contribute to the strength and the quality of my action. The stronger my intention. the stronger my belief. the more eloquent. the more powerful my speech will be. And that will translate into a LOT MORE effort in the quality of my action. So you see. even though these are 3 different things. in essence they are the same thing. When all three things combine. When the heart believes. And the tongue articulates what the heart believes. And the limbs ACT upon what the tongue claimed about the heart's belief. THAT's when you get PERFECTION in action. This is why a true believer.  is defined as the one who comprises all three things.
تصدیقٌ بالجنان. قولٌ بالسان. و عملٌ بالارکان
A PERFECT believer is the one who believes in his heart. articulates that belief with his tongue. and ACTS upon that belief with his limbs. In other words there is absolutely NO contradiction. NO conflict between his belief. his speech and his actions. They're all the same.

Now understanding these levels of knowledge. if we look at the ALAM. the whole idea becomes to REVERSE ENGINEER it. Because when we study the ALAM. what we see. is how it works. how it functions. So we study how it operates. to understand its structure. so that we can understand the INTENT of the creator. Because every. THING. شئی. has within it. the مشیئا. and the منشاء. the WILL. and the INTENT of its creator.

If you think about our phones. We are all using them. in this particular way. BECAUSE that was the مشیئا. and the منشاء. the WILL. and the INTENT of its designer. If we reverse engineer the phone. we connect its operation. to the structure of the components. we can determine the will of its designer. The reason everything is structured this way. is BECAUSE. this is how the designer INTENDED for me to use it. And then the user manual confirms that.

So the idea is. study the operations. and the structure of this ALAM. through the manual of the Quran. to understand the INTENT of the RABB. Now when we look at this universe. just like a phone or any other devise. this AALAM is comprised on many different components. But desipite these complete disparate components. it is acting as a single entity. with one UNIFIED purpose. To serve human beings. And if PRAISE is understanding the purpose. and gratitude is ACTING FOR that intended purpose. then EVERYTHING in nature is in a state of HAMD. Because everything understands its purpose. and it does EXACTLY what its supposed to do. which is to serve me. make life possible for me. This is what I learn from my study of how this world is operating.
Which then forces me to think. I TOO am a creation. just like them. Therefore I must ALSO have a purpose. I must also have a HAMD. What is my HAMD?. What is MY praise?. What is MY gratitude?. Because I am a fully functioning. fully operational unit. comprised of all these independent components. I have not only been given the gift of sight through my eyes. I have ALSO been given the gifts of scenery. All the things around me that I can see. I have ALSO been given light. the medium which enables me to SEE things. Again 3 things. The ability to see. the objects that CAN be seen. and the medium through which I can see them. Similarly I have not only been given the gift of hearing. I have also been given the gift of sounds in this world. and the medium of AIR. which enables me to hear these sounds.
I know I did not work for any of these things. Therefore by definition. these are all gifts. And I realize that all these GIFTS. they have a very specific structure to them. My eyes exist in the top part of my face. What if it was in my belly?. Would I be able to see the world the same way as I do today. What if I had one eye on my forehead. would that limit my vision?. Because of how they are placed. my eyes provide me with a linear line of sight. with some peripheral vision. but my ears gives me access to sounds in a complete circular fashion. 360 degrees. because they're placed on the side of my head. What if they were placed on my feet?. or anywhere else except where they are right now?. How would that have worked out for me?. And then why is everything been placed in such a perfect balance?. EVERYTHING that exists on the sides. inside and outside my body. they exist in pairs. And EVERYTHING that exists in the center. stands alone. We have one brain. one nose. one mouth. one neck. one heart. one belly button. one genetal. because they're all in the center. And everything on the side exists in pairs. whether internal or external. eyes. lungs. kidneys. arms. feet. Anything that's on the side. if one side fails. I can still survive using the other. Anything in the center fails. that's it for me. This is INCREDIBLE structure. My eyes can see all the way to the horizon?.  Why can't my ears hear sounds. as far as my eyes can see things. Why can't my nose smell things as far as my ears can hear sounds?. Why can't me tongue taste as far as my nose can smell?. Why do I have this gradual degradation within my senses?. Are these capabilities placed within me to benefit me or harm me?. There is a book in which Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq explains human design to his Dai Hazrat Mufaddal. All his arguments prove one thing. Every creation on this planet has been given EXACTLY what they needed. Not less and not more. Because any less and it would have hurt them. and ANY more and it would have hurt them. There is SO MUCH wisdom in this design. I see everything has been put into place. very systematically. PERFECTLY. to benefit me.

So now that I realize I have been given SO MANY gifts. that are uncountable. invaluable. and ALL good. انا اعطیناک الکوثر. No doubt about it. we have given you Kausar. Why are these Kausar for me?. Because I now have the KNOWLEDGE of how much I NEED these gifts. And what a disaster it would be. if I even LOST one of these gifts. Forget losing. How much would I suffer if any of these gifts even deteriorated. Therefore. ALLAHUAKBAR. It is clearly BEYOND my ability to praise Allah for these amazing gifts. He is BEYOND my ability to be grateful to him for these incredible gifts. So what do I do now?. فصل لربک والنحر. Establish Salaah for your Rabb. and sacrifice.

For the one who REALIZES. the NEED. to praise Allah. For the one who realizes. that he has a NEED to be grateful to Allah. for such a person. these forms of worship. are a TRUE blessing. Because they help him satiate that NEED. that HUNGER. to be grateful to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). But for the one who is ungrateful. For someone who is stuck in the filth of this DUNIYA. who is stuck at the level of the physics chemistry and biology of THINGS. and cannot see anything else beyond that. All he knows is to use these gifts to pursue vain pleasures. chase empty desires.
For the one completely obsessed with himself. his money. his youth. his beauty. his cars. his business. his children. Who believes HE is the creator of his destiny. who believes HE is his own ILAAH. For such a person. worship means ABSOLUTELY nothing. Salaah means NOTHING to such a person. It is as valuable to him. as a phone is valuable to a monkey. Because he has no knowledge. He has no knowledge of his NEED. and so he is not even going to bother looking for THAT instrument. that can satisfy his need.

I was talking to one of the kids the other day. and she told me she's studying how nerve endings work in school. and how these signals are transmitted to the brain when we touch something. And she said. I turned to my friends and said. How can this be without design?. How can this be evolution?. And I felt SO happy. I immediately remembered this hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). that a DISBELIEVER is bewildered by creation. but a BELIEVER is bewildered by his creator. 
الکافر حائرٌ فی المخلوق. والمؤمن حائرٌ فی الخالق
Another kid in her class. same intellect. same maturity. receiving the exact same knowledge of design. she would stop at the level of creation. but she saw Allah behind it. SubhanAllah!. Because this is what the RABB AlALAMEEN wants. For us to study and decode this physical ALAM. to SEE the RABB working behind it. So in essence what Yasu said in her own way. is. لا الہ الا اللہ. How can this be from anyone other than Allah?.

You know. it is so INCREDIBLE. that how these Arabs. in their eloquence. they did not call human beings. الحیوان العاقل. The intellectual beings. Instead they called them. الحیوان الناطق. The articulating animal. Or the animal of reason. Because نطق is also the root word for منطق. which means reason or logic. and we need language in order to reason. We can't think without language. If you ever catch yourself thinking. you'll notice you're using your native language to think in. So they called human beings الحیوان الناطق. because of their ability to articulate. Why?. Because Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) granted this ability to speak ONLY to human beings. as a sign. Because if you look at speech. What is speech?. It is encoding and decoding. I am encoding my intent. I'm taking a MEANING. which is spiritual or meta-physical in nature. and I am encoding that into a structure of physical words. You are then listening to those physical words. decoding it. and extracting the meaning from it. SubhanAllah!. And this langugae. this ability to encode and decode. is what we have as the MOST basic level. Why?. Because THAT is the very nature of this AALAM. It is the WORD of Allah. It is encoded in the physical. so that we can decode it. to extract the MEANING. the meta-physical from it. which is purpose of its creation. Talk about clear signs.

So now if we look at salaah. or any other form of worship for that matter. It is also a physical THING. It is شئی. It belongs to the world of worship. Its from عالم العبادۃ. It's an instrument. and instrument satisfy needs. What is that need that it was built for?. HAMD. Salaah is the food. for the hunger and thirst of HAMD. Our internal NEED for HAMD is what drives us towards Salaah. I cannot emphasize this enough. People ask. why do I need to pray?. It's VERY simple. Are you grateful to your Rabb?. Do you feel the NEED to express your gratitude to him. in a way THAT would make HIM happy?. Then salaah is your answer. It's really that simple.

This is how a believer judges his own gratitude. If you want to know whether you're grateful or not. measure yourself against salaah. Look!. whether I want to talk to you or not. is determined by whether I use my phone or not. correct?. If I really want to talk to you. I'll pick up the phone and I'll call you. If I'm hungry. I'll eat. If I'm thirsty. I'll drink. That's how I know I was thirsty. because I ENJOYED the drink. I know I was REALLY hungry. because I ENJOYED the food. I know I really wanted to talk to you. because I ENJOYED the conversation. If you want to know whether you're grateful to Allah for KAUSAR or not. see if you enjoy SALAAH.
I personally feel this is such a blessing from Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) that he gave us these tools to measure ourselves against. Because we are delusional creatures. We THINK we love. We THINK we're just. We THINK we believe. How do we know for sure?. These are the standards that Allah set for us. These are like symptoms for us. How does a doctor diagnose a physical problem?. through symptoms. right?. If I have a fever. along with a sore throat and runny nose. I clearly have diabetes. LOL. Good thing I didn't go into medicine. 
Knowledge of symptoms. are such an enormous blessing from Allah. Because if we didn't have these symptoms. how would we ever fix the problem? right?. So if I'm feeling this repulsion from Salaah. something is wrong with my HAMD. That's what I need to work on. This is where people go wrong. When someone is not motivated for prayers. they start forcing them with وعید. threats of hellfire. punishment. force. beating. But does that really work?. It doesn't. Because you're not addressing the root cause. HAMD. The question to ask is. why is this person not in NEED of HAMD. What is he missing?. Because HAMD is the MOST natural thing for a human being. You just have to get them there. Once that thirst develops. salaah is just a natural response to it.

Now let's look at the 3 levels of knowledge in the context of religion. The first is شریعۃ. which is the knowledge of operation and function. And this is all about Huqooq (Rights). It begins with Huqooq Allah. The Rights of Allah. These are all the forms of worship. and matters that are related to dealings between the ABD and his Rabb.
Then you have Huqooq AlNafs. Rights of the soul. These cover topics like personal hygine. and day to day etiquettes. how to eat. how to sleep. how to talk. what to say what not to say. how to use the bathroom. what to see. what not to see. What to heart. what not to hear. Basically all rules related to the body and soul.
Then you have Huqooq AlIbaad. Human Rights. These are all related to dealings and interactions with others. These cover laws of marriage. inheritance. politics. contracts. trade. economics. judicial matters. etc.
It's interesting that this word Shareeah. comes from شارع. which means road. But شریعۃ is not just any road. It is a specific road that leads to water. Imagine the Arab desert. scorching heat. blazing sun. extremely dry weather. What could possible be the GREATEST of all blessings for an Arab in the desert?. Water right?. So to them this life. this world was like a hot scorching desert. which in their case. it literally was. And Aakhira or jannah was like a body of cool water.
Now when you're driving on any road. there are laws to be obeyed. for example speed limits. right of way. And these laws are set by a governing body.which are all covered by Huqooq Allah. Then YOU are the one actually taking the journey. so you need to apply certain rules for yourself. like for example. seat belts. check your side mirrors. rearview mirrors. Make sure your car is clean. It is well serviced. well maintained. You've filled it up with gas. These are all covered by Huqooq AlNafs. And then there are all these people travelling besides you on the road. There are rules of interacting with them. right of way. slow lane. fast lane. signal when you're turning. These are all covered by Huqooq AlIbaad (Human rights). So to the Arabs. if they followed the Shareeah. if they abided by these three rights. Rights of Allah. Rights of Self. and Rights of others. it would guarantee. that they would ALL. successfully reach water.

Now everything dictated by shareeah. they're all physical actions. no matter what category of Huqooq you take. They are all physical actions. instruments. Which means they all have prerequisites. they all have dos and don'ts. and they all have How Tos. So if you take salaah as an example. its operational knowledge would be. understanding its pre-requisites. Taharah. That's the first pre-requisite. THEN complete wudu. These are ABSOLUTELY required things. You want to charge the phone battery. you gotta plug the charger in the wall. You may not understand HOW or WHY the charger is charging the phone. but you know it WILL definitely charge. Wudu literally creates that connection. It plugs you into the spiritual socket.
Now Wudu is its own THING. Which means it has its own set of pre-requisites. How Tos and Dos and Dont's.
Then there are the do's and donts of salaah. You can do certain things. and you can't do certain things. You have to recite Surah Fateha. but then you have a choice to recite which ever surah you like after that. You have to do ruku with the tasbeeh. but then you can extend the ruku with other tasbeeh as much as you want. You can't look away from the sajda. you can't speak with anyone. you can't read anything. These are all the How To's of salaah. This is how this instrument works. Makes sense?. Why do I have to do Salaah?. To express my Hamd. How do I operate this instrument called Salaah?. Meet the pre-requisites. follow the dos and don'ts. Keep your hands inside the janemaaz at all times. Simple.

Now once you've gained an understanding of the Shareeah. Once you've gained the knowledge of the NEED to HAMD. and you've gained the knowledge of THAT which will fulfill your need. which is Shareeah.  You're on the road that will lead you to water. You have a direction. you know what you need for you YOURSELF. and how to interact with others. Once you've perfected the outward form. the next level of knowledge is. علم التاویل. The knowledge of Taveel. This is the knowledge of the components. and what they represent. The Misaal and the Mamsool. The symbol and the one it symbolizes. So for example in wudu. why are there certain parts I must wash. and then others that I only have to do masah on?. What does washing symbolize?. What does Masah symbolize?. When I wash my face. why should I put water in my eyes?. In salaah. what does Rukoo symbolize. what does Sajda symbolize. what does Qayaam symbolize. And how are they all connected together. Why Qayam comes first. then rukoo. then sajda. Why is there one rukoo and two sajda. Why is it that I spread my fingers on my knee when I'm in Rukoo. but I bring them together when I'm in sajda. All of this falls under the knowledge of Taveel.
The word taweel means. رجع الی الاول. returning to the beginning. How it all started. And how do you do that?. How do you get to the beginning?. But tracing back the symbols to the ones they symbolize. By decoding the external physical form. to understand what they represent in their counterpart. their interal spiritual form. The external forms are all signs. ayaats. Misaal. They point to the Mamsoolaat. And you trace one sign after the other. and that's how you get to where it all started. The awwal. It is listerally a bridge that connects the Shareeah. to its purpose.
التاویل جَسَرَ الحقائق
Taweel. is the bridge that leads to realities. But if you have not practiced. and mastered the external form. how are you going to understand the internal represenations?. If you don't know the symbols. how are you going to get to the symbolized?. You can't do calculus without learning algebra right?. Can't run until you learn how to walk. you'll fall.

So Taveel connects you to this third level of knowledge. which is the knowledge of the ESSENCE. or the INTENT. It is the knowledge of how it all began. and how it will all end. The knowledge of pre-existence. and eternity. What happened before this physical universe came into existence. What were the factors that led to the creation of this physicality. Why did all of this come into existence. where did it come from. where is it going. how will it all end. WHEN will it all end. What are the realities of these oceans. these trees. the celestial bodies.  That's all covered by the knowledge of the origin. and the return. Mabdaa and Maad.

Shareeah gave us knowledge of the form. Taveel helped us return to the beginning. by tracing the components to their design. Mabda Maad. is how and why these components originated. why they were made this way. why they have this form. this shape. and how will this all return back to where it came from. And then just as in the study of matter today. we can study things at a molecular level. at an atomic level. at a sub-atomic level. There are also realms of knowledge that explain each composition at an extremely minute level. So then you have haqaiq. After that you have Daqaiq. After that you have Haqaiq Alyia. After that you have Daqaiqul Daqaia. After that you have Ifaadaat. So you can see there is no end to knowledge.

And BTW how do you verify all these 3 levels of knowledge?. How do you prove to yourself that these concepts are not made up fictitious stuff?. Because you can't use the physical universe to prove them. Mabda Maad is a realm of knowledge BEFORE physicality even existed. So how to you know for sure that all of this is true?. The Quran. EVERY single thing can be proven from the Quran. Hazrat Zia Ali Sahab used to say. The ignorant thinks the Quran is just a book of stories. But the AALIM knows that its a book of Haqaiq and Daqaiq.


I hope. I've given you SOME clarity on how all of this is organized. and the importance of a systematic. progressive study. I know a lot of people. who've studied a little bit of this. a little bit of that. and a ultimately a whole lot of nothing. This is because they just study randomly. little bit from here. little bit from there. So that's what they end up with. Random knowledge. confusions. So you have to study systematically. but that takes a lot of patience.
And BTW. where do these sessions fit into this?. All I'm hoping to do in these sessions. is show you the way to get you from the scorching sands of the desert. to this road that will lead you to water. I hope and pray. I'm getting you to the شارع. But there is a LONG LONG road ahead of you. You HAVE to learn Shareeah. before you learn TAVEEL. before you learn Mabda Maad. It's a LONG journey. But I can tell you from personal experience. WALLHI.It's an AMAZING journey. But I can only get you to the road. You're the one who has to walk on it. We all have our own walking to do. And walking. is a PHYSICAL act. It is not a verbal claim. and it is not a good intention. It is physical work.
 

For those of you who have time. I want to share 4 things. that have really helped me improve my salaah. And I hope that InshaAllah it does the same for you.

The first and foremost is. REMEMBER why you are praying. remember the purpose of this instrument. We appreciate Allah's blessings. and we NEED to express our gratitude to him. and the tool given to us. to statisfy that NEED of HAMD. is salaah. That is the ONLY reason to pray.
But then while we're perfecting our prayers. through daily practice. we also need to make an effort to study taveel and mabda maad. because what these uloom do is. they increase our CONVICTION of HAMD. They raise the intensity of Hamd in our hearts. They make us more appreciative. more grateful for Allah's blessings. Look. from Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) to Maulana Ali. to Imams. to Duaat. to manaseeb. to us. we're all doing the EXACT same salaah. But the quality of conviction is different at each level. And what gives strength to that conviction. is these higher realms of knowledge. The MORE you know. the more THIRSTY you will be HAMD. and the more you will want to drink from this fountain of salaah. So that's my first recommendation. Study. Make that effort. I promise you it will be a rewarding one. Begin by studying the Shareeah. and perfecting the outward.

Shareeah. even though the most precious thing we have. it is the most undervalued entity in our lives
It teaches us discipline. love. patience. courage. ettiquettes. hiearrchy. ADAB. It teaches us all the divine attributes.
Designed and formulated by Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . He witnessed the spiritual world. and designed Shareeah on the same pattern for us.



Then the next thing is. Understand what you say in salaah. You don't have to be a master of Arabic for that. All translations are available. I have translated pretty much all the duas for you. Make an effort to understand them sentence by sentence. And to begin. Begin with your rukoo and and sujood. Slow them down. Some of you guys pray so fast. I'm sure it starts a hurricane somewhere. No wonder texas gets so many hurricanes. Its because of your rukoo and sujood. When you go into rukoo. the person standing next to you gets hit with a wind. SWOOSH. LOL. Slow down. At least slow down your rukoo and your sujood. Start there. Visualize your HAMD when you're in RUKU. Subhana Rabi alazeem wabihamdih. My Rabb is SO perfect and amazing. and he is worthy of all praise and gratitude. Subhana Rabbiyal Aala wataala. My Rabb is so lofty and so mighty. Reflect on these words. Do this JUST for your FARZ. forget the rest. Just FRAZ.  That's not much to do right?. But reflect on these words. These are EXTREMELY powerful words. SubhanAllah and AlHamdulillah. They are the MOST beloved words to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) said in a hadees.
کلِمَتَینْ. خَفِیفَتَینِ عَلی الِّسَانْ. ثَقِیلَتَینِ فِی المِیزَانْ. حَبِیبَتَینِ اِلَی الرَّحمٰنْ
Two words. کلِمَتَینْ. SubhanAllah and AlHamdulillah. خَفِیفَتَینِ عَلی الِّسَانْ. Extremely Light on the tongue.
ثَقِیلَتَینِ فِی المِیزَانْ. Extremely Heavy on the scales on the day of judgment.
حَبِیبَتَینِ اِلَی الرَّحمٰنْ. Extremely beloved to the Rehman.

And we're constantly repeating these words in our tasbeehaat. So start there. and slowly make an effort to expand that out. Understand the surahs. then the tashahhud. and then expand. It will help a LOT with your focus. This is the reason why we lose focus. Because we don't know what we're saying. If I started doing these sessions in Urdu right now. how long will it take. before those of you who don't understand Urdu. how long before you pass out?. Few minutes right?. That's what happens in salaah. we begin with this enthusiasm. and then we zonk out. because we don't know what we're saying. So that's my second suggestion.

The next thing is make salaah an EVENT in your life. Salaah and ALL forms of worship are NOT meant to be an activity. they are meant to be an experience. We have to learn to experience our salaah. Prepare for it. think about it in advance. When you wake up in the morning to go to school. Do you just roll out of bed and head out to school?. Actually I know some of you do. LOL. But hopefully there are some. who actually prepare for school. Parents. when you get ready to go to work. you don't just get up and walk out right?. You shower. you dress up. and then you head out. Because work is a really important thing. isn't it?.
Well guess what?. Salaah is a MUCH MORE important thing. Allah. our RABB. is a very important entity. Orepare for him. Dress up for him. A person who is praying in his Tshirts and Pajamas. CLEARLY does not understand what he's doing. If you're doing that. especially for Fajr. you have ABSOLUTELY NO idea who you're standing before and what you're doing. Cause I guarantee you. you would not show up to work and stand before your boss in that outfit. The outfit that you're standing in. before ALLAH.
Some say. oh its not haraam. Its pure 100% cotton. so techincally I can pray in it. Well techincally it's not illegal for you. to show up to work in your bathrobe and slippers. is it?. If technicality is all that matters. then show up like that to work. You won't get arrested. Why don't you?. Because you know your boss will not like that. it is disrespectful to him. Well Salaah. is not meeting your boss. it is not meeting your teacher. it is meeting your creator. your Rabb. Be mindful of that. It'll completely change your experience of salaah. Start thinking about salaah. and start preparing for it in advance. Before you begin your day. check the timings for all prayers. and plan your day accordingly. Make it a priority in your life. It's like anything else in life. If you make it important. it WILL become important. It's all up to you.
And try not to pray late. Pray in the earlier portion of the time. Understand that it's our RABB that is calling us. What'll happen if I show up to work 45 minutes late everyday. and tell my boss. Oh you know.  the second I wanna leave.  my son wraps himself around my leg and starts crying. that's why I come in late everyday. It's SO cute I'll show you a video next time. I don't think my boss will find that cute. If it makes sense to not keep my boss waiting. then how can it make sense to keep my master. my Rabb waiting?. so try your best to pray at the earliest time possible. I promise you it'll change your experience of salaah. I understand it's not always easy to do that with our work and life styles. But atleast try to do the best you can.
I always remind myself of this fact. that a dog. chewing on a bone. What's the MOST pleasurable delight in the world to a dog. a bone. But when its master calls. it drops the bone and comes running to its master. So how is it then. that my glorious master. RABB AlALAMEEN. He calls me. حی علی الصلوۃ. حی علی الفلاح. and I just keep doing what I'm doing. ignoring him completely?. May Allah protect me from falling to a level. which would make a dog look better than me.

And finally. measure your salaah by the time you spend when you're NOT in salaah. This is the HARDEST PART. for ALL of us. Make an effort to be obedient to Allah. And this is where you will see the effects of your salaah. Every instrument in the world. has a definitive result. right?. How do I know your knife is working properly. because it cuts. A microwave is working properly. if the food is coming out hot. My phone is working properly. if I'm able to communicate with people. EVERY instrument has a definitive result. What is the result of salaah?. How do you know your salaah is working?. Is it some special tingly feeling in your chest while you're in prayer?. No. that's heart burn.
Where do the effects of salaah show up?. When you're not in salaah. TAQWAA. Consciousness of the presence of Allah in your life. If you are thinking more and more about your Rabb. while you're in school. while you're at work. If your sins. your evil actions are constantly eating at you. they disgust you. if your good actions for the sake of Allah are beginning to please you. KNOW that your salaah is working. But even after praying 5 times a day. all you're doing is lying. cheating. gossiping. back biting. hurting peoples feelings. using foul language. watching filth on the internet. then you're not really praying. EVEN if you're going through the motions. Something is VERY  wrong there. If the power outlet in the wall is working. and the charger is working fine. but the phone is still not charging. Where's the problem?. The phone battery. right?. The battery is dead. You can't show up to salaah with a dead heart and expect salaah to charge it for you. Evil acts. Sins. they KILL the heart. Allah says.
وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ ۖ إِنَّ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ تَنْهَىٰ عَنِ ٱلْفَحْشَآءِ وَٱلْمُنكَرِ
Establish prayer. No doubt about it. salaah prevents you from evil and ludeness. And the word INNA is used there. which means DEFINITELY. ABSOLUTELY. NO DOUBT IT. Salaah prevents you from evils and shamelessness. So if someone is praying. and still engaged in shameful acts. then they're not really praying.

 




 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

Intro

What is love? - benefit. from Hubb. seed


Let me explain gratitude to you. In classical arabic. the word for gratitude is شکر. Even in Urdu you say. شکریہ. in arabic you say. شُکراً. So the tri-literal root for these words is شکر. And you can see that the three letters are connected. There is no gap in between any of these. The first letter sheen. represents the gratitude of the heart or the mind. which is the recognition of the benefit. the second letter represents the tongue praising. or eulogizing the benefactor. and the third letter is fulfilling the purpose of the benefit. So gratitude. or شکر. involves the heart. the tongue and the limbs. When the heart recognizes the benefit. the tongue praises the benefactor. and the limbs get busy with acquiring the benefit as intended by the benefactor.

You insert yourself into the benefit. you start using it for your own benefit. in ways not intended for us. you get شرک. same letters. different sequence.  SubhanAllah! 
that start using the benefit what what's NOT intended. For example. Allah gave me a tongue. to articulate my emotions. and ultimately praise him. But instead I use it to hurt people. I use it to sing stupid songs. I use it to gossip. to backbite. to slander. In other words I corrupt it's purpose. and now what happens. it's no longer gratitude. it's ingratitude. That's why when I change the sequence of the letters in شکر. what do I get?. I get شرک.



And shukar is based on 5 foundations.
1. humility towards the benefactor
2. love for him
3. acknowledgment of the benefit
4. praising the benefactor
5. not using the gift in a manner which the benefactor dislikes.

And what that does is. کَشْرٌ. Same 3 letters?. which means the act of uncovering. or exposing to view. that which was hidden. which is the blessings of Allah. resulting from Shukr.
شَکَر. is when a camels udder fills up with milk to the point that it looks like its going to burst. that's شَکَر. And when the baby camel sucks out the milk from such a full udder. that process is called. شَکِرَۃ. to benefit completely from abundant blessings of Allah. What happens when then the baby sucks drinks the milk?. becomes strong?.


The word begins with the letter. sheen. which is for شئی. And I just told you that. شئی. is the manifestation of the will. شئی. is from مشیئا. OK?. So in this example. Khala's مشیئا. her will was love. and what came out of it. the شئی.  is the meal. which is a manifestation of her love. makes sense?. That's sheen. How many letters after that?. Kaaf and Ra. I won't go into the linguistics of it, because it'll get too complicated and overwhelming. and I'll lose the focus of todays session.
concept of saying "Thank you". of verbalizing the words. "Thank you". it falls under the category of praise. NOT gratitude.

 

Grammatical Analysis

Today we're going to do a linguistic analysis of the words.  الحمد للہ. And there is a two fold purpose to that. The first is that by this analysis we will get to understand the true meaning of Hamd from the Quranic perspective. Because gratitude is a very subjective word. We all can have our own definitions of the word Hamd in our heads. What does Alhamdulilla mean?. Praise belongs to Allah. Gratitude belongs to Allah. Thank you Allah. You're awesome Allah. So there are various mental images of الحمد للہ. And so it becomes that we understand the only definition that actually counts. The only definition that matters. which is what the Quran consideres Hamd. The second purpose is that I want to show you the prefection. in the usage of this word. الحمد للہ. and I want us all to understand. why NO other words could have been used in its place.

As I said earlier. in Arabic. the word Hamd is a composite of two words. The first is المدح which mean praise. And the second is الشکر  which means thanks or gratitude. So then why did Allah not say. المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین. Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah.

Lets begin by understanding the difference between the two words.
You're walking down the street and you see a beautiful car. What you do?. Do you thank it? Or do you praise it?. Hopefully you don't thank it! Hopefully you don't walk up to the car patt it on the hood and say thank you so much BMW. The normal thing to do. would be to praise it . It's a beautiful car! You praise it!. If you go to somebody's house who just had a baby. Do you thank the baby?. Or do you praise the baby?. You praise it!. Oh  what a cute baby! Such a beautiful baby. You don't thank a baby!.

Thanks is something entirely different. Thanks is only done when someone does something for you. If somebody lends you money. you say shukran. If somebody gives you something. if somebody donates to your cause. When somebody helps you with your effort. shows you a kindness. In other words DOES something FOR you. You say thank you. And if you don't say it. you show the person thanks. Because shukar can also be shown. It does not always have to be verbal. And that's why Allah says.
ٱعْمَلُوٓا۟ آلَ دَاوُۥدَ شُكْرًۭا
Show me through your actions that you are grateful. So Shukr or gratitude has to be in return for something nice. something beneficial done for you. Whereas when you see something impressive. When you see something beautiful . When you see something that intrigues you and interests you. you will praise it!

Also understand this distinction. that someone you thank. is not necessarily someone you priase. Now generally in coversation. these two ARE used together. I can say. Thank you so much for doing this for me. you're SO amazing!. In this case I thanked and praised together. But then it is also possible that I can thank someone. but not priase them. Let's think about that for a second. How do you thank someone without actually praising them. Let's look at an example or two from the Quran. You know Moosa AS was raised in a pretty interesting home. Where was he raised?. What was his address?. You know he had a pretty famous address. He is adopted and raised by Firon. Now years later when Moosa AS returns to him and delivers the message of Allah to him. Firon basically says. how dare you? How dare you talk to me this way?
قَالَ أَلَمْ نُرَبِّكَ فِينَا وَلِيدًۭا . وَلَبِثْتَ فِينَا مِنْ عُمُرِكَ سِنِينَ
Did we not raise you as a newborn in this house? Did you not spend many years of your life here? How dare you talk to me like that?. In other words what is Firon saying?. Aren't you what?. Aren't you grateful?. And then Moosa responds.
وَتِلْكَ نِعْمَةٌۭ تَمُنُّهَا عَلَىَّ
That is the favor. you did in fact do for me. Thanks!. That is Moosa AS's way of expressing gratitude. So even though Firon is a guy who will NEVER be praised. The guy will never be praised. especially not by a prophet. But when he does a favor, he will still be what?.  Thanked! Thanks can exist without praise.

Quran  talks about the rights of parents. And Allah says about parents.
أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ إِلَىَّ ٱلْمَصِيرُ
Be grateful to me and both of your parents!
وَإِن جَهَدَاكَ عَلَىٰٓ أَن تُشْرِكَ بِى مَا لَيْسَ لَكَ بِهِۦ عِلْمٌۭ
If your parents are struggling against you. If they are the ones telling you to disbelieve. to commit shirk. Don't obey them. But you still have to be what?. the verse began by saying . but you still have to be grateful to them. In other words if your parents are doing shirk.  Will you praise them? No! You will not praise them. But you still have to be what? You still have to be grateful to them!
Think about Abraham AS. He does not praise what his father does. But he is still thankful to him isn't he?

So the first thing I want you to understand. is that words. الشکر و المدح. praise and gratitude. are two different things. and they are mututally exclusive. Sometimes you can have praise without thanks. And then there are times where you can be grateful to someone. but not praise them. But the word حمد necessarily means both things together!. When Allah says. الحمد للہ. He is saying praise is for Allah. And he is ALSO saying gratitude is for Allah. And he is not just saying one or the other. He is saying that they BOTH exist together.

مدح
Now what if the ayah read. المدح للہ رب العالمین . All praise is for Allah. What would be the problem with that?. The problem with that is. that المدح is praise. that is not always genuine. Praise can be insincere. Let's say you come home with a really bad report card. You walk home and as soon as you enter the house you say.  Mom! OMG. Your cooking smells so delicious.   And she hasn't even started cooking yet. So you're praising her but it's not genuine. You get it?. Praise could be fake. There is fake praise done for kings. for bosses. for judges.  It is done all the time!. People praise physical appearances. You look so beautiful!. That's a false praise. Because you are not worthy of that praise. because YOU did not make you look beautiful. ALLAH made you look beautiful by giving you these features. That's why in Arabic when you praise someone's look. you don't say Hamida. You would say. Madaha. Because it's a false praise. Even though. the time and energy some some women put into makeup. There is this lady in my office. she puts on SO MUCH makeup. So much powder. I always imagine that if I went over and slapped her. there would be like a cloud of powder all around her. LOL
So Madah can be false praise. it can be insincere praise. But Hamd cannot be a false praise. it cannot be insincere. why?. Because Hamd. generates in the heart. by the awareness of the magnificence.  and the glory of the one being praised.  I'll say that again. Hamd. the praise element of hamd. it occurs when the heart becomes aware of the magnificence. and the glory of the one being praised. It is done because of the the knowledge one acquires. about the glory. the brilliance. the greatness of the one that is being praised. It can therefore never be false. Once I gain the knowledge of gravity and exeperience it. I then can never lie about gravity. because I have now witnessed it as a fact. and therefore I do not have a choice but to declare it. Its the realization that if I say gravity does not exist. it does not affect the law of gravity in any way shape or form. gravity will still exist. Only I will get hurt by ignoring and rejecting the principles of gravity. Therefore my statement about gravity can now never be false.
It's the same with Hamd for Allah. He is worthy of praise by the knowledge of who he is through his 99 attributes. Not because you and I are praising him. He is worth of praise. even if there is absolutely no one praising him. He is not dependent on our praise. We are dependent on praising him. He does not need our praise. He does not need our hamd. it is our need that we praise him. the more knowledge we gain about him. about his being. about his 99 attributes. we are forced to turn to him with Hamd. He does not need our hamd at all.


. When you praise somebody and you do not really mean it for example you are praising in order to get something in return that is Madah. Hamd means that O Allah you are worthy of every single ultimate praise because of who you are. Not because of what you have given me. Even if you had not given me anything. Even if I did not exist you would be worthy of being praised . You would be worthy of my Hamd. Not because of what you have done for me but because of who you are.




Or sometimes praise is done just to impress somebody. but you don't necessarily mean it. For example when I go to a job interview and it goes terrible. It was the worst interview I ever had. I absolutely hated the guys that interviewed me. But even then when I am leaving. I say. It was nice meething you. It was not nice meeting him. but I still say that. It's fake praise you understand? So when the word مدح is used. it could be fake. it has the possiblity to be insincere. and that word in itself makes it appropriate for Allah. But HAMD. hamd cannot be insincere. Linquistically the word Hamd can only be used for genuine praise.

Now let's think about شکر . If Allah said الشکر للہ رب العلمین . Which means thanks or gratitude is for Allah. What's the problem with that?. Thanks is ONLY done when you are acknowledging a favor. Something was done for you. and you realize and appreciate that something was done for you. and then you finally thank the one who did the favor for you. You had a flat tire. Somebody came and helped you out. You say thank you! Thanks can only happen when you have a REASON to thank. In other words gratitude is a reaction. Is that clear to everybody?. Thank you is ALWAYS a reaction. Thank you is not something you start with. Ever! . You don't meet somebody just passing by and you say. hey you! thanks!! . You never do that.

When Allah uses the word Hamd. linguistically. this word combines both praise and thanks with certain rules. And the rules are. that praise HAS to be genuine. it can NEVER be fake. it cannot be manufactured. And secondly. gratitude is not reactionary. Therefore linquistically. saying الحمد للہ . is more powerful than saying المدح للہ  and it is more powerful than saying الشکر للہ. It is more comprehensive than both of them. Allah chose something to say. that is better than both of them combined. subhanAllah

Now here's another thing. . In English so far how many words did I have to use to replace the word Hamd. I had to use two words. I had to use gratitude and I had  to use praise . But how many words did Allah use? One! So here we are learning about a complication that occurs when we start translating the Quran. Allah uses one word, but to get the idea across we need to use a couple of words . But what if Allah himself used both words . What if Allah said  المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین . Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah . If Allah had done that would it have been the same? Actually NO! It would not have been the same because of a beautiful principle of the Arabic language . And it is actually a principle of all languages . They say in Arabic:
خیر الکلام ما قل و دل
which means.  the best kinds of speech is that . which uses very few words, but still gets the point across completely . When you use fewer words and get your point across .  that is eloquence . Now some of us MashaAllah have friends that talk to us for 30 minutes . But they still haven't made a point yet .  They say a lot . But they don't actually say anything . And you're hoping they still get to the point. hopefully before Christmas . Some people use too many words to even describe the simplest of things . The best kind of speech.  is one that is brief . that's easier on the tongue . that gets the point across . So alhamd, from an eloquence standpoint, is better than saying المدح و الشکر للہ

Another reason for not saying.المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین . is that in classical Arabic. when you put the word AND  in between two things. which is the letter و. it separates both words even in meaning. When I say  المدح و الشکر للہ. linguistically what I'm saying. is that praise belongs to Allah for some things. and gratitude belongs to Allah for other things. They're not always combined. Because the words aren't combined. This is a cool feature of Arabic language. You don't say what you don't mean. So if we use the two words gratitude and praise and combined them with an AND. in classical Arabic that means. that sometimes I am in the mood to praise him. but not thank them . And then there are other times when I'm in the mood to thank him. but not praise him. But when Allah says AlHamdulillah. that means for every act he does. for every blessing he gives. genuine praise. and unconditional gratitude is for Allah. BOTH at the same time. You don't get to pick and choose which one.

So now if you own a nice car. and you say AlHamdulillah. What have you just done?.  You genuinely praised Allah for giving human beings the ability to create cars. to design cars. manufacture it. AND you thank Allah for letting you own one. So you are praising and thanking Allah both at the same time. Thats all captured in this beautiful word. HAMD.  And this is why. AlHamdulillah  is the attitude of a true Muslim. Because AlHamdulillah is optimistic in nature.  You know sometimes you're going through a difficult time. and somebody comes and asks you. How are you doing and you just say. Oh you know. life sucks. but Alhamdulillah. You're not really praising him or thanking him when you say it that way. AlHamdulillah  is not something we just say. or throw around. It's a reminder for an attitude!. Allah is not interested in what comes out of our tongues. He's more interested in what comes out of our tongues.  that is also connected to our hearts. So we have to mean what we say. when we say AlHamdulillah.

If I'm going through a difficult time. someone asks me. How is it going?. AlHamdulillah!!. I'm grateful to Allah because whatever I'm going through. because it could always have been worse. Someone right now in the world is going through a much harsher version of what I'm going through. I'm grateful to Allah that he is linient with me. and AlHamdulillah. I praise him. because it is only He who can and will get me out of my situation. So a sincere AlHamdulillah. is an optimistic attitude towards Allah. This may seem a bit contradictory right now. but InshaAllah it will become a lot more clear when we talk about trials and tribulations. whether they are a curse or a blessing.

Now let's look at this phrase. الحمد للہ. grammatically. In the arabic language you can use nouns and you can use verbs. Between nouns and verbs. which has tenses? You know present tense, future tense, past tense?. Verbs have a tense. Nouns do not have a tense. There's no past tense noun or present tense noun or future tense noun. right?. Now when I say. I praise Allah. Did I use a noun or a verb?. I used a verb. What tenses is it?.  It's the present tense. 
But when I say praise belongs to Allah. Is the word praise a noun or a verb?.  It is now a noun. Allah could have used a verb. He could've said.  احمدُ اللہ. I praise Allah. He could've said نحمد اللہ .  WE praise Allah. But Allah did not use a verb. He used a noun. Why?. Now here is what makes this so beautiful. When I use a verb. obviously there is going to be a tense associated with it. and when I use a present tense to say. I praise Allah. then I am only talking about the present. I said nothing about the past. and I said nothing about the future. If I use the past tense. then I am not guaranteeing anything about the future or the present. Because a tense has to be one or the other. A verb is limited. It is temporary. But Allah used a noun. And nouns are what?.  They are permanent. Allah's genuine praise and unconditional gratitude. is described with permanence. You know what that means?. It means I may be praising Allah now. but the praise of Allah has always been there. And I am not going to be here in this world forever. but the praise and gratitude of Allah will always be there forever. His praise and gratitude are not dependent on me. A huge reality within Alhamdulillah. is that the praise and gratitude of Allah is permanent. and it is not dependent on me. it's not because of me!.
See when we use the verb. somebody needs to DO the verb. It's called the subject. or the فاعل  in Arabic. There has to be a doer. You cant just go into a conversation and say. Failed the test!. Who failed the test?. You cant just say. Disappeared!. What disappeared?.  Oh my book disappeared. You see?. When you use a verb you need somebody to do it. You need a subject. You cannot just have a verb all by itself. It doesn't make sense. It creates confusion. But a noun doesn't need someone to do it. A noun does not need a subject. A noun is independent by itself. An apple is an apple. it can exist all by itself. independent of any doer. So when Allah used the word AlHamd. He made it a noun. he made it independent. He doesn't need anyone to do the actual praise. and he doesn't need anyone to be grateful. Had he used a verb. that would have meant. that he needed someone to praise him. and he needed someone to be grateful to him.
Even if Allah said everything and everyone praises and is grateful to Allah. that too would have been limited. Why?. Because everything and everyone implies everyone and everything that exists NOW. in the present. It excludes everything and everyone in the past or the future. And that is why Allah used a noun for his praise and gratitude. He used the word Hamd as a noun. so that it is not confined in time and space. Because Allah does not need his creation to praise him and be grateful to Him. Even if there was not a single creation in this world. the Hamd of Allah would always still be there. his praise and gratitude does not require a doer. SubhanAllah!. All of this captured in just one word.

Now what if Allah said. أِحمد اللہ رب العلمین. What if he used a command. Praise Allah! The master of Alameen. Wouldn't that have been better?. I mean after all he is master. so a command could make sense. So why didn't he make it a command. I'll give you an example to help you understand. I tell my daughter Erum to bring me a glass of water. I say. Hey Erum! bring me a glass of water!.  I'm giving her a command. Once she hears me. she has two possible choices. She can either bring me the glass of water. OR. she can bring me the glass of water. Hahaha. Those are the only two clear choices as far as she's concerned.
Now if Allah said to praise him as a command. What are the two things that could happen?.  Some would praise him. Some would obey his command. And then there would be others who would disobey him. When you tell someone to do something. the ball is in their court . It depends on them . Maybe they'll choose to do it . Maybe they won't. Allah did not talk about praise and gratitude in a way that depends on us. He did not put the ball in our court. He said whether you do it or not. Whether you are grateful to me or not. Whether you praise me are not . My praise and gratitude is always still there. My Hamd is still there. It has been there forever. and it WILL be there forever. Human beings will come and go. nations will come and go. Generations will come and go. THIS WORLD will come and go. But the Hamd of Allah will always be there. It is a matter of fact . SubhanAllah!

Now what if Allah said. انَّا الحمد للہ رب العلمین. Certainly. For sure. No doubt about it. ABSOLUTELY. Hamd is for Allah. Now what sounds more powerful?. Is All praise and gratitude belongs to Allah more powerful. Or is it saying. Definitely. Certainly. Absolutely Hamd is for Allah. Obviously the latter one?. So how come Allah didn't say.انَّا الحمد للہ رب العلمین. A Khateeb uses it all the time. I say it in the beginning of sessions all the time to glorify Allah.
انا الحمد للہ نحمدہ و نستعینہ و نستغفر بہ ن. . So how come Allah didn't say it?
If you remember our sessions on the miracle of Quran. on the topic of conversation. I told you there are two kinds of communications. A communication can either be informative or it can emotional. جملۃ انشائیۃ  and جملۃ خبریۃ . Either you have speech that is expressing your feelings and emotions. or you have speech that is communicating information. These are the two kinds of speech that human beings are capable of. That's it. Let's look at an example. Right now. when I'm teaching you about Hamd. am I delivering information. or am I expressing my emotions?. I am giving you information. This is informative speech. But when I'm talking to my friend. And I'm telling my friend how I feel about someone or something. what kind of communication is that?. That is an emotional conversation. So those are the only two types of speech we as human beings are capable of.
